## Lessons Learned (WO-0070 — g3-parallel-merge)

**Features**: P3-W9-F07 (G3 (Knowledge) parallel query merging by entity with temporal priority)
**Rejections**: 0 (verifier-green on first attempt; verdict PASS at HEAD `1e0f297`)
**Critic blockers**: none — two warnings, both acknowledged + justified deviations that **strengthen** the test rather than weaken it: (1) SA1 upper-bound tightened from scope_in #9 literal `< 700 ms` to `< 500 ms` because a sequential 3×200 ms = ~603 ms slips through `< 700` and would have made the M1 mutation contract toothless; (2) `#[allow(dead_code)]` on private `join_all_g3` helper so the M1 in-place mutation (replace parallel fan-out with sequential `.await` loop) compiles cleanly under crate-level `#![deny(warnings)]` instead of surfacing as a build error
**ADRs raised**: none
**Coverage**: `ucil-daemon` 89.22% line (env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER; floor 80%); new file `g3.rs` ~720 LOC ships with 31 SA-numbered assertions across 8 sub-checks

### What worked

- **Pre-baked M1/M2/M3 mutation contract in the RFR (5th consecutive WO).** Pre-mutation md5 snapshot (`69356f91cb321fe9f63903187a9c410c`) shipped with the RFR. Each row gives file/line/patch/expected-panic/restore command. Verifier applied all three in-place via `Edit` (no `git stash`), observed SA1/SA2/SA3 panics with verbatim `(SAn) <semantic name>; left: ..., right: ...` bodies, restored via `git checkout -- crates/ucil-daemon/src/g3.rs`, confirmed md5 match. Pattern is now stable across WO-0066, WO-0067, WO-0068, WO-0069, WO-0070.
- **Frozen test at module root (DEC-0007) applied first try.** `pub async fn test_g3_parallel_merge` lives at `executor.rs:3167` (NOT under `mod tests { ... }`); substring selector `executor::test_g3_parallel_merge` resolves cleanly. WO-0068 lessons §"For planner: module-root placement" successfully consumed by both planner and executor — no mid-WO refactor commit needed (compare WO-0068's commit `07436d5f` hoist-out-of-mod-tests).
- **Spirit-over-literal SA1 tightening (commit `cf24e87`).** Scope_in #9 prescribed `wall_elapsed_ms in [180, 700)` but with 3 sources × 200 ms sleeps the serial total is ~603 ms — slipping through `< 700`. Executor tightened the upper bound to `< 500 ms`, fully disclosed in commit body + RFR's "Disclosed deviations" §3. This is a stronger assertion than spec, and made the M1 mutation contract load-bearing. Cite WO-0068 lessons-learned For executor #4: when the literal scope_in directive sabotages the spec's stated intent ("parallelism confirmed via dual-bound"), follow the spirit and document.
- **Per-source deadline as UNCONDITIONAL `const` (4500 ms), NOT `min`'d with master_deadline.** Same shape as WO-0068's `cross_group::CROSS_GROUP_PER_GROUP_DEADLINE`. Avoids the deadline-collapse race where `tokio::time::Timeout::poll` (polls inner-first) lets per-group win on tight masters and SA-style "master deadline trips" tests fail non-deterministically. WO-0068 lessons §"For executor: per-group `tokio::time::timeout` deadline MUST be strictly larger than tight master deadlines" successfully carried.
- **Atomic M1 mutation contract via `#[allow(dead_code)]` on private helper.** The M1 mutation pattern (replace parallel fan-out with sequential `.await` loop) orphans `join_all_g3`. Without the allow, `#![deny(warnings)]` (lib.rs:152) converts the dead-code warning into a compile error — the verifier observes a build failure instead of the SA1 panic. Pre-emptively annotating the helper with `#[allow(dead_code)]` + a rustdoc citation of the M1 contract keeps the mutation atomic and one-step. Disclosed in commit `cf24e87` and RFR §4.
- **DEC-0008 §4 dependency-inversion seam pattern (UCIL-owned `G3Source` trait) avoids the `ucil-core` → `ucil-daemon` cycle.** Real `G3Source` impls (`CodebaseMemoryG3Source`, `Mem0G3Source`) are deferred to follow-up WOs paired with the F05/F06 plugin-runtime wiring. The trait + orchestration shell + entity-keyed merger ships standalone in `crates/ucil-daemon/src/g3.rs`. Same shape as `G1Source` (WO-0047), `GroupExecutor` (WO-0068).
- **§15.2 tracing on the orchestrator.** `#[tracing::instrument(name = "ucil.group.knowledge", ...)]` on `execute_g3` per master-plan §15.2. WO-0067 lessons §"Pure-deterministic modules: §15.2 tracing does NOT apply" applied in reverse — this IS async/IO orchestration so tracing applies. Critic check confirmed.
- **Module-coherence per DEC-0005 for the NEW `g3.rs` file (~720 LOC in one feat commit).** Splitting helper-by-helper would have produced stub-shaped intermediate states AND broken the M1/M2/M3 mutation-restoration contract — all three mutations target sites inside the same file. Critic precedent cited from WO-0067 ceqp.rs (548 LOC), WO-0068 cross_group.rs (788 LOC).
- **Word-ban scrub coverage of production-side files only.** AC16 grep `mock|fake|stub` on `g3.rs` + verify script returned zero matches. Test-side `TestG3Source` impl in `executor.rs:3194-3276` is exempt under WO-0048 line 363 + WO-0068 lessons §"Test helpers under #[cfg(test)] exempt" carve-out (DEC-0008 §4 dependency-inversion seam, NOT external-system mocks).

### What to carry forward

**For planner**:
- **Compute parallelism dual-bound upper limits as `max_per_source_sleep_ms * (N_sources / 2)` (or tighter) so the bound is load-bearing.** WO-0070 scope_in #9 prescribed `wall_elapsed_ms in [180, 700)` but with 3 sources × 200 ms the sequential total is 603 ms, slipping through `< 700`. Executor tightened to `< 500` to make the M1 mutation contract bite. Future WOs prescribing parallelism dual-bound discipline should compute the upper bound mathematically from the per-source sleep × source count, NOT pick a round-number margin. Pure planner-side hygiene; no UCIL source impact.
- **Pre-emptively place `#[allow(dead_code)]` on the parallel-join helper when the M1 mutation pattern (replace fan-out with sequential `.await` loop) is prescribed.** The mutation always orphans the `join_all_*` helper, and `#![deny(warnings)]` converts dead-code into a build error. Either (a) pre-emptively annotate the helper in `scope_in` (e.g., "the helper MUST carry `#[allow(dead_code)]` with a rustdoc citing the M1 contract"), OR (b) specify the mutation must also comment-out the helper. WO-0070 picked (a) — document this in the mutation-contract pre-baking template.
- **F07 was the consumer WO that introduced the G3 group runtime; F08+ (`tools/list`-driven group dispatch wiring + classify-then-dispatch routing) are now dependency-unblocked.** Per WO-0069 §"For planner: F07 dependency-unblocked", the next planner pass should bundle the daemon-side wiring of `crates/ucil-daemon/src/server.rs` or `lifecycle.rs` to route incoming MCP queries through `classify_query` (F01, WO-0067) before group dispatch — same WO can also bundle the deferred `crates/ucil-core/src/lib.rs` re-exports of `classify_query` + `parse_reason` (WO-0067) and `cross_group::*` consumer wiring (WO-0068).
- **AC25 ("no merge commits introduced on feat") needs to tolerate a 1-commit divergence when the gate-side critic agent commits its report to main between executor RFR push and verifier startup.** WO-0070's verifier observed `git log feat..main = 1` — the diverging commit was `733c593 chore(critic): WO-0070 critic report`, an administrative critic-report on main. Spirit of "no merge commits accidentally introduced on feat" is intact (the feat branch carries 6 linear commits, zero merge commits). Future WOs should reword AC25 as "feat branch carries zero merge commits" (using `git log feat ^main --merges` returning empty) rather than the current "feat..main = 0" form which produces a workflow-timing false-flag.
- **Standing coverage workaround now 26 WOs deep (WO-0058..WO-0070).** Continue citing scope_out + AC23 standing protocol until a dedicated harness-improvement WO replaces `coverage-gate.sh` to use `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER`. Same Bucket B / Bucket D triage status as WO-0067/WO-0068/WO-0069.
- **AC36/AC37 phase-1/phase-2 effectiveness-gate flake now five WOs deep** (WO-0067, WO-0068, WO-0069, WO-0070 all disclosed-deviated this step). Three pre-existing flake escalations carry as standing scope_out items: `20260507T0357Z-effectiveness-nav-rust-symbol-rs-line-flake.md`, `20260507T1629Z-effectiveness-refactor-rename-python-fixture-missing-symbol.md`, `20260507T1930Z-effectiveness-nav-rust-symbol-doctest-caller-flake.md`. Awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO.

**For executor**:
- **When scope_in prescribes a parallelism dual-bound upper limit that does not catch sequential execution, tighten the bound and disclose the deviation.** WO-0070 commit `cf24e87` tightened SA1 from `< 700 ms` to `< 500 ms` so 3×200 ms = 603 ms sequential trips the assertion. Cite WO-0068 For executor #4 (spirit-over-literal) precedent in the commit body, document in the RFR's "Disclosed deviations" section, and note the M1 mutation contract relies on the tightened bound. Future executors confronting the same shape should follow this pattern.
- **For the M1 fan-out → sequential `.await` mutation pattern, pre-emptively annotate the parallel-join helper with `#[allow(dead_code)]` + a rustdoc citing the M1 contract** so the mutation compiles cleanly under `#![deny(warnings)]` and produces the SA panic instead of a build error. WO-0070's `join_all_g3` (g3.rs:331-378) is the template. Cite the mutation contract in the rustdoc explicitly.
- **Bundle the NEW source file + Cargo.toml dep changes (if any) + `lib.rs` mod decl + `lib.rs` re-export block in ONE cohesive feat commit per DEC-0005 module-coherence**, even if it crosses 700 LOC. WO-0070's commit `4a63eae` (717 insertions on g3.rs + lib.rs) is the template — same as WO-0068's cross_group.rs (788 LOC) and WO-0067's ceqp.rs (548 LOC). Splitting helper-by-helper produces stub-shaped intermediate states AND breaks the mutation-restoration contract. Cite DEC-0005 + WO-0067/0068 precedent in the commit body.
- **For module-root frozen tests in `executor.rs`**, the test should be `#[cfg(test)] #[tokio::test(flavor = "multi_thread", worker_threads = 4)] pub async fn test_*` at module root. Multi-thread flavor is required for parallelism SA1 to be observable (single-thread serializes futures). WO-0070's `test_g3_parallel_merge` confirms this pattern works with the substring selector resolving cleanly.

**For verifier**:
- **The M1 fan-out → sequential `.await` mutation requires multi-line `Edit` of the parallel-fan-out block** (`g3.rs:473-485` for WO-0070). Snap md5 BEFORE editing (`md5sum crates/ucil-daemon/src/g3.rs`), apply the `Edit`, run targeted `cargo test -p ucil-daemon executor::test_g3_parallel_merge`, observe `(SA1) parallel wall < 500 ms; left: 603, right: 500` panic, restore via `git checkout -- crates/ucil-daemon/src/g3.rs`, confirm md5 matches the WO-pre-baked `69356f91cb321fe9f63903187a9c410c`. Pattern is now stable across WO-0066, WO-0067, WO-0068, WO-0069, WO-0070.
- **`scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug surfaced AGAIN on WO-0070.** Symptom: false-positive merge conflict on `ucil-build/verification-reports/coverage-ucil-daemon.md` from a stale stash entry. Workaround: `git checkout HEAD -- ucil-build/verification-reports/coverage-ucil-daemon.md`. The M1/M2/M3 in-place mutation contract from the RFR is the authoritative anti-laziness layer — reality-check.sh is informational. Bucket B candidate for triage; carries from WO-0067, WO-0068, WO-0069.
- **AC25 1-commit divergence between feat and main caused by gate-side critic-report commit on main is a workflow-timing artifact, NOT a defect.** The critic agent commits its report to main between the executor's RFR push and the verifier's startup. Confirm via `git log feat ^main --merges` returning empty + the feat branch carrying linear commits since branch point. Resolve via `--ff-only` after the critic report is cherry-picked into the feat branch, or via fast-forward-after-rebase. WO-0070's verification-report row #25 is the template for this disclosed observation.

**Test-type effectiveness (which acceptance_tests caught bugs vs. were ceremonial)**:
- All three mutations (M1 sequential `.await`, M2 inverted temporal in conflict-cluster, M3 inverted confidence in agreement-cluster) detected on first run by the frozen-test-at-module-root selector. SA1..SA8 sub-assertions correctly localised the failures. Zero ceremonial assertions — every SA mapped to a load-bearing semantic check (parallelism wall-time, temporal-priority on conflict, confidence-priority on agreement, entity-union on disjoint queries, partial-error tolerance, partial-timeout tolerance, master-deadline trip, empty-source neutrality).
- The dual-bound parallelism canary (SA1: `wall_elapsed_ms in [180, 500)`) is a strong regression detector — any drift back to sequential execution surfaces immediately as `left: 603, right: 500`. Carry to any future fan-out orchestration tests with N×T ms sleepers (compute upper bound as `T * (N / 2)` or tighter, NOT a round number).
- The temporal-priority + confidence-priority cluster mutations (M2/M3 swap of `>` ↔ `<`) detected via SA-tagged panics with full diagnostic content (`left: "uses bcrypt", right: "uses argon2"` and `left: 0.7, right: 0.9`). The panic body itself doubles as a useful debugging dump of the cluster-merger's tie-break ladder.

### Technical debt incurred

- **None new.** Pre-existing follow-ups carry forward unchanged:
  1. `scripts/verify/coverage-gate.sh` harness improvement to use `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER` (now 26 WOs deep — Bucket B / Bucket D triage candidate).
  2. `scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug (carries from WO-0067/WO-0068/WO-0069; surfaced on WO-0070's verifier session).
  3. Effectiveness-gate.sh claude-p sub-session timeout flake (3 open escalations) — pre-existing standing scope_out, awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO.
  4. AC25 "no merge commits introduced on feat" wording is misleading when gate-side critic agent commits to main during the executor→verifier handoff window — recommend rewording to `git log feat ^main --merges` returning empty.
- **Net-new planner observations from this WO** (NOT debt; planner-side hygiene for future WOs to absorb):
  - Future WOs prescribing parallelism dual-bound discipline must compute the upper bound from `max_per_source_sleep_ms * (N_sources / 2)` (or tighter) — round-number margins (e.g., `< 700` for 3×200 ms) are NOT load-bearing.
  - Future WOs prescribing the M1 fan-out → sequential `.await` mutation pattern must pre-emptively place `#[allow(dead_code)]` on the parallel-join helper in `scope_in` (with a rustdoc citing the M1 contract) — otherwise the mutation surfaces as a compile error under `#![deny(warnings)]` instead of the SA panic.
- WO-0070 inherits but does NOT advance debt items 1, 2, 3; debt item 4 is net-new from this WO. The two net-new planner observations are documented above for the next planner pass to absorb without becoming a debt entry.

## Lessons Learned (WO-0072 — codegraphcontext-plugin-manifest)

**Features**: P3-W9-F08 (CodeGraphContext G4 Architecture plugin manifest — establishes `architecture.*` capability namespace)
**Rejections**: 0 in this WO (verifier-green on first attempt; verdict PASS at HEAD `a7da4341`). F08 attempts pre-flip = 2 (this was the 3rd-and-last attempt before escalation trigger #1; prior attempts failed on F10/graphiti bundling and forbidden_paths/scope-creep, NOT on the F08 surface itself).
**Critic blockers**: none — four soft warnings (1: cosmetic `wo-0071` carryover strings inside the rewritten verify script, non-functional naming carryover; 2: historical WO-0071 references inside test rustdoc — intentional provenance documentation; 3: M3 patch substitution from `--with falkordblite` removal to `mcp → mcpz` typo — empirically grounded planner-spec correction disclosed in RFR §1; 4: two commits exceeding 50-LOC soft target accepted under DEC-0005 module-coherence carve-out cited in scope_in #12)
**ADRs raised**: none new — DEC-0019 (defer P3-W9-F10 graphiti to Phase 7 hardening) was authored prior to this WO and is referenced as the immutable §4 disposition that drives the WO's solo-F08 scope
**Coverage**: `ucil-daemon` 87.88% line (floor 85%); WO is purely additive on tests + manifests + scripts — pre-WO baseline preserved (no `crates/ucil-daemon/src/**` source changes per scope_in #2 + DEC-0019 §1.a)

### What worked

- **Cherry-pick re-packaging mechanic for "split-the-WO" recovery from a multi-feature blocked WO.** WO-0071 bundled F08 (codegraphcontext, clean) + F10 (graphiti, blocked on tolerant-handshake daemon-source change) and was rejected by the critic on the F10 surface. The RCF (`ucil-build/verification-reports/root-cause-WO-0071.md`) recommended split-the-WO. WO-0072 cherry-picked exactly four clean F08 commits (`1d52a3f`, `39850a1`, `b23bdfe`, partial `e5f10bb`) from `feat/WO-0071`, EXCLUDING `9953a0f` (DEC-0019 spurious-frame drain — deferred) and the unwritten DEC-0019-attempt-2 ADR + `12a705d` (the prior RFR). The substantive F08 work was preserved byte-identical; only one commit (the F08-slice of `e5f10bb`) needed a fresh SHA because the cherry-pick was partial (graphiti+install-graphiti+P3-W9-F10.sh+g3-graphiti-test dropped). This is the canonical pattern for recovering a feature trapped inside a multi-feature failed WO without re-implementing the substantive work.
- **Trailer-carryover acceptance for cherry-picked commits per scope_in #3.** Three of the four cherry-picked commits retain their `Work-order: WO-0071` trailer; the partial-cherry-pick commit (`a45ccbe`) was rewritten to `Work-order: WO-0072`. Critic precedent at WO-0067 (substantive provenance preserved across WOs) accepts the carryover. This avoids the noise of `git commit --amend`-ing four commits pre-push solely to flip a trailer string when the substantive lineage is documented in the RFR's Provenance table.
- **Operator-state-aware M3 mutation substitution (RFR Disclosed Deviations §1).** The planner-prescribed M3 (`remove --with falkordblite from transport.args`) did not flip the test on operator machines that have ever run `install-codegraphcontext-mcp.sh`. Reason: the upstream server creates `~/.codegraphcontext/.env` on first invocation and configures `database=falkordb` therein; subsequent runs use that config and start cleanly without `--with falkordblite`, emitting a normal `tools/list` reply. The executor empirically discovered this, substituted M3 to `mcp → mcpz` (typo on the stdio-server subcommand), confirmed the substitute flips PASS→FAIL with a substantively distinct failure mode (`StdioTransport(Os { kind: BrokenPipe })`) from M1 (pre-spawn ENOENT) and M2 (post-handshake assertion panic). Critic + verifier independently accepted the substitution. WO-0068 lessons §planner "Empirical reality wins; document and move on" applied verbatim.
- **Pre-baked M1/M2/M3 mutation contract in the RFR (6th consecutive WO).** Pre-mutation md5 snapshots (`7e04dcfd...` plugin.toml, `a8fa5a7d...` g4 test) shipped with the RFR. Verifier applied all three in-place via `Edit`, confirmed substantive distinct failure modes via verbatim observed-panic strings, restored via `git checkout --`, confirmed md5 match. Pattern is now stable across WO-0066 → WO-0072.
- **Frozen-test module-root placement (DEC-0007 + WO-0068 §planner) applied first try via cherry-pick provenance.** The cherry-picked test in `crates/ucil-daemon/tests/g4_plugin_manifests.rs` already lived inside `mod g4_plugin_manifests { ... }` at module root (line 46) with a single `#[tokio::test] async fn codegraphcontext_manifest_health_check` (line 91). Substring selector `g4_plugin_manifests::codegraphcontext_manifest_health_check` resolves cleanly. No mid-WO refactor needed — the WO-0068 lesson successfully propagated to the WO-0071 executor and survived the cherry-pick.
- **Establishment of the `architecture.*` capability namespace.** F08 is the first G4 (Architecture) plugin landing; capabilities provide `["architecture.dependency_graph", "architecture.blast_radius"]`. Continues the namespace convention from G2 (`search.*` probe, `navigate.*` scip), G3 (`knowledge.*` codebase-memory + mem0). Subsequent G4 plugins (gitnexus, dep-cruiser, axon, deptry, nx, bazel per master-plan §14.1 line 1676-1677) should extend this namespace.
- **Separate-file-per-group integration test isolation per WO-0069 §executor.** New file `tests/g4_plugin_manifests.rs` is independent of `tests/plugin_manifests.rs` (WO-0044 G2 regression guard) and `tests/g3_plugin_manifests.rs` (WO-0069 G3 regression guard). Both prior files were explicitly listed in `forbidden_paths` and remained untouched. The pattern (one tests file per group) is now proven across G2/G3/G4 and should continue for G1, G5..G8.
- **No mocks of MCP server / JSON-RPC dialogue / `tokio::process::Command`.** Real `uvx --with falkordblite codegraphcontext@0.4.7 mcp start` subprocess via `PluginManager::health_check_with_timeout`; live `tools/list` JSON-RPC handshake returning 25 tools. Critic check 2 verified the rustdoc declares mocking FORBIDDEN at `tests/g4_plugin_manifests.rs:10`. Meets master-plan §15.4 / CLAUDE.md "no mocks of critical deps" verbatim.

### What to carry forward

**For planner**:
- **The cherry-pick split-the-WO mechanic is now the canonical recovery shape for a multi-feature WO that fails on a subset of features.** When an RCF recommends split-the-WO (`ucil-build/verification-reports/root-cause-WO-NNNN.md`), the next WO scope_in should: (a) name each cherry-pick source SHA explicitly with subject + ordering, (b) name the EXCLUDED SHAs explicitly (with rationale citing the deferral ADR), (c) carve out trailer-carryover acceptance per WO-0067 precedent, (d) require a sanity `git diff main feat -- <forbidden-paths>` audit returning empty post-cherry-pick, (e) require the new RFR to ship a `## Provenance` table with one row per cherry-picked commit (origin SHA → new SHA → subject → trailer). WO-0072 scope_in #1-#3 + #15 + RFR Provenance section is the working template.
- **For external-plugin manifest WOs whose upstream server creates persistent operator state on first run, prescribe BOTH a freshly-cleaned M3 AND a steady-state-aware M3.** WO-0072's `~/.codegraphcontext/.env` operator-state file persisted across the executor's runs and neutralized the planner-prescribed `--with falkordblite` removal. Future planner passes targeting plugins with similar persistent state (e.g., `~/.<tool>/config`, `~/.<tool>/db.sqlite`, `~/.cache/<tool>/`) MUST EITHER (a) prescribe the M3 to mutate something the operator-state file cannot rescue (transport subcommand typo, `tools/list` JSON-RPC method-name typo, etc.), OR (b) prescribe a `rm -rf ~/.<tool>/` pre-mutation step before applying the M3. The substitute-M3 pattern of `mcp → mcpz` (mutate the canonical subcommand to a typo) is general — the upstream server cannot recover from a typo'd subcommand because it never reaches its operator-state config file. Carry this for any future external-MCP-server plugin manifest WOs.
- **F09 (G4 Architecture parallel executor) is now dependency-unblocked.** F08 lands solo per DEC-0019 §4. F10 (graphiti) is deferred to Phase 7. F09 is the next G4-related WO; per scope_out #9 of WO-0072, F09 introduces the G4 group runtime and consumes the F08 manifest + P1-W5-F06 LSP call hierarchy. The next planner pass for G4 should bundle F09 with the daemon-side `G4Source` adapter for CodeGraphContext (via `PluginManager::health_check_with_timeout`-equivalent runtime invocation) and a separate `G4Source` for any LSP-call-hierarchy backing source. Same dependency-inversion seam pattern as `G1Source` (WO-0047) / `G3Source` (WO-0070) per DEC-0008 §4.
- **DEC-0019 §1.a daemon-side spurious-frame drain MUST be re-emitted as a Phase 7 hardening WO.** The original code change (`9953a0f`) modifies `crates/ucil-daemon/src/plugin_manager.rs::send_tools_list` to drain spurious MCP frames before reading the JSON-RPC response — addresses upstream MCP servers that emit non-spec-compliant pre-handshake frames. Phase 7 planner pass should re-emit it with: (a) its own dedicated WO (no feature bundling), (b) sibling ADR justifying tolerant-handshake behaviour, (c) integration test asserting both spec-compliant AND spurious-frame-emitting plugin servers complete the handshake cleanly, (d) verify-script smoke against a deliberately-out-of-spec MCP fixture. Master-plan §17.4 (MCP robustness sweep) is the home for this work.
- **Standing coverage workaround now 28 WOs deep (WO-0058..WO-0072).** Continue citing scope_out + AC23 standing protocol until a dedicated harness-improvement WO replaces `coverage-gate.sh` to use `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER`. Same Bucket B / Bucket D triage status as WO-0067/WO-0068/WO-0069/WO-0070. NOTE: WO-0072's verifier session reported the gate-script measured cleanly without the workaround (`[coverage-gate] PASS — ucil-daemon line=88%`) — the sccache RUSTC_WRAPPER interaction may be intermittent / environment-sensitive. Continue the standing scope_out wording but the harness-improvement urgency is lower than previously assessed.
- **AC30/AC31 phase-1/phase-2 effectiveness-gate flake now six WOs deep** (WO-0067, WO-0068, WO-0069, WO-0070, WO-0072 all carry the standing scope_out). Three pre-existing flake escalations carry: `20260507T0357Z-effectiveness-nav-rust-symbol-rs-line-flake.md`, `20260507T1629Z-effectiveness-refactor-rename-python-fixture-missing-symbol.md`, `20260507T1930Z-effectiveness-nav-rust-symbol-doctest-caller-flake.md`. Awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO.

**For executor**:
- **For cherry-pick-based WOs, run the post-cherry-pick sanity audits BEFORE pushing — `git diff main feat -- <forbidden-paths>` for each entry in `forbidden_paths` MUST return empty.** WO-0072 ran six audits per scope_in #2: daemon source, graphiti manifest, graphiti install/verify scripts, decisions/, plugin_manifests.rs, g3_plugin_manifests.rs — all returned empty. If any audit fails, the cherry-pick must be redone (likely a missed `--strategy=resolve` or accidental include). Cite WO-0072 scope_in #2 as the audit checklist template.
- **When the planner-prescribed M3 fails to flip the test under realistic operator conditions, substitute it with a different mutation that DOES flip the test, document fully in the RFR's "Disclosed Deviations" section, and confirm the substitute hits a distinct failure mode from M1 + M2.** WO-0072 RFR §1 is the template — name the planner's M3 verbatim, explain the empirical observation (`~/.codegraphcontext/.env` neutralizes the patch), name the substitute M3 with rationale (preserves planner intent: structural transport.args poison hitting upstream-server runtime initialization), confirm failure-mode independence (`Spawn` ENOENT vs assertion panic vs `BrokenPipe` mid-handshake — three distinct surfaces), provide verbatim observed-panic strings. Cite WO-0068 §planner "Empirical reality wins" precedent.
- **Cosmetic carryover strings inside cherry-picked or rewritten files are tolerable as long as substantive correctness is unaffected.** WO-0072's rewritten `scripts/verify/P3-W9-F08.sh` retains `wo-0071`-prefixed temp-path strings (`CARGO_LOG="/tmp/wo-0071-f08-cargo.log"`, etc.) that don't impact correctness — the script still operates against the right fixture and asserts the right selectors. Critic flagged as Warning #1 with recommendation "follow-up cosmetic-fix WO". Don't block on cosmetic-only string carryover; document the carryover in the RFR's Provenance section and let triage convert to a Bucket-B/D micro-WO if it ever matters.
- **For external-plugin manifest WOs targeting plugins with persistent operator-state config files, the executor SHOULD verify the planner's M3 holds under steady-state conditions BEFORE writing the RFR.** Specifically: run the install script once (or otherwise let the upstream server create its operator-state file), then test the planner's M3. If the M3 fails to flip, substitute with a state-immune mutation (typo on the canonical transport subcommand, typo on a JSON-RPC method, removal of a manifest field that has no operator-state fallback) and document. Don't ship the RFR with an M3 that the verifier will re-discover doesn't flip.
- **Word-ban scrub MUST cover production-side files (manifest, install script, verify script) but EXEMPT integration-test files under `#[cfg(test)]` / `tests/` whose `//!` rustdoc DECLARES the forbidden patterns are forbidden.** WO-0072's `tests/g4_plugin_manifests.rs:10` contains the substring `Mocking ` only inside a leading `//!` rustdoc declaring "Mocking ... is forbidden." This is a NEGATIVE assertion forbidding mocking, NOT a mock implementation. Carve out per scope_in #11 + WO-0048 line 363 + WO-0069 §executor. The pre-flight grep on production paths returned empty (`! grep -qiE 'mock|fake|stub' plugins/.../plugin.toml scripts/devtools/install-*.sh scripts/verify/P3-W9-F0*.sh` clean).

**For verifier**:
- **For cherry-pick-based WOs, validate the substantive provenance via the RFR's Provenance table — confirm each `Origin SHA` exists at the named branch, the new `<New SHA>` subject matches origin verbatim, and the `Excluded` list is genuinely absent from the feat branch via `git diff main feat -- <excluded-paths>` returning empty.** WO-0072 verifier confirmed all four origins via `git show <SHA>` on `feat/WO-0071` archive, confirmed exclusions via the six `git diff main feat -- ...` audits per scope_in #2. Reject if any origin SHA is missing, mismatched, or the exclusion list shows non-empty diff.
- **When the executor disclosed a substituted M3 (planner-spec correction), independently confirm the substitute flips PASS→FAIL with a substantively distinct failure mode from M1 + M2.** WO-0072 verifier ran the substituted M3 (`mcp → mcpz`) from a clean checkout post-`cargo clean`, observed `StdioTransport(Os { code: 32, kind: BrokenPipe })` panic, restored via `git checkout --`, confirmed md5 match against `7e04dcfd...`. Failure-mode independence verified: M1 = pre-spawn ENOENT (process never starts), M2 = post-handshake assertion panic (process spoke MCP, test rejected the tool list), M3 = mid-handshake transport-level broken-pipe (process started but exited before completing JSON-RPC handshake). Three substantively distinct surfaces — accept the substitution.
- **`scripts/verify/coverage-gate.sh` may produce stale reports across worktree boundaries.** WO-0072 verifier observed `ucil-build/verification-reports/coverage-ucil-daemon.md` was previously stale (FAIL from WO-0070 worktree); regenerated cleanly with the current PASS result. The stale-report carry-over is informational, NOT a blocker — re-run `coverage-gate.sh` from the verifier's clean worktree and accept the regenerated value.
- **`scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug surfaced AGAIN on WO-0072** (`stash@{0}: On feat/WO-0063...` carries from prior session runs). Workaround: the M1/M2/M3 in-place mutation contract from the RFR is the authoritative anti-laziness layer; reality-check.sh is informational. Bucket B candidate for triage; carries from WO-0067, WO-0068, WO-0069, WO-0070.
- **For 3rd-attempt features at attempts=2, the verifier MUST be especially rigorous about not introducing false-flag rejections that would tip into escalation trigger #1 (3-strike feature-rejection halt).** WO-0072 was F08's 3rd attempt; the prior two attempts failed on F10 bundling and forbidden_paths/scope-creep, NOT on the F08 surface itself. The cherry-pick + isolation reduces re-fail risk because the substantive F08 work (manifest TOML + g4 test + verify script) was already verified clean in WO-0071's attempt-2 critic run. The verifier's job is to confirm the cherry-pick is faithful + the mutation contract holds, NOT to invent new acceptance bars. WO-0072 verified PASS on first attempt — the pattern works.

**Test-type effectiveness (which acceptance_tests caught bugs vs. were ceremonial)**:
- All three mutations (M1 codegraphcontext transport.command poison, M2 expected-tool-name regression, M3 substituted: `mcp → mcpz`) detected on first run by the frozen-test module-root selector. M1/M3 panics carry the structured `PluginError::*` chain (Spawn ENOENT for M1, StdioTransport BrokenPipe for M3) — unambiguous detection signals. M2 panic carries the full live 25-tool list as the assertion message (`got: ["add_code_to_graph", "check_job_status", "list_jobs", ...]`) — the panic body itself doubles as a useful diagnostic dump of the upstream MCP server's advertised tool catalog at the pinned version. Any drift in the upstream server's tool list at v0.4.7 would surface here as a side effect.
- The `tools/list` cargo-test path (load-bearing) confirms the manifest spawn + JSON-RPC handshake protocol prefix end-to-end. The verify-script's tool-level dep-graph + analyze smoke against a tmpdir copy of `tests/fixtures/rust-project` confirms the upstream server's actual functional surface (`index_repository` + `analyze_code_relationships` returning structured results: `OK: index=377b analyze=10169b`). Both layers are non-ceremonial — they catch substantively different defect classes (manifest-shape vs upstream-server-functional).
- AC11 (`! grep -qE '"(main|latest|master|head|develop|dev|nightly)"'`) catches the floating-ref class for any pinned-version manifest; not ceremonial — re-running on a hypothetical regression would catch a `version = "main"` slip.
- AC15 (`git diff main HEAD -- crates/ucil-daemon/src/` empty) is ceremonial in this WO (executor cherry-picked specifically to exclude the daemon source change); however, it's load-bearing as a regression detector — if any future executor accidentally re-introduces the deferred `9953a0f` patch, this audit catches it immediately.

### Technical debt incurred

- **None new.** Pre-existing follow-ups carry forward unchanged:
  1. `scripts/verify/coverage-gate.sh` harness improvement to use `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER` (now 28 WOs deep — Bucket B / Bucket D triage candidate). NOTE: WO-0072 reported the gate-script measured cleanly this run; the urgency is lower than previously assessed but the workaround is still standing protocol.
  2. `scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug (carries from WO-0067/0068/0069/0070; surfaced again on WO-0072's verifier session).
  3. Effectiveness-gate.sh claude-p sub-session timeout flake (3 open escalations) — pre-existing standing scope_out, awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO.
  4. AC25 "no merge commits introduced on feat" wording carries from WO-0070 — recommend rewording to `git log feat ^main --merges` returning empty (WO-0072 used the reworded form successfully).
- **Phase-7-deferred work** (NOT debt — explicit ADR'd deferral per DEC-0019):
  - `9953a0f` daemon spurious-frame-drain code change (`crates/ucil-daemon/src/plugin_manager.rs::send_tools_list`) — re-emit as a dedicated Phase 7 hardening WO with sibling ADR + integration test against a deliberately-out-of-spec MCP fixture. Master-plan §17.4 MCP robustness sweep is the home.
  - P3-W9-F10 graphiti plugin manifest — re-emit as a dedicated Phase 7 hardening WO once the daemon-side tolerant-handshake lands. Cherry-pick from `feat/WO-0071-archive` if the archived branch is preserved; otherwise re-implement from scratch per master-plan §13 plugin manifest contract.
- **Net-new planner observations from this WO** (NOT debt; planner-side hygiene for future planner passes to absorb):
  - For external-plugin manifest WOs whose upstream server creates persistent operator-state config files (`~/.<tool>/.env`, `~/.<tool>/config`, `~/.<tool>/db.sqlite`, `~/.cache/<tool>/`), prescribe an M3 mutation that the operator-state file cannot rescue (transport subcommand typo, JSON-RPC method-name typo) — NOT a mutation to a `--with`-style optional dependency that the operator-state config can route around. The `mcp → mcpz` substitution shape is the general template.
  - For "split-the-WO" recovery scenarios where an RCF recommends isolating one feature from a multi-feature failed WO, the canonical scope_in shape is: cherry-pick mechanic + sanity audit + trailer-carryover acceptance + RFR Provenance table. WO-0072 scope_in #1-#3 + #15 + RFR Provenance section is the proven template.
- WO-0072 inherits but does NOT advance debt items 1, 2, 3, 4. The two net-new planner observations are documented above for the next planner pass to absorb without becoming a debt entry.

## Lessons Learned (WO-0073 — g4-architecture-parallel-query)

**Features**: P3-W9-F09 (G4 Architecture parallel-query orchestrator + edge-union/BFS-blast-radius merger)
**Rejections**: 0 (verifier-green on first attempt; verdict PASS at HEAD `daa56cc`; critic verdict CLEAN)
**Critic blockers**: none — one soft warning (subject-line over-run on 4/5 commits, same range as WO-0070 / WO-0067; not blocking, accepted via commit-style.md soft-target wording)
**ADRs raised**: none
**Coverage**: `ucil-daemon` 89.66% line via `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov` (≥80% floor); new file `g4.rs` alone reports 94.39% line coverage

### What worked

- **Direct G3 → G4 template port.** WO-0073 mirrored WO-0070's G3 shape verbatim: `G4Source` trait (DEC-0008 §4 DI seam) ≅ `G3Source`, `execute_g4` (parallel orchestrator with `tokio::time::timeout` + `poll_fn`-based `join_all_g4` helper) ≅ `execute_g3`, `merge_g4_dependency_union` (edge-union + BFS-blast-radius) ≅ `merge_g3_unified`, frozen-test-at-module-root ≅ same. Five lessons-learned items from WO-0070 (`#[allow(dead_code)]` on parallel-join, unconditional-const per-source deadline, multi-thread tokio test flavor, alphabetical pub mod / pub use placement, `git log feat ^main --merges` AC25 wording) were copied into WO-0073 scope_in verbatim and held. Zero re-discovery work.
- **Pre-baked M1/M2/M3 mutation contract with structured patch + selector + restore + expected panic.** Verifier applied each mutation in-place via `Edit` (no `git stash`), observed the SA-tagged panic with verbatim left/right values matching the RFR's expected panic string (M1: `left: 603, right: 500`; M2: `left: 3, right: 2`; M3: `left: 2, right: 1`), restored via `git checkout -- crates/ucil-daemon/src/g4.rs`, confirmed md5sum match against the pre-mutation snapshot (`06d821601b81c12e162aa602d7815085`), then proceeded. The mature pattern.
- **`==` → `!=` 2-character mutation as the canonical M2 inverted-dedup shape.** M2 mutated `ue.edge.source == edge.source` → `ue.edge.source != edge.source` at `g4.rs:737` — single-character flip in an existing `position()` predicate. Cleanest possible mutation patch; the verifier's `Edit` was one rune-pair. Carry this for any future dedup-merge mutation contract: identify the `==` inside the `position()` / `find()` predicate and flip to `!=`.
- **SA1 dual-bound 500 ms ceiling held at 603 ms observed.** The WO-0070 dual-bound formula (`max_per_source_sleep_ms × N_sources / 2 + noise_margin`) computed `200 × 3/2 + 200 = 500` for 3×200 ms sources. Under the M1 sequential-execution mutation, observed wall-time was 603 ms — well within the formula's prediction (3×200 ≈ 600), trapping the mutation cleanly. The "NOT a round 700 ms" lesson is now empirically validated across G3 + G4. Future G-group WOs (G5+) should keep the formula and avoid round numbers.
- **Ground-truth-on-conflict sentinel pattern (reserved enum field + TODO comment + dedicated AC grep) for future-hook deferral.** F09 ships `G4EdgeOrigin::{Inferred, GroundTruth}` enum + a sentinel `TODO(P3-W10-F14 / future)` comment in `merge_g4_dependency_union` documenting the resolution branch's future activation when dependency-cruiser / deptry plugs in. AC30 grep enforces the sentinel's presence. NO test SA exercises the unreachable branch (it would fail-by-construction since only Inferred sources exist in F09). Same pattern as WO-0070's `validity_window` deferral. This is the canonical "ship the data-model field + sentinel + AC grep, defer the load-bearing branch to its dedicated WO" template.
- **Single-feature WO with 5-commit estimate landed at exactly 5 commits.** Commit 1 (`78f813f`, NEW `g4.rs` 898 LOC, DEC-0005 module-coherence carve-out), commit 2 (`e08f8fa`, `pub mod` + `pub use` 3 LOC), commit 3 (`5c5b447`, frozen test 737 LOC at module root, DEC-0007), commit 4 (`5040685`, verify script 117 LOC), commit 5 (`3b548c9`, RFR 197 LOC). Estimate matched reality; no surprise mid-WO commits. The 5-commit shape (NEW module + lib.rs wiring + frozen test + verify script + RFR) is the canonical single-feature G-group runtime WO shape.
- **`#[tracing::instrument(name = "ucil.group.architecture", …)]` decorator placement on `execute_g4`.** Master-plan §15.2 + WO-0067 lesson "tracing applies to async/IO orchestration unlike pure-deterministic ceqp.rs" applied cleanly. The named span (`ucil.group.architecture`) extends the established naming convention from G1 / G3 (`ucil.group.<group_name>`).

### What to carry forward

**For planner**:
- **F11 (incremental computation integration test) is orthogonal to G4 and stays a separate WO.** Per scope_out #7 — Salsa-engine + tree-sitter pipeline surface, NOT the architecture group runtime.
- **The next G4-related WO is the production-wiring WO bundling `CodeGraphContextG4Source` + `LSPCallHierarchyG4Source` impls.** Consumes F08 (CodeGraphContext manifest, WO-0072) + P1-W5-F06 (LSP diagnostics bridge call hierarchy). Same DEC-0008 §4 dependency-inversion seam pattern as the deferred G1 production wiring (TestG1Source → real CodebaseMemoryG1Source / Mem0G1Source) and G3 production wiring. The seam is intentional — F09's TestG4Source impls in `executor.rs` are NOT mocks of any external wire format; they are UCIL-internal trait impls per DEC-0008 §4.
- **P3-W10-F14 (dependency-cruiser plugin manifest) is the load-bearing trigger for the ground-truth-on-conflict resolution branch.** When P3-W10-F14 lands, the `merge_g4_dependency_union` resolver must upgrade `G4EdgeOrigin::GroundTruth` edges over `G4EdgeOrigin::Inferred` edges for the same `(source, target, edge_kind)` tuple. The sentinel `TODO(P3-W10-F14 / future)` at `g4.rs:725-733` names the file/site explicitly. The follow-up WO scope_in should: (a) cite this sentinel verbatim, (b) add a new SA (e.g., SA9) that asserts ground-truth precedence, (c) remove the `TODO` comment in the same commit that activates the branch.
- **The G3 → G4 template port is now a proven recipe — apply the same shape to G5..G8.** When the next G-group runtime WO lands (G5..G8 per master-plan §5.5+), planner should reuse the canonical scope_in shape: NEW `g<N>.rs` (DEC-0005 module-coherence; one cohesive feat commit even at 700-900 LOC), `<G>Source` trait + `<G>Query` + `<G>SourceOutput` + `<G>Outcome` + group-specific result types, `pub async fn execute_g<N>` + `pub fn merge_g<N>_*`, `pub const G<N>_MASTER_DEADLINE` + `pub const G<N>_PER_SOURCE_DEADLINE` (unconditional consts), `#[tracing::instrument(name = "ucil.group.<name>", …)]`, `#[allow(dead_code)]` on the parallel-join helper, frozen test at executor.rs module root with ≥7 SA-numbered assertions, multi-thread tokio test flavor, dual-bound parallelism upper-bound formula (NOT round numbers), alphabetical `pub mod` / `pub use` placement, pre-baked M1/M2/M3 contract with file/line/restore commands, ground-truth/validity-window-style sentinel for any deferred load-bearing branch.
- **Standing coverage workaround now 29 WOs deep (WO-0058..WO-0073).** Continue scope_out + AC23 standing-protocol substantive coverage check until a dedicated harness-improvement WO replaces `coverage-gate.sh` to use `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER`. WO-0072's verifier session reported the gate-script measured cleanly without the workaround; WO-0073 reports the substantive measurement at 89.66% via the workaround. The intermittent sccache RUSTC_WRAPPER interaction continues to track lower urgency than previously assessed — but the standing wording is unchanged.
- **AC30/AC31 phase-1/phase-2 effectiveness-gate flake now seven WOs deep** (WO-0067, WO-0068, WO-0069, WO-0070, WO-0072, WO-0073). Three pre-existing flake escalations carry: `20260507T0357Z-effectiveness-nav-rust-symbol-rs-line-flake.md`, `20260507T1629Z-effectiveness-refactor-rename-python-fixture-missing-symbol.md`, `20260507T1930Z-effectiveness-nav-rust-symbol-doctest-caller-flake.md`. Awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO.
- **Cross-group executor wiring (G4 → `Group::G4` enum dispatch in `cross_group::execute_cross_group`) is a separate follow-up WO.** Per scope_out #3 — `Group::G4` already exists from WO-0068 but the dispatch arm is not yet wired to call `execute_g4`. The follow-up WO is small (single match-arm + dispatch test) and should land after the G4 production-wiring WO so the dispatch arm uses real `G4Source` impls.

**For executor**:
- **DON'T flatten the per-source deadline by min'ing it with `master_deadline`.** WO-0068/0070 lesson held again on G4: the per-source `Duration::from_millis(4_500)` is an UNCONDITIONAL const, NOT `min(G4_PER_SOURCE_DEADLINE, master_deadline)`. The per-source only wins on true global stalls (sleeper > 4.5 s); the master only wins on tight budgets (master < 4.5 s). Document the inversion inline at the deadline-computation site with a citation to WO-0068/0070 lessons-learned.
- **DON'T pick round-number SA1 parallelism ceilings.** Compute the upper bound from `max_per_source_sleep_ms × (N_sources / 2) + noise_margin`. For 3×200 ms sources, `200 × 3/2 + 200 = 500` ms; 700 ms would let serial 3×200=600 ms slip through, NOT trapping the M1 sequential-execution mutation. Verified empirically on G4: M1 produced wall-time 603 ms, well above the 500 ms ceiling.
- **DON'T forget `#[allow(dead_code)]` on the parallel-join helper.** Under `#![deny(warnings)]` (`crates/ucil-daemon/src/lib.rs:152`), the M1 sequential-await mutation orphans the helper and the dead-code warning becomes a compile error, breaking the M1 atomic-step contract. Pre-emptive `#[allow(dead_code)]` on the helper keeps the mutation one-rune-flip-friendly. WO-0070 + WO-0073 both verified.
- **DON'T place frozen tests under `mod tests { ... }`.** DEC-0007 + WO-0068/0070 lesson: the frozen test must live at MODULE ROOT inside `executor.rs`, NOT under `mod tests { ... }`. The substring selector `executor::test_g<N>_<test_name>` MUST resolve cleanly (NOT `executor::tests::test_g<N>_<test_name>`). The verify script's `^[[:space:]]*(pub )?(async )?fn test_<name>\(\)` grep guard enforces this; a regression slips into a `^[[:space:]]*    fn test_<name>\(\)` (4-space indent inside the tests module).
- **DON'T import `regex` for word-ban scrubs or simple sentinel-trigger patterns inside production code.** Use `str::contains` + `str::find` + manual byte-level scan. WO-0067 lesson reaffirmed; `g4.rs` carries zero `regex` dependency despite parsing edge_kind enum patterns.
- **DO declare `#[tokio::test(flavor = "multi_thread", worker_threads = 4)]` on the frozen test.** Single-threaded tokio runtime serializes tasks and trivially defeats the SA1 parallelism assertion (3 sources sleeping 200 ms each would serialize to 600 ms regardless of `join_all_g<N>` correctness). WO-0070 + WO-0073 verified.
- **DO make every `assert!` / `assert_eq!` carry a `(SAn) <semantic name>; left: <X>; right: <Y>` panic body** per DEC-0007. Mutation diagnosis is then trivial — verifier reads the panic line, identifies the SA, restores the file. Eight SA labels (SA1..SA8) for parallelism, edge-union dedup, disjoint-source emission, BFS depth-tracking, multiplicative coupling propagation, partial-Errored resilience, partial-TimedOut resilience, master-deadline-trip — covers the full G4 contract surface.

**For verifier**:
- **For G-group runtime WOs with pre-baked M1/M2/M3 contracts mirroring WO-0070's shape, use the same in-place mutation + restore protocol.** Snapshot md5sum BEFORE first mutation; apply each mutation via `Edit` (NOT `git stash`); run targeted `cargo test -p ucil-daemon executor::test_g<N>_<test_name> --no-fail-fast` selector; observe SA-tagged panic with verbatim left/right values; restore via `git checkout -- crates/ucil-daemon/src/g<N>.rs`; confirm md5sum match; proceed to next mutation. Independence between mutations is guaranteed by the restore-and-confirm-md5 step.
- **The `(SAn) <semantic_name>; left: <X>; right: <Y>` panic body format makes verifier mutation-confirmation trivial.** WO-0073's M1 panic was `(SA1) parallel wall < 500 ms; left: 603, right: 500` — verifier reads the line, confirms SA1 matches the expected M1 outcome, no grep/diff required. Reject any WO whose mutations don't carry this format.
- **Substantive coverage measurement: `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov --package <crate> --summary-only --json | jq '.data[0].totals.lines.percent'` is the AC23 standing protocol.** The gate-script `coverage-gate.sh` may produce stale or near-zero values intermittently due to sccache RUSTC_WRAPPER interaction. WO-0073 reported 89.66% via the workaround; gate-script has reported clean values in some recent runs (WO-0072 verifier). Use the workaround value as authoritative.
- **`scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug carries from WO-0067/0068/0069/0070/0072 to WO-0073.** Workaround unchanged: the M1/M2/M3 in-place mutation contract from the RFR is the authoritative anti-laziness layer; reality-check.sh is informational only. Bucket B candidate for triage. Do NOT block on reality-check.sh's spurious merge-conflict reports in unrelated `verification-reports/coverage-*.md` files.
- **For mirror-shaped WOs (G3 → G4, and any future G5+), confirm the planner-claimed mirroring is faithful by spot-checking the orchestrator's `tokio::time::timeout` placement, the `poll_fn`-based `join_all_g<N>` helper shape, the unconditional-const per-source deadline, the `#[allow(dead_code)]` on the helper, and the alphabetical `pub mod` / `pub use` placement.** All five hold for WO-0073 G4. If any hint slips, the M1 mutation may not compile cleanly under `#![deny(warnings)]`, breaking the verifier's atomic-step contract.

**Test-type effectiveness (which acceptance_tests caught bugs vs. were ceremonial)**:
- **All 8 SA assertions (SA1..SA8) are non-ceremonial.** Each covers a distinct semantic contract: SA1 parallelism, SA2 edge-union dedup, SA3 disjoint-source-edge merge, SA4 BFS depth-tracking, SA5 multiplicative coupling propagation, SA6 partial-Errored resilience, SA7 partial-TimedOut resilience, SA8 master-deadline-trip. The pre-baked M1/M2/M3 mutations target SA1/SA2/SA4 specifically and all flipped on first run. SA3/SA5/SA6/SA7/SA8 are not exercised by the mutation contract but cover load-bearing semantics that any future regression in `merge_g4_dependency_union` (e.g., changing the multiplicative coupling propagation to additive) or `execute_g4` (e.g., dropping the per-source timeout wrapper, or treating Errored sources as Available) would surface.
- **The DEC-0007 SA-numbered panic-body format pays compounding dividends.** Verifier mutation-confirmation is mechanical (no grep, no diff, just read the panic line) → 8/8 SAs ship with this format → mutation diagnosis is instant.
- **AC30 (`TODO(P3-W10-F14 / future)` ground-truth sentinel grep) is non-ceremonial as a regression detector.** When P3-W10-F14 (dependency-cruiser) lands and activates the branch, the executor must remove the TODO comment in the same commit. The grep would catch a partial implementation that activates the branch but forgets to remove the sentinel.
- **AC15 (`#[tracing::instrument]` grep on g4.rs) is load-bearing for master-plan §15.2 compliance.** Removing the decorator silently would break observability for the architecture group's spans (`ucil.group.architecture`) but compile cleanly. The grep catches this.

  2. `scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug (carries from WO-0067/0068/0069/0070/0072).
