## Lessons Learned (WO-0074 — context7-and-repomix-plugin-manifests)

**Features**: P3-W10-F02 (Context7 G5 plugin manifest), P3-W10-F03 (Repomix G5 plugin manifest)
**Rejections**: 0 (verifier-green on first attempt; verdict PASS at HEAD `9f900820`; critic verdict CLEAN with 4 advisory warnings, none blocking)
**Critic blockers**: none — 4 soft warnings (F03 reduction-ratio measurement scope, env-gated runtime skip paths, F03 verify script LOC without explicit DEC-0005 cite, F02 bash sleep-based JSON-RPC timing)
**ADRs raised**: none
**Coverage**: `ucil-daemon` 89.6527% line via `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov --package ucil-daemon --tests --summary-only --json` (≥85% floor); WO is purely additive on tests + manifests + scripts (no `crates/ucil-daemon/src/**` source changes), pre-WO baseline preserved by construction.

### What worked

- **Direct G3 → G5 paired-manifest template port via WO-0069 shape parent.** WO-0074 mirrored WO-0069's G3 (`codebase-memory + mem0`) paired-manifest precedent verbatim, retargeted from Knowledge to Context group. Two stdio MCP servers (Context7 v2.2.4 + Repomix v1.14.0) get hand-authored TOML manifests under a new `plugins/context/<name>/plugin.toml` directory; two devtools install scripts; one new `crates/ucil-daemon/tests/g5_plugin_manifests.rs` integration test file (peer of `g3_plugin_manifests.rs` / `g4_plugin_manifests.rs`); two replacement verify scripts. The G3 → G4 (WO-0073) → G5 (WO-0074) recipe is now triple-verified — applies to G6..G8 forward.
- **Pre-baked M1/M2 mutation contract with restore-and-md5-confirm.** Both M1 (`transport.command = "npx"` → `"/__ucil_test_nonexistent_M1__"`) and M2 (`"resolve-library-id"` / `"pack_codebase"` → `"NON_EXISTENT_TOOL_M2"`) applied independently per feature, produced expected ENOENT-class spawn errors (M1) and SA-tagged panics with full live `tools/list` (M2: `(SA1) expected resolve-library-id tool in advertised set; got: ["resolve-library-id", "query-docs"]` and `(SA2) expected pack_codebase tool in advertised set; got: [<8 repomix tools>]`), restored via `git checkout --` + md5sum-match-confirm, ran cleanly. The mature WO-0072/0073-shape pattern carries unchanged.
- **Live `tools/list` capture BEFORE writing assertion literals.** Executor spawned `npx -y @upstash/context7-mcp@2.2.4` and `npx -y repomix@1.14.0 --mcp` directly to capture canonical tool names (Context7 v2.2.x: `resolve-library-id` + `query-docs` — NOT `get-library-docs` as the planner's plan-summary suggested; Repomix v1.14.0: `pack_codebase` + 7 others) and embedded the full live list in the manifest top-of-file rustdoc + integration-test panic body. The planner's plan-summary `query-docs` rename surfaced this validation cost.
- **DEC-0005 module-coherence carve-out cited explicitly on plugin-manifest commits.** Both `ef2f845` (Context7 88 LOC) and `b8f593f` (Repomix 86 LOC) commits cite DEC-0005 in the body. The 8-commit cadence held: 4× plugin/devtools, 1× integration test, 2× verify scripts, 1× RFR. Test-file commit (`ccfdf3f` 216 LOC) and verify-script commits (`62cf71c` 210 LOC F02, `9b9b701` 384 LOC F03) implicitly fall under the same carve-out as one cohesive harness — flagged as a soft critic warning but not blocking.
- **Substantive AC23/AC24 coverage protocol + `--no-default-features --features default` arg-pair workaround for ucil-daemon's missing `default` feature.** The literal WO acceptance criterion arg-pair (`--no-default-features --features default`) errors because `ucil-daemon`'s Cargo.toml has no `default` feature defined; without that pair, `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov --package ucil-daemon --tests --summary-only --json` runs cleanly and reports 89.65%. Both spellings documented in the RFR; verifier accepted the workaround form.

### What to carry forward

**For planner**:
- **G5 production-wiring WO is the next dep-blocked follow-up.** Per scope_out #14 — bundle `Context7G5Source` + `RepomixG5Source` + (eventually) `AiderRepoMapG5Source` traits + impls, consuming both manifests from WO-0074 over `tokio::process::Command` + MCP wire format. Same DEC-0008 §4 dependency-inversion seam pattern as the deferred G1 / G3 / G4 production-wiring WOs. The seam is intentional — F02/F03 ship manifests-only; runtime wiring lands later. Aider repo-map (P3-W10-F01) is a separate solo WO requiring substantial Rust reimplementation of PageRank over the call graph (master plan §4.5 line 345).
- **F03 reduction-ratio spec line vs. WO literal needs planner reconciliation in next G5 WO.** WO-0074 scope_in #7 specified "compute the packed-output char-count from the `tools/call` response's content payload" — Repomix returns a ~3 KB metadata summary + outputFilePath pointer in `result.content[]` while writing the full packed XML to a side-file (199276 → 139741 bytes ≈ 30% reduction on the rust-project fixture; well below the master-plan §3.1 line 343 "70% token reduction" claim). The 0.9848 ratio is mathematically correct for the JSON-RPC reply but trivially exceeds the threshold because Repomix bounds the agent-facing payload at ~3 KB regardless of input size. Future planners writing G5+ packing-tool acceptance scripts should specify which measurement is load-bearing (agent-facing payload vs. side-file artifact). Either: (a) accept the agent-facing payload as the load-bearing measurement (Claude-Code-relevant; what the agent actually consumes), or (b) re-spec to read the side-file at `outputFilePath` and assert ≥60% reduction there. The rust-project fixture's measured 30% side-file reduction calibrates the master-plan's 70% claim against measured reality — a future planner may want to revisit the §3.1 claim or substitute a denser fixture.
- **G5 → G6/G7/G8 paired-manifest template port: keep the `g<N>_plugin_manifests.rs` peer file shape.** WO-0074 confirmed the WO-0069 lesson §"separate integration test file per phase/group" — `g5_plugin_manifests.rs` peer of `g3_plugin_manifests.rs` / `g4_plugin_manifests.rs` / `plugin_manifests.rs` keeps each group's `UCIL_SKIP_<GROUP>_PLUGIN_E2E` opt-out scoped distinctly (here: `UCIL_SKIP_CONTEXT_PLUGIN_E2E`). Future G6+ WOs should NOT consolidate into one shared test file.
- **Standing coverage workaround now 30 WOs deep (WO-0058..WO-0074).** Continue scope_out + AC23 standing-protocol substantive coverage check. The intermittent sccache RUSTC_WRAPPER interaction continues to track lower urgency than previously assessed; gate-script reported clean output in WO-0072 + sometimes WO-0073, but the workaround remains the authoritative standing protocol.
- **AC30/AC31 phase-1/phase-2 effectiveness-gate flake now eight WOs deep** (WO-0067, WO-0068, WO-0069, WO-0070, WO-0072, WO-0073, WO-0074). Three pre-existing flake escalations carry; awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO. NOT a blocker — phase-3 work is unaffected.

**For executor**:
- **DON'T translate live `tools/list` names to snake_case when they ship kebab-case.** Context7 v2.2.x emits `resolve-library-id` and `query-docs` in kebab-case. The manifest `[capabilities] provides` list and the integration-test assertion literal MUST use the canonical kebab-case-as-emitted form, NOT a snake-cased translation. Confirmed empirically — M2 mutation produced the live tool list verbatim.
- **DON'T use `--mcp` as a devtools warm-up flag.** `repomix --mcp` spawns the MCP server and blocks on stdin; use `--help` instead for the npm-cache warm-up trigger. Context7's `--help` works analogously. WO-0074 install scripts both use `--help` (not the MCP-mode flag) for warm-up.
- **DON'T forget to escape `UCIL_SKIP_<GROUP>_PLUGIN_E2E` env-var gate-skip paths in test rustdoc + script comments.** WO-0074 documented all three skip paths (test file `skip_via_env()`, F02 verify script, F03 verify script) inline per scope_in #5/#6/#7 ("default to RUN; verifier MUST NOT set either opt-out"). Future G6+ WOs should preserve this documentation pattern — the skip is opt-in by design but a verifier with a stale shell environment could silently skip the load-bearing assertions.
- **DO use python polling with a deadline, NOT bash sleep-based timing, for tools/call wall-time-sensitive smokes.** F03 verify script uses `python3` with a 60-second deadline + `socket`-style polling against the JSON-RPC stdout FIFO; F02 verify script uses bash `sleep 1 → sleep 1 → sleep 10` heuristic. The python form is more robust under slow-network conditions (Context7 reaches context7.com over HTTPS) and should be the canonical shape for any future plugin verify script that asserts a wall-time budget. The bash sleep-based form is a soft flake risk on transient network slowness (>10s response wall-time would race the stdin close).
- **DO copy `tests/fixtures/rust-project` into a `mktemp -d` tmpdir BEFORE invoking `pack_codebase`.** Forbidden_paths mandate `tests/fixtures/**` is read-only; the F03 verify script copies into a tmpdir at line 126 before running the MCP `tools/call`. WO-0074 honored this; future G6+ packing-tool verify scripts MUST follow.
- **DO measure both content-payload reduction AND side-file reduction in the verify-script log output.** F03 verify script logs both `content_chars=3026` (agent-facing) and `side_file_chars=139741` (full packed XML); only the content-payload reduction is the load-bearing assertion per WO scope_in #7 literal, but the side-file reduction is logged for verifier diagnostic visibility + future-planner calibration. Future packing-tool WOs should preserve this dual-measurement logging pattern even if only one is load-bearing.

**For verifier**:
- **For plugin-manifest WOs with pre-baked M1/M2 mutation contracts, use the same in-place mutation + restore-and-md5-confirm protocol as G-runtime WOs.** Snapshot md5sum BEFORE first mutation; apply each mutation via `Edit` (NOT `git stash`); run targeted `cargo test -p ucil-daemon --test g<N>_plugin_manifests g<N>_plugin_manifests::<test_name>` selector; observe SA-tagged panic with full live `tools/list` (M2) or ENOENT-class `Spawn { source: Os { code: 2, kind: NotFound } }` chain (M1); restore via `git checkout -- <file>`; confirm md5sum match; proceed.
- **The `(SAn) <semantic_name>; got: <full-live-tool-list>` panic body format makes verifier mutation-confirmation trivial for plugin-manifest WOs too.** WO-0074's M2 panic was `(SA1) expected resolve-library-id tool in advertised set; got: ["resolve-library-id", "query-docs"]` — verifier reads the panic line, confirms SA1 matches the expected M2 outcome, no grep/diff required. The WO-0073 G-runtime SA-numbered format extends cleanly to plugin-manifest WOs.
- **Ensure `UCIL_SKIP_EXTERNAL_PLUGIN_TESTS` and `UCIL_SKIP_CONTEXT_PLUGIN_E2E` are NOT exported when running `cargo test g<N>_plugin_manifests::*` and `bash scripts/verify/P3-W10-F0[23].sh`.** The skip is opt-in by design but a verifier with a stale shell environment could silently skip the load-bearing assertions. WO-0074 verifier `unset`'d both before each test run; future plugin-manifest WO verifier should preserve this pre-flight check. The skip path emits `[OK] P3-W10-F02` / `[OK] P3-W10-F03` and exits 0 silently — no warning surfaces if the env var is set.
- **`scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug carries from WO-0067/0068/0069/0070/0072/0073 to WO-0074.** Workaround unchanged: the M1/M2 in-place mutation contract from the RFR is the authoritative anti-laziness layer; reality-check.sh is informational only. WO-0074 verifier observed `No local changes to save` on F02 stash (pre-existing-stash bug) and `skip (no commits found)` on F03 (additive-only WOs are skipped). Bucket B candidate; do NOT block on reality-check.sh's spurious diagnostics. The substantive coverage measurement + M1/M2 + critic SA-format inspection is the authoritative anti-laziness chain.
- **Substantive AC23/AC24 coverage measurement: both literal-form and workaround-form are valid.** WO-0074 verifier accepted the workaround form (`env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov --package ucil-daemon --tests --summary-only --json | jq '.data[0].totals.lines.percent'` → 89.6527%) when the literal `--no-default-features --features default` pair errored on missing `default` feature. Future plugin-manifest WOs that don't touch `crates/ucil-daemon/src/**` preserve the pre-WO coverage baseline by construction; both spellings should be acceptable.

**Test-type effectiveness (which acceptance_tests caught bugs vs. were ceremonial)**:
- **Both M1 and M2 SA assertions (per feature) are non-ceremonial.** M1 catches manifest `transport.command` rot (e.g., upstream renames the npm package's bin entry); M2 catches upstream tool-name renames (e.g., Context7 v2.2.x renamed `get-library-docs` → `query-docs` — the executor caught this via live `tools/list` capture, NOT a stale planner literal). Both mutations flipped on first attempt with verbatim left/right values matching the RFR's expected panic shape.
- **The DEC-0007 SA-numbered panic-body format extends cleanly from G-runtime WOs to plugin-manifest WOs.** Verifier mutation-confirmation is mechanical. SA1 (Context7 resolve-library-id) and SA2 (Repomix pack_codebase) ship with this format; future plugin-manifest WOs should preserve.
- **Tool-level smoke (F02 `tools/call resolve-library-id libraryName=vitest` + F03 `tools/call pack_codebase` + wall-time + reduction ratio) is non-ceremonial.** F02 smoke caught the agent-facing content payload shape (1751 chars mentioning vitest); F03 smoke caught wall-time (221.4 ms) and reduction ratio (0.9848 content-payload). Both are load-bearing acceptance signals. The smoke layer is what differentiates a manifest-only WO from a manifest+e2e WO.
- **The `UCIL_SKIP_CONTEXT_PLUGIN_E2E` env-gated runtime skip path is potentially-ceremonial.** Default-to-RUN per WO scope_in #5/#6/#7 means the skip path never fires in the standard verifier flow. Surfaces a soft critic warning (silently exits OK) but not a regression detector — its purpose is to allow CI runners without npm/node to skip cleanly. Could be removed if all CI runners gain npm/node guarantees.

### Technical debt incurred

- **None new.** Pre-existing follow-ups carry forward unchanged from WO-0073:
  1. `scripts/verify/coverage-gate.sh` harness improvement to use `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER` (now 30 WOs deep; Bucket B / Bucket D triage candidate; intermittent — clean in WO-0072 + sometimes WO-0073/WO-0074, stale-FAIL artifact in WO-0074 verifier run).
  2. `scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug (carries from WO-0067/0068/0069/0070/0072/0073).
  3. Effectiveness-gate.sh claude-p sub-session timeout flake (3 open escalations) — pre-existing standing scope_out, awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO.
  4. AC25 "no merge commits introduced on feat" wording — `git log feat ^main --merges = 0` form used successfully in WO-0070 / WO-0072 / WO-0073 / WO-0074.
- **F03 reduction-ratio measurement scope reconciliation** (NOT debt; planner-territory judgment call): WO-0074 scope_in #7 literal vs F03 spec line "≥60% token reduction vs naive file concatenation" measure different things on Repomix's split-payload-architecture (agent-facing JSON-RPC content[] ~3 KB vs. side-file packed XML at outputFilePath). Both measurements logged by the verify script for verifier visibility. Future planner writing G5+ packing-tool acceptance scripts should specify which is load-bearing. Master-plan §3.1 line 343 "70% token reduction" claim is calibrated against measured reality (~30% on rust-project fixture's dense rustdoc-heavy content) — possible §3.1 revision target or denser-fixture substitution candidate.
- **Net-new follow-up work surfaced by F02/F03** (NOT debt; deferred-by-design):
  - G5 production-wiring WO (`Context7G5Source` + `RepomixG5Source` real impls consuming F02 + F03 over `tokio::process::Command` + MCP wire format) — deferred per scope_out #14, parallel to G1 / G3 / G4 production-wiring deferrals.
  - Aider repo-map (P3-W10-F01) — deferred per scope_out #1, separate solo WO requiring PageRank-over-call-graph reimplementation in Rust (master plan §4.5 line 345).
- WO-0074 inherits but does NOT advance debt items 1, 2, 3, 4. The two net-new follow-up items above are deferred-by-design, NOT debt — each has an explicit triggering WO or condition.

## Lessons Learned (WO-0075 — g6-platform-plugin-manifests)

**Features**: P3-W10-F05 (GitHub MCP), P3-W10-F06 (Git MCP), P3-W10-F07 (Filesystem MCP)
**Rejections**: 0 (verifier-green on first attempt; verdict PASS at HEAD `f7e7075`; critic verdict CLEAN with one non-blocking warning on `std::process::Command` in async test helpers)
**Critic blockers**: none — 1 soft warning (W1: blocking `std::process::Command::output()` inside async test helpers `assert_is_git_repo` + `init_git_repo_if_needed`, called from `git_manifest_health_check` via `#[tokio::test]`; would block the tokio worker for a small ≤300 ms fixture-init footprint; not gate-blocking because peer files have no precedent for git-repo fabrication and the violation is in test-only code)
**ADRs raised**: none
**Coverage**: `ucil-daemon` 89.66% line via `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov --package ucil-daemon --tests --summary-only --json` (≥85% floor); WO is purely additive on tests + manifests + scripts (no `crates/ucil-daemon/src/**` source changes), pre-WO baseline preserved by construction.

### What worked

- **G3 → G4 → G5 → G6 paired-manifest template port is now quadruple-verified.** WO-0075 mirrored WO-0074's G5 (Context7 + Repomix) shape verbatim, scaled from 2 to 3 features for the official `@modelcontextprotocol/servers` upstream (GitHub MCP via npx, Git MCP via uvx, Filesystem MCP via npx). The recipe now has zero per-feature execution risk — confidence for G7/G8 forward is high. New `g6_plugin_manifests.rs` peer file, three new manifests under `plugins/platform/<name>/plugin.toml`, three install scripts, three replacement verify scripts; the `UCIL_SKIP_PLATFORM_PLUGIN_E2E` opt-out scoped distinctly from prior groups' env-vars.
- **Pre-baked M1/M2 mutation contract scaled cleanly to three features.** Three M1 mutations (transport.command poison per manifest) + three M2 mutations (expected-tool-name regression per test) applied independently; restore-and-md5-confirm protocol held; `(SA0)`-`(SA3)` SA-numbered panic-body format ships full live `tools/list` arrays in panic text per DEC-0007 + WO-0073/0074 carry-over. Verifier mutation-confirmation is mechanical at this maturity.
- **Live `tools/list` capture surfaced master-plan-vocabulary-vs-upstream-literal divergences for ALL three sources.** GitHub MCP emits 26 tools, none named `list_repositories` (closest is `search_repositories`); chosen M2 literal `list_pull_requests` maps verbatim to capability `platform.github.list_pull_requests`. Git MCP emits 12 tools, no `git_blame` (the `platform.git.blame` capability is forward-compatible; `git_diff`/`git_log`/`git_show` together span the use-case). Filesystem MCP emits 14 tools including `read_file`, `write_file`, `edit_file`, `move_file` — read-side tools verified, write-side tools NOT exercised per F07 spec scope. Capability NAMES (master-plan vocabulary) decouple from upstream tool LITERALS (per WO-0074 §executor #1 lesson — confirmed at scale).
- **F05 GitHub PAT short-circuit pattern (Mem0 precedent) worked unchanged.** `tools/list` cargo-test path is the load-bearing assertion — works without auth and returns the static 26-tool catalog regardless of `GITHUB_PERSONAL_ACCESS_TOKEN` presence. The `tools/call search_repositories` smoke gates on env presence; `[SKIP]` exit 0 if unset. Verifier ran clean with env unset.
- **F06 fabricates a fresh git repo at runtime in a tmpdir copy of `tests/fixtures/rust-project`.** New pattern not seen in g3/g4/g5 peers — `init_git_repo_if_needed` runs `git init` + `git add .` + `git commit` against the tmpdir copy because the fixture is a plain dir, not a git repo. The fixture-pristineness invariant holds (forbidden_paths preserves `tests/fixtures/**` read-only) because mutations land in the `mktemp -d` copy.

### What to carry forward

**For planner**:
- **G6 production-wiring WO is the next dep-blocked follow-up (F08).** Per scope_out #11 — bundle `GitHubG6Source` + `GitG6Source` + `FilesystemG6Source` traits + impls + `execute_g6` orchestrator + `merge_g6_platform_context` aggregation, consuming all three manifests over `tokio::process::Command` + MCP wire format. Same DEC-0008 §4 dependency-inversion seam pattern as the deferred G1/G3/G4/G5 production-wiring WOs. F08 is the dep-blocked feature ID for that follow-up.
- **G7 + G8 paired-manifest WOs apply the same shape as G6 — three or more features, one peer test file each, fresh `UCIL_SKIP_<GROUP>_PLUGIN_E2E` env-var.** The recipe is now quadruple-verified through G6. G7 (Quality? — TBD per master-plan §4.7) and G8 (Testing? — TBD per master-plan §4.8) follow the same recipe verbatim.
- **For F07-style read-only-by-spec WOs against upstream tools that ALSO advertise write-side tools, document the read-only invariant explicitly in scope_in.** WO-0075 scope_in #9 + scope_out #13 spelled out "secure file read and directory listing only — no `write_file` / `move_file` / `delete` exercises even though upstream advertises them"; critic verified the verify script + integration test match this invariant. Future WOs against upstream tools with destructive surfaces should preserve this dual scope_in + scope_out wording.
- **Document upstream-vocabulary-divergence for the planner's M2 literal choice.** When the master-plan capability name (e.g. `platform.github.list_repositories`) does NOT match an upstream literal tool name (e.g. GitHub MCP has `search_repositories` instead), the planner should call out the divergence in scope_in (per WO-0075 scope_in #1: "the master-plan §3.1 vocabulary `list_repositories` etc. is the capability NAME independent of the upstream's literal tool name"). Otherwise the executor must improvise the M2 target choice. WO-0075 surfaced this for both GitHub (`list_repositories` doesn't exist) and Git (`git_blame` doesn't exist).
- **Standing coverage workaround now 31 WOs deep (WO-0058..WO-0075).** Continue scope_out + AC23 standing-protocol substantive coverage check via `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov`. The intermittent sccache RUSTC_WRAPPER interaction continues to track lower urgency than previously assessed; gate-script intermittently produces clean output but the workaround remains the authoritative standing protocol.
- **AC30/AC31 phase-1/phase-2 effectiveness-gate flake now nine WOs deep** (WO-0067..WO-0075). Three pre-existing flake escalations carry; awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO. NOT a blocker — phase-3 work is unaffected.

**For executor**:
- **In async integration tests, use `tokio::process::Command` even for fixture-setup helpers.** WO-0075 critic warning W1: `std::process::Command::output()` blocks the tokio worker; `.claude/rules/rust-style.md` §"Async" line 23 mandates `tokio::process::Command` in async paths. The fixture-init footprint is small (≤300 ms total for `git init` + `git add` + `git commit`), but the rule is unconditional. Mitigation is a one-line switch to `tokio::process::Command` with `.output().await`. Future WOs that fabricate fixtures inside `#[tokio::test]` bodies MUST use the async form. The blocking form passes verifier as test-only debt today, but it's a lurking critic warning every time it appears.
- **For Filesystem MCP installs, `--help` does NOT work as a warm-up flag for `@modelcontextprotocol/server-filesystem` — npm fetch primes the cache as a side-effect anyway.** Executor noted this in the RFR: `install-filesystem-mcp.sh` runs `--help` warm-up but the upstream binary doesn't honor it; the npm-cache-fetch side-effect is what populates the cache for the integration test's first spawn. The install script still exits 0 because it's informational-only. Future install scripts for upstream binaries that don't support `--help` should preserve this pattern (run the warm-up command anyway for the npm-cache side-effect, exit 0 regardless).
- **Capture live `tools/list` from EVERY upstream binary BEFORE writing the manifest's `[capabilities] provides` list AND the integration-test panic-body literal.** WO-0075 captured 26 + 12 + 14 tools across the three sources; the full live arrays are embedded in the manifest top-of-file rustdoc + integration-test SA-tagged panic strings + RFR §"Live tool name capture" section. The executor's one-shot driver script (`/tmp/wo-0075-capture.py`) is a reusable shape — keep this kind of capture step in the executor's pre-flight, NOT after writing the test, so the manifest provides list reflects reality. WO-0074 lesson §executor #1 reaffirmed at scale.
- **For F06-style WOs that need a git repo at runtime in the tmpdir, use the `init_git_repo_if_needed` shape.** Copy the fixture into a `mktemp -d` first, THEN run `git init` + `git add .` + `git commit -m "fixture"` against the copy. The fixture remains pristine (forbidden_paths invariant); the upstream Git MCP server gets a real git repo to query. Use `tokio::process::Command` (per W1 above), NOT `std::process::Command`.
- **Apply WO-0074 §executor lessons #1-#5 verbatim — they all carried.** #1 (no kebab→snake translation; live capture documented in manifest comments — 26/12/14 tool counts), #2 (no `--mcp` for warm-up; use `--help`), #3 (`UCIL_SKIP_PLATFORM_PLUGIN_E2E` documented in test rustdoc + all three verify scripts), #4 (python deadline polling in all three verify scripts), #5 (fixture copy BEFORE invoking — F06.sh:107). Continue forward to G7/G8.

**For verifier**:
- **For tri-feature plugin-manifest WOs with 3× M1 + 3× M2 mutations, run them sequentially — restore between each so the md5sum confirm catches an incomplete restore.** WO-0075 verifier ran 6 mutations total (3× M1 transport.command poison per manifest + 3× M2 expected-tool-name regression per test). Snapshot md5sum BEFORE first mutation per file (one snapshot for `g6_plugin_manifests.rs` covers all three M2 since the file is shared); apply each mutation via `Edit` (NOT `git stash`); run targeted `cargo test -p ucil-daemon --test g6_plugin_manifests g6_plugin_manifests::<test_name>` selector; observe SA-tagged panic with full live `tools/list` (M2) or `Spawn { source: Os { code: 2, kind: NotFound } }` chain (M1); restore via `git checkout -- <file>`; confirm md5sum match; proceed.
- **The `(SA0)`-`(SAn)` SA-numbered panic-body format with full live tool-list embedding is now mature for plugin-manifest WOs.** WO-0075's `(SA1)`/`(SA2)`/`(SA3)` panics each ship the full live tool-list verbatim — verifier reads the SA-tag, confirms semantic match against the M2 expected literal, no grep/diff required. Continue forward as the canonical mutation-confirmation surface for G7/G8 manifest WOs.
- **Ensure `UCIL_SKIP_EXTERNAL_PLUGIN_TESTS` and `UCIL_SKIP_PLATFORM_PLUGIN_E2E` are NOT exported.** WO-0075 scope_in #14 + #15 mandate this pre-flight; the skip path emits `[OK] P3-W10-F0X` and exits 0 silently with no warning surface. WO-0075 verifier `unset`'d both before each test run. Future plugin-manifest WO verifiers preserve this pre-flight check — and per-group, the env-var name changes (`UCIL_SKIP_KNOWLEDGE_PLUGIN_E2E` for G3, `UCIL_SKIP_ARCHITECTURE_PLUGIN_E2E` for G4, `UCIL_SKIP_CONTEXT_PLUGIN_E2E` for G5, `UCIL_SKIP_PLATFORM_PLUGIN_E2E` for G6); G7/G8 will introduce their own.
- **For F05-style API-key-gated WOs, do NOT export the API-key env var (e.g. `GITHUB_PERSONAL_ACCESS_TOKEN`) when verifying.** WO-0075 verifier ran with `GITHUB_PERSONAL_ACCESS_TOKEN` unset; the `tools/list` cargo-test path is the load-bearing assertion regardless of token presence. The `tools/call search_repositories` smoke `[SKIP]`-exits 0 if unset, which is the spec-correct behavior. Exporting the token would unnecessarily reach api.github.com over HTTPS during verification — slower, network-dependent, optional. Keep verification deterministic.
- **`scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug carries to WO-0075.** Workaround unchanged: the M1/M2 in-place mutation contract from the RFR is the authoritative anti-laziness layer; reality-check.sh is informational only. Bucket B candidate; do NOT block on its spurious diagnostics.
- **Substantive AC23/AC24 coverage measurement: `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov --package ucil-daemon --tests --summary-only --json | jq '.data[0].totals.lines.percent'` is the canonical form.** WO-0075 reported 89.66%; the literal `--no-default-features --features default` arg-pair errors because `ucil-daemon`'s Cargo.toml has no `default` feature defined (per WO-0074 lesson). Future plugin-manifest WOs that don't touch `crates/ucil-daemon/src/**` preserve the pre-WO coverage baseline by construction.

**Test-type effectiveness (which acceptance_tests caught bugs vs. were ceremonial)**:
- **All 6 mutation contracts (3× M1 + 3× M2) are non-ceremonial.** M1 catches manifest `transport.command` rot (e.g., upstream renames the npm/pypi package's bin entry, or sysadmin removes `npx`/`uvx` from PATH); M2 catches upstream tool-name renames (e.g., GitHub MCP renaming `list_pull_requests` → `list_prs` in a future release would flip the M2 panic). Both mutations flipped on first attempt with verbatim left/right values matching the RFR's expected panic shape per feature.
- **Tool-level smokes are non-ceremonial across all three features.** F05's `tools/list` capture (26 tools) caught the upstream catalog shape; F06's `tools/call git_log` caught the hex-SHA-prefixed commit-shaped output (208 chars on the rust-project HEAD); F07's `tools/call read_file` + `tools/call list_directory` caught the read-side payload + 3-file directory listing. Each smoke layer differentiates a manifest-only WO from a manifest+e2e WO.
- **The `UCIL_SKIP_PLATFORM_PLUGIN_E2E` env-gated runtime skip path is potentially-ceremonial.** Default-to-RUN per scope_in #6/#7/#8/#9 means the skip path never fires in the standard verifier flow. Surfaces a soft critic warning (silently exits OK) but not a regression detector — its purpose is to allow CI runners without npm/uvx/python3 to skip cleanly. Could be removed if all CI runners gain the three runtimes.
- **F05's `[SKIP] tools/call gated on GITHUB_PERSONAL_ACCESS_TOKEN` short-circuit is non-ceremonial AS A SPEC-CORRECTNESS check.** It never fires under the verifier's clean-env flow (the canonical run leaves the env unset), but it documents the spec-correct behavior: the API-key-gated `tools/call` is optional, the `tools/list` cargo-test path is mandatory. Removing the short-circuit would force the verifier to either always-skip or always-export the token, neither of which matches the spec.

### Technical debt incurred

- **W1: `std::process::Command` blocks tokio in `g6_plugin_manifests.rs:182-250` async test helpers.** Critic surfaced this as non-blocking soft warning. Mitigation is a one-line per-call switch to `tokio::process::Command::output().await`. Carry-forward as a low-priority Bucket D micro-WO candidate (≤6 LOC), or fold into the G6 production-wiring follow-up that will likely touch this file. The blocking form is gate-acceptable today as test-only debt; future test-fixture helpers in async paths should NOT replicate this pattern.
- **Pre-existing follow-ups carry forward unchanged from WO-0074:**
  1. `scripts/verify/coverage-gate.sh` harness improvement to use `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER` (now 31 WOs deep; Bucket B / Bucket D triage candidate; intermittent).
  2. `scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug (carries from WO-0067/0068/0069/0070/0072/0073/0074).
  3. Effectiveness-gate.sh claude-p sub-session timeout flake (3 open escalations) — pre-existing standing scope_out, awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO.
  4. AC25 "no merge commits introduced on feat" wording — `git log feat ^main --merges = 0` form used successfully in WO-0070..WO-0075.
- **Net-new follow-up work surfaced by F05/F06/F07** (NOT debt; deferred-by-design):
  - G6 production-wiring WO (`GitHubG6Source` + `GitG6Source` + `FilesystemG6Source` real impls + `execute_g6` orchestrator + `merge_g6_platform_context` aggregation, consuming all three manifests over `tokio::process::Command` + MCP wire format) — deferred per scope_out #3 / #11 / #14, parallel to G1/G3/G4/G5 production-wiring deferrals. F08 is the dep-blocked feature ID.
- WO-0075 introduces ONE new low-priority debt item (W1) and inherits but does NOT advance debt items 1-4 above.

## Lessons Learned (WO-0076 — eslint-and-semgrep-quality-plugin-manifests)

**Features**: P3-W11-F02 (ESLint MCP), P3-W11-F04 (Semgrep MCP) — P3-W11-F03 (Ruff MCP) explicitly deferred per DEC-0020
**Rejections**: 0 (verifier-green on first attempt; critic verdict CLEAN with two non-blocking soft warnings on `unsafe set_var` + missing-ADR for the unsafe block)
**Critic blockers**: none — 2 soft warnings (W1: `unsafe std::env::set_var("SEMGREP_PATH", ...)` in `g7_plugin_manifests.rs:342-344` claims a `--test-threads=1` protocol that is NOT enforced anywhere in the diff — verify scripts incidentally avoid the race via single-test selectors but a whole-file `cargo test` invocation would race on a multi-core machine; W2: this is the first `unsafe` block introduced by any `g{N}_plugin_manifests.rs` peer file and `.claude/rules/rust-style.md §Unsafe` requires an ADR cite — neither warning gate-blocking but both flag a cleaner-fix follow-up via `Command::env` spawn-time propagation)
**ADRs raised**: DEC-0020 (planner-authored alongside WO — preemptive Ruff MCP deferral; no executor-authored ADRs)
**Coverage**: `ucil-daemon` 89.66% line via `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov --package ucil-daemon --tests --summary-only --json` (≥85% floor); WO is purely additive on tests + manifests + scripts (no `crates/ucil-daemon/src/**` source changes), pre-WO baseline preserved by construction.

### What worked

- **G3 → G4 → G5 → G6 → G7 paired-manifest template port is now quintuple-verified.** WO-0076 mirrored WO-0075's G6 (GitHub + Git + Filesystem) shape verbatim, scaled-down from 3 to 2 features (Ruff deferred per DEC-0020). New `g7_plugin_manifests.rs` peer file, two new manifests under `plugins/quality/<name>/plugin.toml`, two install scripts, two replacement verify scripts; the `UCIL_SKIP_QUALITY_PLUGIN_E2E` opt-out scoped distinctly from prior groups' env-vars (`UCIL_SKIP_KNOWLEDGE_*` G3, `UCIL_SKIP_ARCHITECTURE_*` G4, `UCIL_SKIP_CONTEXT_*` G5, `UCIL_SKIP_PLATFORM_*` G6 — now `UCIL_SKIP_QUALITY_*` G7). The recipe has zero per-feature execution risk at this maturity; G8 forward is mechanical.
- **WO-0075 W1 lesson pre-emptively applied — ZERO critic warning surfaced.** The WO-0075 critic surfaced `std::process::Command` blocking the tokio worker as a soft warning. WO-0076 scope_in #5 + AC13 baked the carve-out into the work-order itself: `! grep -qE 'std::process::Command' crates/ucil-daemon/tests/g7_plugin_manifests.rs`. Executor wrote `version_check`, `resolve_working_semgrep`, `copy_fixture_to_tmpdir` helpers using `tokio::process::Command` from the start. Critic verified clean. **This validates the "carry-forward lessons via pre-emptive scope_in carve-outs + AC enforcement" pattern.** Lessons written to phase-log are not advisory — when planner promotes them to scope_in items + acceptance criteria, the executor produces clean code on first attempt.
- **Live `tools/list` capture surfaced an upstream regression (Semgrep 0.9.0 → 0.8.1 pivot) BEFORE manifest sealing.** Pre-flight live capture against `uvx semgrep-mcp@0.9.0` (the version the planner prescribed in scope_in #2) returned a single `deprecation_notice` tool — the canonical 8-tool scan surface (`semgrep_scan`, `security_check`, `semgrep_findings`, etc.) was removed in v0.9.0 and replaced with a router pointing at the hosted `mcp.semgrep.ai` HTTP server or the `semgrep mcp -t stdio` CLI subcommand. Pinning to 0.9.0 would have failed the F04 acceptance criterion ("≥1 security finding using the OWASP rule set"). Executor pivoted to v0.8.1 (last release with the canonical scan surface), documented the pivot as a Disclosed Deviation in the manifest top-of-file rustdoc + RFR, and shipped clean.
- **External-CLI-dependency short-circuit pattern (new variant of WO-0069 Mem0 API-key gate).** Both `semgrep-mcp@0.8.1` and `@0.9.0` invoke `semgrep --pro --version` from the upstream lifespan handler BEFORE the MCP server reaches its initialize handshake. If the Semgrep CLI is missing (or broken), the server raises `McpError` and the integration test sees `BrokenPipe` before tools/list completes. Executor wrote `resolve_working_semgrep()` helper that filters out the broken uvx-bundled venv semgrep (uvx prepends a venv that ships an `opentelemetry-instrumentation-requests`-conflicting binary) and gates on a successful `semgrep --version`. When no working CLI is found, the smoke `[SKIP]`-exits 0 (operator-state, NOT failure). The integration test additionally exports `SEMGREP_PATH` to the spawned uvx subprocess so `find_semgrep_info` resolves the working binary instead of the broken venv-bundled one.
- **F02 ESLint config + deliberate-lint-violation fabrication pattern.** ESLint MCP zero-config produces zero findings on the read-only `tests/fixtures/typescript-project`. Executor fabricated a minimal `eslint.config.js` + a `bad.js` deliberate-lint-violation file (`var x = 1; const unused = 42;`) in the tmpdir copy BEFORE invoking the upstream binary. The `tools/call lint-files` smoke produces 3 structured findings with `filePath/ruleId/severity/line` keys per F02 spec. Fixture-pristineness invariant holds (forbidden_paths preserves `tests/fixtures/**` read-only) because mutations land in the `mktemp -d` tmpdir copy.
- **Pre-baked M1/M2 mutation contract scaled cleanly to two features.** Two M1 mutations (transport.command poison per manifest: `"npx"` → ENOENT for ESLint, `"uvx"` → ENOENT for Semgrep) + two M2 mutations (expected-tool-name regression: `"lint-files"` → `"NON_EXISTENT_TOOL_M2"` in `eslint_manifest_health_check`, `"semgrep_scan"` → same in `semgrep_manifest_health_check`); `(SA0)`-`(SA2)` SA-numbered panic-body format ships full live `tools/list` arrays per DEC-0007. Verifier mutation-confirmation mechanical at this maturity.
- **DEC-0020 preemptive-deferral pattern (PyPI-404 + npm-search + GitHub-search triad) successfully replaced a 30-min DEC-0019-style 2-attempt-blocked spiral.** WO-0071 attempt-1 + attempt-2 absorbed ~30 min of executor cycles + critic + verifier wall-time before DEC-0019 deferred graphiti reactively. WO-0076 saved that entire spiral by checking upstream availability AT PLANNER TIME (DEC-0020 §Context documents the triad) and authoring the deferral preemptively. **This is now a reusable preemptive-deferral pattern for any future master-plan-anticipated-but-not-yet-published MCP server (Sonarqube, Snyk, Trivy, RuboCop, etc.).**

### What to carry forward

**For planner**:
- **Run the upstream-availability sweep (PyPI-404 + npm-search + GitHub-search triad) BEFORE bundling any master-plan-anticipated MCP server into a WO.** DEC-0020 §Context documents the curl/npm/gh exact-command triad — `curl -sLI https://pypi.org/pypi/<pkg>/json` (expect non-404), `npm view <pkg>` (expect non-empty), `gh repo view <vendor>/<pkg>` (expect existing public repo). If ANY canonical published package exists with stable releases, emit the WO; if NONE has emerged, author a DEC-NNNN deferral ADR citing DEC-0020 as lineage. **This pattern saves a full WO worth of executor cycles per blocked feature (DEC-0019 reactive cost was ~30 min wall-time per attempt × 2 attempts).**
- **Live `tools/list` MUST be captured AT THE SPECIFIC PINNED VERSION before sealing a manifest's `[capabilities] provides` list.** WO-0076 surfaced that `uvx semgrep-mcp@0.9.0` (pre-flight LATEST publish 2025-09-29) ships a single `deprecation_notice` tool — the v0.8.1 8-tool canonical scan surface was removed. **Latest != stable canonical surface.** The planner's scope_in MUST direct the executor to capture live tool-lists at the EXACT pinned version, NOT trust pre-flight version-search alone. Future planner passes for plugin-manifest WOs SHOULD include a scope_in line like: "Executor MUST live-capture `tools/list` at the prescribed pinned version BEFORE manifest sealing; if the canonical tool surface is missing or deprecated, pivot down to the latest preceding release that exposes the canonical surface and document the pivot as a Disclosed Deviation in the manifest top-of-file rustdoc + RFR."
- **For MCP servers with external CLI dependencies, document the CLI dep as load-bearing operator-state in scope_in.** Semgrep MCP requires `semgrep` on PATH (or `SEMGREP_PATH`) — this surfaced as a Disclosed Deviation in WO-0076 because no prior G-group plugin had an external-CLI dep. Future planner passes for plugin-manifest WOs (Sonarqube MCP needs Sonar CLI; Snyk MCP needs Snyk CLI; Trivy MCP needs Trivy CLI; RuboCop MCP needs Ruby + RuboCop) SHOULD declare the CLI dependency in scope_in as a first-class load-bearing detail, NOT discover it post-implementation. Suggested scope_in shape: "External operator-state: `<binary>` CLI must be on PATH or located via `<BINARY>_PATH` env var. Integration test + verify script MUST gate the smoke on a pre-flight `<binary> --version` check; `[SKIP]` exit 0 on miss (operator-state, NOT failure)."
- **G7 → G8 paired-manifest WO applies the same shape as G7 — two or more features, one peer test file each, fresh `UCIL_SKIP_TESTING_PLUGIN_E2E` env-var.** Recipe is now quintuple-verified through G7. G8 (master-plan §4.8 — Testing) follows the same recipe verbatim.
- **For verify scripts that use parent-process env-var mutation (e.g. `SEMGREP_PATH`), prescribe `--test-threads=1` enforcement OR direct `Command::env` propagation in scope_in.** WO-0076 critic W1 surfaced that the test file claims a `--test-threads=1` protocol the diff doesn't enforce. The cleanest fix is `Command::env("SEMGREP_PATH", ...)` on the spawned child via `PluginManager::spawn`-time API — but that requires a daemon-side `manifest.transport.env` table + spawn-time env propagation which is out of scope for a plugin-manifest WO. Future planner passes that touch parent-process env-var mutation in `#[tokio::test]` async fns SHOULD either (a) require `--test-threads=1` in the verify scripts as a scope_in item, OR (b) bundle a small daemon-side `manifest.transport.env` table change as a co-WO so the executor can use the cleaner `Command::env` form.
- **Standing coverage workaround now 32 WOs deep (WO-0058..WO-0076).** Continue scope_out + AC23 standing-protocol substantive coverage check via `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov`. The intermittent sccache RUSTC_WRAPPER interaction continues at lower urgency.
- **AC30/AC31 phase-1/phase-2 effectiveness-gate flake now ten WOs deep** (WO-0067..WO-0076). Three pre-existing flake escalations carry; awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO. NOT a blocker — phase-3 work is unaffected.

**For executor**:
- **Live `tools/list` capture AT THE SPECIFIC PINNED VERSION is non-negotiable before writing manifest `[capabilities] provides` literals.** WO-0076 caught the Semgrep 0.9.0 → 0.8.1 regression because the executor lived-captured at v0.9.0 BEFORE writing the manifest. Skipping the live capture would have produced a manifest pinned to v0.9.0 with a fabricated 8-tool `provides` list that doesn't match the upstream's actual single-tool surface — M2 mutation would have flipped trivially (every literal would mismatch), but the manifest itself would be a lie. **Capture live, manifest after.**
- **For external-CLI-dependent MCP servers, write a `resolve_working_<binary>` helper that filters broken bundled-venv binaries.** WO-0076's `resolve_working_semgrep()` shape: iterate candidate paths (env var first, then PATH probe, then well-known install dirs), call `<binary> --version` via `tokio::process::Command::output().await`, accept on success + reject on broken venv `ImportError` exit code. The helper is reusable for any future MCP server with an external CLI dep (Sonarqube, Snyk, Trivy, RuboCop). Filter shape: parse the version output, reject if it contains `ModuleNotFoundError` / `ImportError` / `Traceback` / non-zero exit code.
- **For ESLint-style MCP servers that require config + lint-target file fabrication, the tmpdir is the right place.** WO-0076 F02 wrote `eslint.config.js` (`import js from "@eslint/js"; export default [js.configs.recommended];`) + a deliberate-lint-violation `bad.js` (`var x = 1; const unused = 42;`) in the tmpdir copy. The ESLint MCP server runs from the tmpdir as cwd, picks up the fabricated config, and produces 3 findings against `bad.js`. **Fixture-pristineness invariant holds; mutations land in `mktemp -d` only.** This pattern generalizes to any MCP server that needs a config file the upstream binary expects in cwd.
- **For `unsafe std::env::set_var` in `#[tokio::test]` async fn bodies, prefer `Command::env` on the spawned child.** WO-0076 W1 critic warning: `unsafe { set_var("SEMGREP_PATH", ...) }` mutates the parent process's env table; Rust 2024 marked this `unsafe` because concurrent set_var/getenv across threads is UB. The cleanest fix (when the daemon-side `PluginManager` exposes a `Command::env` API at spawn time) is to pass the env-var to the spawned child only. Until the daemon ships `manifest.transport.env` propagation, the workaround is `--test-threads=1` enforcement in the verify script + a SAFETY comment citing the protocol. **Future executors SHOULD avoid parent-process env-var mutation when a per-spawn alternative exists.**
- **Apply WO-0075 §executor lessons #1-#5 verbatim — they all carried forward to G7.** #1 (no kebab→snake translation; live capture documented in manifest comments — `lint-files` kebab-case + `semgrep_scan` snake_case both verbatim per upstream emission), #2 (no `--mcp` for warm-up; both install scripts use `--help`), #3 (`UCIL_SKIP_QUALITY_PLUGIN_E2E` documented in test rustdoc + both verify scripts), #4 (python deadline polling in both verify scripts: 90s init / 30s tools-list / 60s tools-call for ESLint; 180s init / 30s tools-list / 120s tools-call for Semgrep — Semgrep scans take 10-30s on cold rule-cache), #5 (fixture copy BEFORE invoking — both F02.sh + F04.sh).
- **Apply WO-0075 §executor W1 lesson pre-emptively — it works.** WO-0076 baked `tokio::process::Command` use into AC13 (`! grep -qE 'std::process::Command' ...`). Critic verified clean — ZERO warning. **Pre-emptive carve-outs in scope_in + AC enforcement convert recurring critic warnings into one-shot clean reviews.** Continue forward as a pattern: every recurring critic warning surfaced at WO-N becomes a scope_in item + AC at WO-N+1.

**For verifier**:
- **For two-feature plugin-manifest WOs with 2× M1 + 2× M2 mutations, run them sequentially — restore between each.** WO-0076 verifier ran 4 mutations total (2× M1 transport.command poison per manifest + 2× M2 expected-tool-name regression per test). Snapshot md5sum BEFORE first mutation per file (one snapshot for `g7_plugin_manifests.rs` covers both M2 since the file is shared); apply each mutation via `Edit` (NOT `git stash`); run targeted `cargo test -p ucil-daemon --test g7_plugin_manifests g7_plugin_manifests::<test_name>` selector; observe SA-tagged panic with full live `tools/list` (M2) or `Spawn { source: Os { code: 2, kind: NotFound } }` chain (M1); restore via `git checkout -- <file>`; confirm md5sum match; proceed.
- **Ensure `UCIL_SKIP_EXTERNAL_PLUGIN_TESTS` and `UCIL_SKIP_QUALITY_PLUGIN_E2E` are NOT exported.** WO-0076 scope_in #12 + #13 mandate this pre-flight; the skip path emits `[OK] P3-W11-F0X` and exits 0 silently. Per-group, the env-var name changes (G3 → G7 covered above; G8 introduces its own).
- **For Semgrep-style WOs that require external CLI on PATH, ensure `semgrep --version` returns clean BEFORE running the verify script.** The integration test's `resolve_working_semgrep()` filters broken venv binaries, but if NO working binary exists at all, the smoke `[SKIP]`-exits 0 — which is spec-correct per the operator-state short-circuit pattern, but means the verifier's M2 mutation against `"semgrep_scan"` won't trigger. Verify the skip path is NOT firing by grepping the cargo test output for `[SKIP]` strings and the verify-script log for `tools/call` reply assertions. If `[SKIP]` fires, install Semgrep CLI per `scripts/devtools/install-semgrep-mcp.sh` operator guidance and re-run.
- **Watch for `unsafe` blocks in test code without ADR cite — soft critic-warning category to flag.** `.claude/rules/rust-style.md §Unsafe` requires an ADR justification for any `unsafe` block. WO-0076's `unsafe { set_var("SEMGREP_PATH", ...) }` is the first such block in any `g{N}_plugin_manifests.rs` peer file. Future plugin-manifest WOs that introduce `unsafe` MUST either include an ADR or mechanize the protocol the SAFETY comment claims (e.g. `--test-threads=1` in cargo config or verify scripts). Verifier should grep the diff for `unsafe ` and reject if no adjacent ADR cite exists.
- **The `(SA0)`-`(SAn)` SA-numbered panic-body format is now mature for plugin-manifest WOs.** WO-0076's `(SA0)`/`(SA1)`/`(SA2)` panics each ship the full live tool-list verbatim — verifier reads the SA-tag, confirms semantic match against the M2 expected literal, no grep/diff required. Continue forward as the canonical mutation-confirmation surface for G8 manifest WOs.
- **`scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug carries to WO-0076.** Workaround unchanged: the M1/M2 in-place mutation contract from the RFR is the authoritative anti-laziness layer; reality-check.sh is informational only. Bucket B candidate; do NOT block on its spurious diagnostics.
- **Substantive AC23/AC24 coverage measurement: `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov --package ucil-daemon --tests --summary-only --json | jq '.data[0].totals.lines.percent'` is the canonical form.** WO-0076 reported 89.66%; the literal `--no-default-features --features default` arg-pair errors because `ucil-daemon`'s Cargo.toml has no `default` feature defined (per WO-0074/0075 lesson). Future plugin-manifest WOs that don't touch `crates/ucil-daemon/src/**` preserve the pre-WO coverage baseline by construction.

**Test-type effectiveness (which acceptance_tests caught bugs vs. were ceremonial)**:
- **All 4 mutation contracts (2× M1 + 2× M2) are non-ceremonial.** M1 catches manifest `transport.command` rot (e.g., upstream renames the npm/pypi package's bin entry, or sysadmin removes `npx`/`uvx` from PATH); M2 catches upstream tool-name renames (e.g., a hypothetical `@eslint/mcp@1.0.0` renaming `lint-files` → `lint_files`, OR a hypothetical `semgrep-mcp@0.9.x` removing `semgrep_scan` would flip the M2 panic — and indeed the v0.9.0 capture surfaced exactly this regression). Both mutation classes flipped on first attempt with verbatim left/right values matching the RFR's expected panic shape per feature.
- **Tool-level smokes are non-ceremonial across both features.** F02's `tools/call lint-files` produced 3 structured findings (`no-unused-vars` rule, severity 2, line 1, file `bad.js`) — caught the upstream's structured-finding payload shape (`filePath`/`ruleId`/`severity`/`line`). F04's `tools/call semgrep_scan {code_files, config: "p/owasp-top-ten"}` produced 1 OWASP A03 Injection finding (`subprocess-shell-true`) — caught the upstream's structured-finding payload shape (`check_id`/`extra.severity`/`path`/`start.line`). Each smoke layer differentiates a manifest-only WO from a manifest+e2e WO.
- **The `UCIL_SKIP_QUALITY_PLUGIN_E2E` env-gated runtime skip path is potentially-ceremonial** (same shape as G6's `UCIL_SKIP_PLATFORM_PLUGIN_E2E`). Default-to-RUN per scope_in #5/#6/#7 means the skip path never fires in the standard verifier flow. Surfaces a soft critic warning (silently exits OK) but not a regression detector — its purpose is to allow CI runners without npm/uvx/python3 to skip cleanly. Could be removed if all CI runners gain the three runtimes.
- **F04's `[SKIP] gated on resolve_working_semgrep()` short-circuit is non-ceremonial AS A SPEC-CORRECTNESS check.** It documents the spec-correct behavior: when the Semgrep CLI is missing or broken, the smoke skips with a clear diagnostic rather than producing a false-failure. Removing the short-circuit would force the verifier to either always-skip (when CLI missing) or hard-fail on operator-state (when CLI missing), neither of which matches the load-bearing assertion model. Same shape as F05's `GITHUB_PERSONAL_ACCESS_TOKEN` short-circuit per WO-0075.

### Technical debt incurred

- **W1 (NEW): `unsafe std::env::set_var("SEMGREP_PATH", ...)` in `g7_plugin_manifests.rs:342-344` claims a `--test-threads=1` protocol that is not enforced.** Critic surfaced this as non-blocking soft warning. Mitigation options (ranked): (a) use `Command::env("SEMGREP_PATH", &semgrep_path)` directly on the spawned child via `PluginManager::spawn`-time API — cleanest, requires a daemon-side `manifest.transport.env` table change (out-of-scope for a plugin-manifest WO; bundle as a co-WO); (b) hard-pin `--test-threads=1` in both verify scripts; (c) wrap the `set_var` in a `serial_test`-annotated `#[serial(env_semgrep)]`. Carry-forward as a low-priority Bucket D micro-WO candidate (≤8 LOC for option b).
- **W2 (NEW): `unsafe` block without ADR cite.** First `unsafe` introduced by any `g{N}_plugin_manifests.rs` peer file. Mitigation tied to W1's option (a) — switching to `Command::env` removes the unsafe block entirely. If W1 is resolved via option (a) or (c), W2 dissolves; if via option (b), an ADR documenting the test-environment protocol should accompany.
- **Pre-existing follow-ups carry forward unchanged from WO-0075:**
  1. `scripts/verify/coverage-gate.sh` harness improvement to use `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER` (now 32 WOs deep; Bucket B / Bucket D triage candidate; intermittent).
  2. `scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug (carries from WO-0067/0068/0069/0070/0072/0073/0074/0075).
  3. Effectiveness-gate.sh claude-p sub-session timeout flake (3 open escalations) — pre-existing standing scope_out, awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO.
  4. AC25 "no merge commits introduced on feat" wording — `git log feat ^main --merges = 0` form used successfully in WO-0070..WO-0076.
- **Net-new follow-up work surfaced by WO-0076** (NOT debt; deferred-by-design):
  - **Daemon-side `manifest.transport.env` table + spawn-time env propagation.** Resolves W1+W2 cleanly. Bucket D candidate or part of a future G7 production-wiring WO.
  - **G7 production-wiring WO (`EsLintG7Source` + `SemgrepG7Source` traits + impls + `execute_g7` orchestrator + `merge_g7_quality_context` aggregation, consuming both manifests over `tokio::process::Command` + MCP wire format).** Deferred per scope_out #2 / #3 / #14, parallel to G1/G3/G4/G5/G6 production-wiring deferrals. F05 is the dep-blocked feature ID for the follow-up — currently dep-blocked on F01 (LSP diagnostics bridge wired into G7) not F02/F04 alone, so this WO advances F05's manifest readiness but not its full dep graph.
  - **DEC-0020 §Revisit-trigger re-check at next planner pass that suspects an upstream Ruff MCP server has emerged.** P3-W11-F03 deferred-pending-upstream; the curl/npm/gh triad is documented for re-examination.
- WO-0076 introduces TWO new low-priority debt items (W1 + W2, tightly coupled) and inherits but does NOT advance debt items 1-4 above.

## Lessons Learned (WO-0077 — mcp-pytest-runner-plugin-manifest)

**Features**: P3-W11-F08 (mcp-pytest-runner) — P3-W11-F07 (test-runner-mcp) explicitly deferred per DEC-0021
**Rejections**: 0 (verifier-green on first attempt; critic verdict CLEAN with one non-blocking soft warning on commit-size for the verify script — precedent-acceptable per WO-0072/0074/0075/0076)
**Critic blockers**: none — 1 soft warning (W1: 472-LOC `scripts/verify/P3-W11-F08.sh` single commit exceeds the ~200-LOC soft target; coherent shell script where splitting would be artificial; same shape as WO-0072/0074/0075/0076 verify scripts; consider DEC-0005 module-coherence citation in future commit bodies)
**ADRs raised**: DEC-0021 (planner-authored alongside WO — preemptive test-runner-mcp deferral; no executor-authored ADRs)
**Coverage**: `ucil-daemon` 89.65% line via `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov --package ucil-daemon --tests --summary-only --json` (≥85% floor); WO is purely additive on tests + manifests + scripts (no `crates/ucil-daemon/src/**` source changes), pre-WO baseline preserved by construction.

### What worked

- **G3 → G4 → G5 → G6 → G7 → G8 paired-manifest template port is now sextuple-verified.** WO-0077 mirrored WO-0076's G7 shape verbatim, retargeted from `quality.*` to `testing.*` namespace and scaled-down from 2 to 1 feature (test-runner-mcp deferred per DEC-0021). New `g8_plugin_manifests.rs` peer file, one new manifest under `plugins/testing/mcp-pytest-runner/plugin.toml`, one install script, one replacement verify script; the `UCIL_SKIP_TESTING_PLUGIN_E2E` opt-out scoped distinctly from prior groups' env-vars (`UCIL_SKIP_KNOWLEDGE_*` G3, `UCIL_SKIP_ARCHITECTURE_*` G4, `UCIL_SKIP_CONTEXT_*` G5, `UCIL_SKIP_PLATFORM_*` G6, `UCIL_SKIP_QUALITY_*` G7, now `UCIL_SKIP_TESTING_*` G8). The recipe has zero per-feature execution risk at this maturity — G8 closes the Phase 3 paired-manifest WO sweep.
- **DEC-0021 is the THIRD application of the preemptive-deferral pattern — chain DEC-0019 reactive → DEC-0020 preemptive → DEC-0021 preemptive is now firmly established.** The pre-flight upstream-availability sweep (PyPI-404 + npm-search + GitHub-search triad documented at DEC-0020 §Context) reused verbatim caught test-runner-mcp at planner-time, saving the ~30 min DEC-0019-style 2-attempt-blocked spiral wall-time. Three deferrals (P3-W9-F10 graphiti, P3-W11-F03 ruff, P3-W11-F07 test-runner-mcp) are now mechanically grep-able via `blocked_reason` sentinels for Phase 4/7 re-scoping passes — though only DEC-0019/0020/0021 ADRs are the authoritative deferral markers per the precedent (none of the three features have `blocked_reason` sentinels written; the verifier left F08's `last_verified_*` fields populated and F07 untouched).
- **WO-0075 W1 lesson stays clean across two consecutive WOs (WO-0076 + WO-0077) when pre-emptively applied.** AC `! grep -qE 'std::process::Command' crates/ucil-daemon/tests/g8_plugin_manifests.rs` enforced; rustdoc rephrased ("the tokio variant of the process-spawn API (NOT the blocking standard-library variant)") to avoid the literal string per the WO-0076 carve-out. **The pre-emptive-carve-out + AC-enforcement pattern is now twice-validated end-to-end** — recurring critic warnings surfaced at WO-N → become scope_in items + ACs at WO-N+1 → produce zero-warning critic reviews on first attempt. WO-0077 needed NO direct subprocess spawning (the test calls `PluginManager::health_check_with_timeout` which handles uvx subprocess spawn internally), but the rustdoc word-ban grep still applied; the rephrasing convention is now standard.
- **PyPI package name vs serverInfo.name asymmetry surfaced and documented cleanly.** Live capture against `uvx mcp-pytest-runner@0.2.1` revealed that `serverInfo.name == "pytest-mcp"` while the PyPI package name is `mcp-pytest-runner`. Both names embedded verbatim in manifest top-of-file rustdoc + RFR §"Live tool name capture" section. **Plugin-manifest authors MUST capture both the PyPI/npm package name (the install string) AND the `serverInfo.name` (the runtime advertised name) — they may differ.** Future WOs for MCP servers SHOULD document this asymmetry when present; the planner's pre-flight research surfaces the package name, but the executor's live capture is the only source for the runtime name.
- **Tmpdir-fabrication pattern for src-layout pytest fixtures: fabricate `conftest.py` to put `src/` on `sys.path`.** F08 verify script copies `tests/fixtures/python-project` into a tmpdir, then writes a `conftest.py` (`import sys; from pathlib import Path; sys.path.insert(0, str(Path(__file__).parent / "src"))`) at the tmpdir root so pytest can import the `python_project` package without an editable install. This is in the tmpdir copy ONLY; the read-only fixture stays pristine. **Same shape as WO-0076's ESLint `eslint.config.js` + `bad.js` fabrication pattern** — when an MCP server requires runtime-side configuration the upstream binary expects in cwd, fabricate it in the tmpdir copy. Generalizes to any future MCP server requiring per-project config files.
- **No external CLI dependency — uvx-managed venv handles pytest.** Unlike WO-0076's Semgrep MCP (which required `semgrep --version` on PATH or `SEMGREP_PATH`), `mcp-pytest-runner` resolves pytest via the uvx-managed venv (the upstream package declares pytest as a dependency in its `pyproject.toml`). **No `resolve_working_<binary>` helper or operator-state short-circuit needed.** The integration test calls `PluginManager::health_check_with_timeout` directly; the `tools/call discover_tests` smoke just spawns `uvx mcp-pytest-runner@0.2.1` from the tmpdir. The W1+W2 unsafe-set_var debt from WO-0076 dissolves naturally for this WO (no parent-process env-var mutation needed). **Future planner passes for plugin-manifest WOs SHOULD distinguish between operator-state-CLI-dependent MCP servers (Semgrep, Sonarqube, Snyk, Trivy, RuboCop) and self-resolving MCP servers (mcp-pytest-runner, ESLint MCP via npx).**
- **Cold-cache uvx fetch budget (~30s first run) is the limiting factor for FIRST_RUN_TIMEOUT_MS / verify-script deadlines.** Integration test sets `FIRST_RUN_TIMEOUT_MS = 120_000`; verify script uses 90s/120s deadlines. Subsequent runs are <1s. **For uvx-launched MCP servers, budget at least 90s for cold-cache first runs; document the cold-vs-warm cache asymmetry in the test rustdoc + verify script comments.** Generalizes to any future uvx-launched plugin (mem0 G3, codegraphcontext G4, Context7 + Repomix G5, Semgrep G7, mcp-pytest-runner G8 — five WOs deep with this pattern).
- **SOLO-FEATURE WO with DEFERRED peer pattern is now twice-verified end-to-end.** WO-0072 (codegraphcontext G4 with graphiti deferred per DEC-0019) → WO-0077 (mcp-pytest-runner G8 with test-runner-mcp deferred per DEC-0021). Both shipped clean on first attempt with the same scope_in shape: one feature, one deferred peer, one ADR (planner-authored alongside the WO), one peer test file with a single `#[tokio::test]`, one M1 + one M2 mutation contract. **This shape is now the canonical pattern for paired-feature WOs where one upstream is missing.** Future planner passes SHOULD prefer this shape over a 2-feature WO that requires a git-SHA-pinned third-party fork (which would violate AC32 immutable-tag policy).

### What to carry forward

**For planner**:
- **The preemptive-deferral pattern (PyPI-404 + npm-search + GitHub-search triad → ADR + scope-out) is now THRICE-applied (DEC-0019/0020/0021).** Future planner passes that suspect a master-plan-anticipated MCP server doesn't exist yet MUST run the triad BEFORE bundling the feature into a WO. Saves a full WO worth of executor cycles per blocked feature. The DEC-0019 → DEC-0020 → DEC-0021 chain is the convention; future ADRs MUST cite the preceding ADR(s) as lineage.
- **Capture BOTH PyPI/npm package name AND `serverInfo.name` from live MCP handshake.** Future plugin-manifest WO scope_in items SHOULD include a line like: "Executor MUST live-capture both the PyPI/npm package name (as documented in the manifest's `[plugin] name` field — derived from upstream package) AND the `serverInfo.name` (as emitted by the MCP server's `initialize` response — may differ from package name). Document the asymmetry in the manifest's top-of-file rustdoc when it occurs." The mcp-pytest-runner / pytest-mcp asymmetry is the canonical example.
- **Distinguish operator-state-CLI-dependent vs self-resolving MCP servers in scope_in.** Operator-state-CLI-dependent (Semgrep, Sonarqube, Snyk, Trivy, RuboCop) require external CLI on PATH or via `<BINARY>_PATH` env var, plus a `resolve_working_<binary>` helper, plus an operator-state short-circuit (`[SKIP] CLI not found`). Self-resolving (mcp-pytest-runner, ESLint MCP via npx, Context7, Repomix, Mem0, GitHub MCP, Git MCP, Filesystem MCP, codegraphcontext) resolve dependencies via uvx/npx-managed venv automatically — no helper needed. **Future planner passes SHOULD declare which class the WO falls into in scope_in.**
- **G8 is the LAST G-group of Phase 3.** With WO-0077 shipping mcp-pytest-runner, all eight G-groups (G1 through G8) have at least one plugin manifest landed in Phase 3. The G-group production-wiring follow-up WOs (G1/G3/G4/G5/G6/G7/G8 — all 7 deferred per scope_out conventions) remain as Phase 4/5 work. **Phase 3 paired-manifest WO sweep is COMPLETE** modulo the three ADR-deferred features (DEC-0019/0020/0021).
- **For SOLO-FEATURE WO with deferred peer, mirror the WO-0072/0077 shape verbatim.** One feature, one deferred peer, one ADR (planner-authored alongside the WO), one peer test file with a single `#[tokio::test]`, one M1 + one M2 mutation contract. Avoid 2-feature WOs that require a git-SHA-pinned fork — defer the second feature instead.
- **Standing coverage workaround now 33 WOs deep (WO-0058..WO-0077).** Continue scope_out + AC23 standing-protocol substantive coverage check via `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov`. The intermittent sccache RUSTC_WRAPPER interaction continues at lower urgency.
- **AC30/AC31 phase-1/phase-2 effectiveness-gate flake now eleven WOs deep** (WO-0067..WO-0077). Three pre-existing flake escalations carry; awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO. NOT a blocker — phase-3 work is unaffected.

**For executor**:
- **For uvx-launched MCP servers, budget at least 90s for cold-cache first runs in test/verify-script deadlines.** Cold-cache uvx fetch (resolves the package + deps + downloads wheels) takes up to ~30s; subsequent runs are <1s. WO-0077 used `FIRST_RUN_TIMEOUT_MS = 120_000` in the integration test and 90s/120s deadlines in the verify script. Document the cold-vs-warm cache asymmetry inline.
- **Apply WO-0076 §executor lessons #1-#5 verbatim — they all carried forward to G8.** #1 (no kebab→snake translation; live capture at the pinned version documented in manifest rustdoc — `discover_tests` + `execute_tests` snake_case as emitted by upstream), #2 (no `--mcp` for warm-up; install script uses `uvx … --help`), #3 (`UCIL_SKIP_TESTING_PLUGIN_E2E` documented in test rustdoc + verify script), #4 (python deadline polling in verify script: 90s init / 30s tools-list / 120s tools-call — pytest discovery may take seconds on cold start), #5 (fixture copy BEFORE invoking — verify script uses file-by-file copy with `__pycache__` / `.pytest_cache` prune).
- **Apply WO-0075/0076 §executor W1 lesson pre-emptively — twice-validated.** AC `! grep -qE 'std::process::Command' …` enforced in scope_in + acceptance_criteria; rustdoc rephrased to avoid the literal string. ZERO critic warning across two consecutive WOs (WO-0076 + WO-0077). **Pre-emptive carve-outs in scope_in + AC enforcement convert recurring critic warnings into one-shot clean reviews — proven recipe.**
- **For pytest-style MCP servers, fabricate `conftest.py` for src-layout fixtures.** WO-0077's `conftest.py` (`import sys; from pathlib import Path; sys.path.insert(0, str(Path(__file__).parent / "src"))`) puts the fixture's `src/` directory on `sys.path` so pytest can import the package without an editable install. **Fixture-pristineness invariant holds; mutation lands in `mktemp -d` only.** Generalizes to any future test-runner MCP server requiring per-project pytest config in cwd.
- **PyPI package name vs serverInfo.name MAY differ — document both verbatim in manifest top-of-file rustdoc.** WO-0077's manifest documents both `mcp-pytest-runner` (PyPI package, install string) and `pytest-mcp` (serverInfo.name, runtime advertised name). Future MCP server manifests SHOULD capture both names from live handshake when they differ.

**For verifier**:
- **For SOLO-FEATURE plugin-manifest WOs with 1× M1 + 1× M2 mutations, run them sequentially — restore between each.** WO-0077 verifier ran 2 mutations total. Snapshot md5sum BEFORE first mutation per file; apply each via `Edit` (NOT `git stash`); run targeted `cargo test -p ucil-daemon --test g8_plugin_manifests g8_plugin_manifests::mcp_pytest_runner_manifest_health_check`; observe SA-tagged panic with full live `tools/list` (M2) or `Spawn { source: Os { code: 2, kind: NotFound } }` chain (M1); restore via `git checkout -- <file>`; confirm md5sum match; proceed.
- **Ensure `UCIL_SKIP_EXTERNAL_PLUGIN_TESTS` and `UCIL_SKIP_TESTING_PLUGIN_E2E` are NOT exported.** WO-0077 scope_in #10 mandates this pre-flight; the skip path emits `[OK] P3-W11-F08` and exits 0 silently. Per-group, the env-var name changes — G8 introduces `UCIL_SKIP_TESTING_PLUGIN_E2E` (joining the G3-G7 family).
- **The `(SA0)`-`(SAn)` SA-numbered panic-body format remains the canonical mutation-confirmation surface.** WO-0077's `(SA1)` panic ships the full live tool-list verbatim (`["execute_tests", "discover_tests"]`) — verifier reads the SA-tag, confirms semantic match against the M2 expected literal, no grep/diff required. Continue forward as the canonical mutation-confirmation surface for any future plugin-manifest WOs.
- **`scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug carries to WO-0077.** Workaround unchanged: the M1/M2 in-place mutation contract from the RFR is the authoritative anti-laziness layer; reality-check.sh is informational only. Bucket B candidate; do NOT block on its spurious diagnostics.
- **Substantive AC23/AC24 coverage measurement: `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov --package ucil-daemon --tests --summary-only --json | jq '.data[0].totals.lines.percent'` is the canonical form.** WO-0077 reported 89.65%; the literal `--no-default-features --features default` arg-pair errors because `ucil-daemon`'s Cargo.toml has no `default` feature defined (per WO-0074/0075/0076 lesson). Future plugin-manifest WOs that don't touch `crates/ucil-daemon/src/**` preserve the pre-WO coverage baseline by construction.

**Test-type effectiveness (which acceptance_tests caught bugs vs. were ceremonial)**:
- **Both mutation contracts (1× M1 + 1× M2) are non-ceremonial.** M1 catches manifest `transport.command` rot (e.g., upstream renames the PyPI package's `uvx` entry-point, or sysadmin removes `uvx` from PATH); M2 catches upstream tool-name renames (e.g., a hypothetical `mcp-pytest-runner@0.3.0` renaming `discover_tests` → `pytest_discover` would flip the M2 panic — and indeed v0.9.0 of Semgrep MCP exhibited exactly this regression at WO-0076). Both flipped on first attempt with verbatim left/right values matching the RFR's expected panic shape.
- **Tool-level smoke is non-ceremonial.** F08's `tools/call discover_tests` produced 159 structured findings (canonical `node_id` shape `tests/test_evaluator.py::test_evaluate_arithmetic`); follow-up `tools/call execute_tests` with a 3-id subset returned `exit_code=0, summary={total:3, passed:3, failed:0}`. **The selective-re-run smoke is the load-bearing F08 spec assertion** ("pytest hierarchical test discovery and selective re-run by node ID verified on the fixture python-project") — without it, the WO would only verify discovery, not execution. The two-step smoke (discover → subset → execute) caught the structured node-id-shape contract end-to-end.
- **The `UCIL_SKIP_TESTING_PLUGIN_E2E` env-gated runtime skip path is potentially-ceremonial** (same shape as G3-G7 env-vars). Default-to-RUN per scope_in #4 means the skip path never fires in the standard verifier flow. Surfaces a soft critic warning (silently exits OK) but not a regression detector — its purpose is to allow CI runners without uvx/python3 to skip cleanly. Could be removed if all CI runners gain the two runtimes.
- **No operator-state short-circuit needed for mcp-pytest-runner** (contrast with WO-0076's `resolve_working_semgrep()` and WO-0075's `GITHUB_PERSONAL_ACCESS_TOKEN`). Pytest is uvx-resolved; no operator-state surface required. **The CLI-dependency-class declaration is now a load-bearing distinction in scope_in.**

### Technical debt incurred

- **W1: 472-LOC `scripts/verify/P3-W11-F08.sh` single commit exceeds the ~200-LOC soft target.** Critic surfaced this as non-blocking soft warning; same shape as WO-0072/0074/0075/0076 verify scripts (all in the 400-500 LOC range). Coherent shell script where splitting would be artificial. **Mitigation**: future commit bodies of the same shape SHOULD cite DEC-0005 module-coherence carve-out explicitly. Carry-forward as a soft formatting-convention follow-up — do NOT split the script artificially.
- **Pre-existing follow-ups carry forward unchanged from WO-0076:**
  1. `scripts/verify/coverage-gate.sh` harness improvement to use `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER` (now 33 WOs deep; Bucket B / Bucket D triage candidate; intermittent).
  2. `scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug (carries from WO-0067/0068/0069/0070/0072/0073/0074/0075/0076).
  3. Effectiveness-gate.sh claude-p sub-session timeout flake (3 open escalations) — pre-existing standing scope_out, awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO.
  4. AC25 "no merge commits introduced on feat" wording — `git log feat ^main --merges = 0` form used successfully in WO-0070..WO-0077.
  5. **Daemon-side `manifest.transport.env` table + spawn-time env propagation (carried from WO-0076 W1+W2).** Resolves the unsafe-set_var debt for any future env-var-mutation-needing test. NOT touched by WO-0077 since F08 needed no parent-process env-var mutation. Bucket D candidate or part of a future G7/G3 production-wiring WO.
  6. **G3/G4/G5/G6/G7 production-wiring WOs** (`<Group>Source` traits + impls + `execute_g<N>` orchestrator + `merge_g<N>_<group>_context` aggregation, consuming all manifests over `tokio::process::Command` + MCP wire format). All 5 deferred per scope_out conventions.
  7. **DEC-0020 §Revisit-trigger re-check at next planner pass that suspects an upstream Ruff MCP server has emerged.** P3-W11-F03 deferred-pending-upstream; the curl/npm/gh triad documented for re-examination.
  8. **DEC-0021 §Revisit-trigger re-check at Phase 4 / Phase 7 start** (or sooner if planner suspects an upstream test-runner-mcp server has emerged). P3-W11-F07 deferred-pending-upstream; chain DEC-0019 → DEC-0020 → DEC-0021 documents the precedent.
- **Net-new follow-up work surfaced by WO-0077** (NOT debt; deferred-by-design):
  - **G8 production-wiring WO (`McpPytestRunnerG8Source` trait + impl + `execute_g8` orchestrator + `merge_g8_testing_context` aggregation, consuming the mcp-pytest-runner manifest over `tokio::process::Command` + MCP wire format).** Deferred per scope_out #2 / #3 / #11, parallel to G1/G3/G4/G5/G6/G7 production-wiring deferrals. F09 is the dep-blocked feature ID for the follow-up — currently dep-blocked on F08 + P3-W9-F03 alone (per DEC-0021 §Decision point 5: F07's deferral is admin-satisfied, so F09's dep graph reduces).
- WO-0077 introduces ZERO new high-priority debt items (W1 is a soft formatting warning consistent with prior precedent) and inherits all 8 follow-ups above without advancing them. **The Phase 3 paired-manifest WO sweep is now complete** modulo the three ADR-deferred features (P3-W9-F10 graphiti, P3-W11-F03 ruff, P3-W11-F07 test-runner-mcp).

## Lessons Learned (post-DEC-0022/0023/0024 supersedure 2026-05-08)

**Authored by**: monitor session with explicit user authorization, 2026-05-08T11:30Z.

**Context**: The three deferral ADRs above (DEC-0019 graphiti, DEC-0020 ruff, DEC-0021 test-runner-mcp) were authored by prior planner runs that did insufficient pre-flight upstream-availability searches. A 2026-05-08T11:30Z research sweep found that **all three upstreams exist** — they were just on non-PyPI channels (Docker Hub, PyPI under non-obvious name, npm) that the planner did not check.

**For planner — supersedure summary**:

- **DEC-0022 supersedes DEC-0019** — P3-W9-F10 graphiti is BACK IN PHASE 3 SCOPE. Install via official Zep Docker image `zepai/knowledge-graph-mcp` (or `uvx --from git+https://github.com/getzep/graphiti.git#subdirectory=mcp_server`). Pattern matches Serena P0 docker prior art. Re-emit a fresh WO; F10 has `attempts=2` so the next attempt must succeed cleanly (or hit 3-strikes soft escalation, NOT a halt).
- **DEC-0023 supersedes DEC-0020** — P3-W11-F03 ruff is BACK IN PHASE 3 SCOPE. Install via PyPI `mcp-server-analyzer` (Anselmoo, combines ruff + vulture). Tier-2 fallback: vendor a 50-line FastMCP wrapper. Pattern matches WO-0076 ESLint.
- **DEC-0024 supersedes DEC-0021** — P3-W11-F07 test-runner-mcp is BACK IN PHASE 3 SCOPE. Install via npm `test-runner-mcp` (privsim/mcp-test-runner) SHA-pinned. Pattern matches WO-0077 mcp-pytest-runner.

**For planner — search discipline (NOW MANDATORY)**: `.claude/agents/planner.md` has been updated with a 7-channel pre-flight upstream-availability search matrix. Before authoring ANY deferral ADR, the planner MUST check ALL 7 channels (PyPI, npm, GitHub repo search, GitHub subdirectories of canonical repo, Docker Hub, community forks, maintainer signals on GitHub Discussions/Issues) and document each result in the ADR's "Context" section. Failure to search all 7 channels = forbidden to author a deferral ADR.

**For docs-writer — earlier deferral notes are now historically-accurate-but-stale**: phase-log entries above (lines ~287-294, 358-360, items 7-8 in the most recent WO-0077 deferred-work block) reference DEC-0019/0020/0021 as authoritative deferrals. Those references are now superseded by DEC-0022/0023/0024. Future docs-writer passes may add a "(SUPERSEDED 2026-05-08 — see DEC-0022/0023/0024)" annotation but the historical record stands.

**For planner — next emission priorities**: After WO-0078 (g6-platform-aggregation) ships, the planner has 3 freshly-revived features eligible:
- P3-W9-F10 (graphiti, attempts=2) — emit with docker-image install path per DEC-0022
- P3-W11-F03 (ruff, attempts=0) — emit with `mcp-server-analyzer` install path per DEC-0023
- P3-W11-F07 (test-runner-mcp, attempts=0) — emit with `npx test-runner-mcp` SHA-pinned install path per DEC-0024
