## Lessons Learned (WO-0082 — test-runner-mcp-revival)

**Features**: P3-W11-F07 (test-runner-mcp G8 Testing+CI plugin manifest revival via DEC-0025-corrected upstream)
**Rejections**: 0 (verifier-green on first attempt; verdict PASS at HEAD `93132a6`; merged 1e0f00e)
**Critic blockers**: none — three non-blocking soft warnings (W1: AC13 grep/rustfmt newline collision carry-pattern from WO-0080; W2: scope_in #8 deletion-count vs file-rustdoc-amendment internal contradiction; W3: per-commit LOC over the ~50-line soft target on three commits — all DEC-0005 module-coherence-acceptable)
**ADRs raised**: DEC-0025 (planner-monitor-authored alongside the WO; AMENDS DEC-0024 with corrected source data — bare `test-runner-mcp` is NOT on npm, upstream advertises 1 tool with framework-enum NOT 6 separate tools); proposed-DEC-0025 (executor's authored proposal in WO-0081 escalation; accepted as-is into DEC-0025 final form)
**Coverage**: `ucil-daemon` 89.65% line via `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov --package ucil-daemon --tests --summary-only --json` (≥85% floor); WO is purely additive on tests + manifests + scripts (no `crates/ucil-daemon/src/**` source changes), pre-WO baseline preserved by construction.

### What worked

- **Executor's empirical-validation pattern (live `tools/list` capture BEFORE sealing the manifest) caught two material DEC-0024 errors at zero cost.** WO-0081's executor halt with empirical-validation escalation (`20260508T1435Z-wo-0081-dec-0024-tool-surface-mismatch.md`) discovered: (a) bare `test-runner-mcp` returns 404 from npm — only the third-party scoped mirror `@iflow-mcp/mcp-test-runner@0.2.1` is published; (b) upstream advertises ONE `run_tests` tool with a 7-value `framework` enum, NOT 6 separate framework-specific tools. The DEC-0024 author misread the framework JSON-Schema enum for a tool-count. **Web-search snippets alone are insufficient for npm/PyPI publication claims** — they conflate GitHub repo paths with npm package names AND they misread JSON-Schema enum values for tool counts. The `npx + initialize + tools/list` capture is the only authoritative source for upstream surface shape. This pattern is now load-bearing for ALL future manifest-revival WOs (recorded as DEC-0025 §Lessons-learned for planner verbatim).
- **DEC-0021 → DEC-0024 → DEC-0025 chain-of-corrections documents the deferral → revival → empirical-correction cycle.** Each ADR cites its predecessor; the chain is grep-able for future planner regressions on the same upstream. Anti-laziness contract held: the WO-0081 executor refused to silently substitute the iflow-mcp name for the planner's bare name and refused to relax AC#4 unilaterally — halted and escalated per scope_in #5/#2 boundary. The chain validates the executor's escalation surface as a load-bearing layer above the planner's research surface.
- **Solo-feature G8 plugin-manifest template (WO-0077 mcp-pytest-runner shape) ports cleanly to npm/npx.** WO-0082 mirrors WO-0077 verbatim, retargeted from PyPI/uvx to npm/npx: same `g8_plugin_manifests.rs` peer file (additive only — second test inside the existing `mod` block), same `UCIL_SKIP_TESTING_PLUGIN_E2E` env-gate (extends the existing G8 var verbatim — NO new env-var introduced), same M1+M2 mutation contract shape, same `[lifecycle] hot_cold = true / idle_timeout_minutes = 10`. **The recipe has zero per-feature execution risk at this maturity** — solo-feature plugin-manifest WO shape is now SEPTUPLE-verified across G3/G4/G5/G6/G7/G8 (WO-0072, WO-0074, WO-0075, WO-0076, WO-0077, WO-0079, WO-0080, WO-0082).
- **Three-name asymmetry pattern documented verbatim in manifest top-of-file rustdoc.** Captured all three surface names in the manifest's `pinned 2026-05-08:` block: GitHub upstream `privsim/mcp-test-runner` (canonical source of record), npm package `@iflow-mcp/mcp-test-runner` (only published surface; install string), runtime `serverInfo.name = "test-runner"` (matches `[plugin] name`). Future MCP-server-manifest WOs SHOULD record all three names whenever they differ — the executor's live capture is the only source for the runtime serverInfo.name. WO-0077 captured TWO names (PyPI `mcp-pytest-runner` vs runtime `pytest-mcp`); WO-0082 extends to THREE names.
- **Single-tool-dispatcher pattern for MCP servers using framework enums.** `@iflow-mcp/mcp-test-runner` advertises ONE `run_tests` tool with a `framework` enum {bats, pytest, flutter, jest, go, rust, generic} (7 values). The functional spec ("multi-language unified test execution covers Rust, Python, TypeScript via MCP") is satisfied at the framework-arg level NOT by separate per-framework tools. Master-plan §4.8 line 405 wording is functional NOT structural — the dispatcher pattern satisfies the spec. **Future planner passes for similar multi-language MCP servers SHOULD inspect `inputSchema.<arg>.enum` BEFORE prescribing tool counts in acceptance criteria** — JSON-Schema enums are common upstream-design choices for dispatcher-style tools.
- **DEC-0005 module-coherence carve-out continues to absorb commits over the ~50-line target.** Three commits in WO-0082 exceeded the soft target: `f5c9e77` (273 LOC manifest with provenance comment), `93132a6` (355 LOC verify-script with python smoke driver heredoc), `f3aa92f` (257 LOC RFR document). Splitting any of them would have produced non-meaningful intermediate states (manifest-without-provenance / non-runnable verify script / split RFR). DEC-0005 + WO-0079/0080 precedent cited in commit bodies. Critic accepts as soft warning, NOT blocker. **At this maturity (8 manifest WOs deep), the LOC-over-50 soft warning has effectively become a structural-coherence acknowledgment, not a quality regression.**
- **`scripts/verify/P3-W11-F07.sh` python heredoc smoke driver with 3-tier deadline polling (90s init / 30s tools-list / 60s tools-call).** Mirrors WO-0080's `scripts/verify/P3-W11-F03.sh` + WO-0077's `P3-W11-F08.sh` shape verbatim. Best-effort `try/except Exception: pass` cleanup blocks in the `finally:` clause (closing `proc.stdin`, killing `proc`, closing `smoke_log`) are NOT implementation stubs — same idiom as WO-0080 precedent and accepted by the critic. **The 3-tier deadline structure is now canonical for all uvx/npx-launched MCP-server smoke drivers** — cold-cache fetch budget, tools/list determinism budget, tools/call execution budget are distinct axes.
- **Pre-flight word-ban grep MUST cover ONLY production-side files; integration-test files are exempt under `#[cfg(test)]`/`tests/` carve-out.** WO-0082's grep covered `plugins/testing/test-runner/plugin.toml`, `scripts/devtools/install-test-runner-mcp.sh`, `scripts/verify/P3-W11-F07.sh` — ZERO matches. The integration-test file's rustdoc says "Mocking ... is forbidden" inside a forbidden-pattern declaration, exempt under WO-0048 line 363 + WO-0069 carve-out. Pattern is now SEPTUPLE-validated.

### What to carry forward

**For planner**:
- **The `npx + initialize + tools/list` empirical-validation pattern is NOW MANDATORY for all manifest-revival WOs.** Web-search/research-report claims about npm/PyPI publication MUST be verified with `npm view <pkg> version` / `pip index versions <pkg>` BEFORE the ADR lands. Web-search snippets routinely conflate GitHub repo paths with npm package names AND misread JSON-Schema enum values for tool counts. Any future revival ADR that does NOT cite `npm view` / `pip index versions` output in §Context is a planner anti-pattern. Recorded as DEC-0025 §Lessons-learned verbatim.
- **For MCP servers using framework/dialect enums, prescribe acceptance assertions on the enum NOT on tool count.** WO-0082's load-bearing assertions are: `health.tools.len() == 1` AND `health.tools[0].name == "run_tests"` (cargo test) AND `inputSchema.framework.enum` len ≥ 6 from canonical set (verify script). The framework-enum coverage assertion is in the verify script (independent JSON-RPC capture inspecting inputSchema), NOT in the cargo test — `health.tools` from `PluginManager::health_check_with_timeout` exposes the tool name list but not necessarily the full inputSchema. Future similar WOs SHOULD split this assertion: cargo test asserts on tool name only; verify script's tool-level smoke independently captures inputSchema and asserts on enum coverage.
- **Three-surface name asymmetry: capture GitHub upstream, package-registry name, AND runtime `serverInfo.name`.** When all three differ (as with WO-0082), document all three verbatim in the manifest top-of-file rustdoc + RFR. WO-0077 introduced the two-name pattern (package vs serverInfo); WO-0082 extends to three-name when upstream-of-record (GitHub repo) ≠ package-publisher (npm scope). Future planner passes SHOULD pre-research all three before WO emission.
- **`grep -qE '#\[tokio::test\][[:space:]]*async fn <test_name>'` literal AC will NEVER match rustfmt-formatted source.** This is now the WO-0080 + WO-0082 carry-pattern. rustfmt enforces newline + indent between `#[tokio::test]` and `async fn`, and default `grep` operates per-line. Future scope_in items prescribing such ACs MUST either (a) replace with multiline grep `grep -Pzo` form, (b) replace with cargo test selector resolution check, or (c) explicitly mark the AC as cargo-selector-resolution per the WO-0080 carry-pattern. **Recommend (b) — cargo test selector substring-match is the load-bearing intent of the AC anyway.**
- **scope_in items containing internally contradictory guidance MUST be flagged at WO-emission, not pushed to executor.** WO-0082 scope_in #8's sentence 2 ("file-wide deletion count = 0") vs sentence 3 ("file-level rustdoc may be amended") is structurally contradictory — the actual deletion count is 21 lines (all in the rustdoc preamble per the explicit permission). Future scope_in items should pick ONE invariant: either the test-body-zero-deletions check (the spirit) OR the file-wide diff check (the literal — but then explicitly forbid rustdoc amendment). WO-0082 critic flagged as planner-ambiguity; verifier correctly treated test-body-zero-deletions as load-bearing.
- **The DEC-0019/0020/0021 → DEC-0022/0023/0024 → DEC-0025 supersedure chain is fully discharged** with WO-0079 (graphiti) + WO-0080 (ruff) + WO-0082 (test-runner) all merged. **Phase 3 reaches 21/45 = 46.7%** after F07 lands. Subsequent planner passes (WO-0083+) MUST resume regular Phase 3 feature-list traversal targeting the remaining 24 unfinished features (P3-W9-F11 incremental test suite, P3-W10-F01 Aider repo-map, P3-W10-F04 G5 Context query, P3-W10-F09..F18 dependency-cruiser/Zoekt + bonus-context selector + multi-tier merging + warm processors + architecture/dependencies/blast_radius MCP tools, P3-W11-F01/F05/F06 G7 quality pipeline + severity-merge + quality_issues table, P3-W11-F09..F16 G8 test discovery + check_quality + review_changes + feedback loop + integration test suites + type_check + full-pipeline integration suite). The deferral chain is administratively closed.
- **Standing coverage workaround now 38 WOs deep (WO-0058..WO-0082).** Continue scope_out + AC23 standing-protocol substantive coverage check via `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov`. Bucket B / Bucket D candidate for triage; intermittent.
- **AC30/AC31 phase-1/phase-2 effectiveness-gate flake now 16 WOs deep (WO-0067..WO-0082).** Three pre-existing flake escalations carry; awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO. NOT a blocker — phase-3 work is unaffected.

**For executor**:
- **Apply the WO-0081 live-capture-before-implement pattern to all manifest-revival WOs.** Drive `npx -y <package>@<version>` (or `uvx <package>@<version>`) + `initialize` + `notifications/initialized` + `tools/list` via a one-shot Python driver script BEFORE sealing the manifest. Save the capture to `/tmp/wo-NNNN-capture.out` for the RFR. Compare against the planner's expected literals in scope_in. **If the capture diverges from scope_in, HALT and escalate** — do NOT silently substitute names or relax AC literals. WO-0081 escalation is the canonical precedent.
- **For npx-launched MCP servers, the cold-cache fetch budget is ~30s on first run (resolves package + @modelcontextprotocol/sdk + transitive deps + downloads tarballs).** WO-0082 used `FIRST_RUN_TIMEOUT_MS = 120_000` in the integration test (already set from WO-0077 mcp-pytest-runner; no change needed) and 90s/30s/60s deadlines in the verify script. Subsequent runs are <1s. Same shape as uvx-launched MCP servers (WO-0072, WO-0074, WO-0077, WO-0079).
- **For solo-feature plugin-manifest WOs with deferred peers (WO-0072 / WO-0077 shape) AND for revival WOs (WO-0079 / WO-0080 / WO-0082 shape), the M1 + M2 mutation contract is canonical.** M1 = `transport.command` poison (file: manifest .toml); M2 = expected-tool-name regression (file: integration test). Both reversible via `git checkout --`; both md5-snapshotted before mutation; both confirmed restored after via `md5sum -c`. WO-0082's M2 panic body carries the live `health.tools` list verbatim (`got: ["run_tests"]`) — the panic IS the diagnostic dump for upstream-drift detection.
- **DEC-0005 module-coherence applies to single-file commits over the ~50-line soft target IF splitting would produce non-meaningful intermediate states.** WO-0082 cited DEC-0005 + WO-0079 commit `c448dfc` precedent + WO-0080 in the additive-test commit body. Three other commits (manifest with provenance, verify script with python heredoc, RFR document) are coherent units where splitting would be artificial. **Cite DEC-0005 explicitly in the commit body when the LOC count exceeds the soft target** — critic accepts as soft warning when the carve-out is invoked.
- **`unsafe std::env::set_var` IS NOT NEEDED for self-resolving MCP servers.** test-runner-mcp is self-resolving at the MCP-server level (npx-managed package bundles Node + @modelcontextprotocol/sdk + transitive deps). The wrapper INTERNALLY shells out to `cargo`/`pytest`/`vitest`/`go`/`bats`/`flutter`/`jest` at tool-call time only — those are SECONDARY operator-state CLI dependencies, NOT initialize-time requirements. The W1+W2 unsafe-set_var debt from WO-0076 dissolves naturally. Same applies to WO-0077 mcp-pytest-runner. Future planner passes SHOULD distinguish operator-state-CLI-dependent (Semgrep, Sonarqube, Snyk, Trivy, RuboCop) vs self-resolving (mcp-pytest-runner, test-runner-mcp via `@iflow-mcp/mcp-test-runner`, ESLint MCP via npx, Context7, Repomix, Mem0, GitHub MCP, Git MCP, Filesystem MCP, codegraphcontext) at scope_in time.
- **Three commits over the 50-line soft target are acceptable when each is a coherent unit.** WO-0082's `f5c9e77` (manifest+provenance), `93132a6` (verify-script with python heredoc), `f3aa92f` (RFR document) are all single coherent artifacts. Splitting any of them produces stub-shaped intermediate states. Cite DEC-0005 in the commit body whenever invoking this carve-out.

**For verifier**:
- **For revival-WO solo-feature plugin-manifest WOs, run M1 + M2 mutations sequentially with md5 snapshot/verify between each.** WO-0082's `/tmp/wo-0082-test-runner-orig.md5` (`ea1e6ab983757e9e66458f350a4e8c34`) and `/tmp/wo-0082-g8tests-orig.md5` (`bcf6fe3a70eefc8a76b9e02246e61a26`) capture the pre-mutation state; `git checkout -- <file>` + `md5sum -c <snapshot>.md5` confirms restoration. The RFR's "Mutation contract" section is the canonical template — six rows per mutation (file, patch, selector, expected panic, restore, pre-md5). DO NOT use `git stash` for mutations — `scripts/reality-check.sh`'s pre-existing-stash bug interacts badly. Use `Edit` for in-place, `git checkout --` for restore.
- **AC `grep -qE '#\[tokio::test\][[:space:]]*async fn <test_name>' <file>` will NEVER match rustfmt-formatted source.** Treat as cargo-selector-resolution per the WO-0080 + WO-0082 carry-pattern: the load-bearing intent is `cargo test -p ucil-daemon --test g8_plugin_manifests g8_plugin_manifests::test_runner_manifest_health_check` resolving uniquely (substring-match without `--exact`). Verifier should run the cargo selector and confirm `1 passed` / `0 failed` rather than running the literal grep.
- **The `(SAn) <semantic name>` panic-body format remains canonical for mutation confirmation.** WO-0082's `(SA2)` panic ships the full live tool-list verbatim (`got: ["run_tests"]`) — verifier reads the SA-tag, confirms semantic match against the M2 expected literal, no grep/diff required. Continue forward as the canonical mutation-confirmation surface.
- **Verifier MUST NOT set `UCIL_SKIP_EXTERNAL_PLUGIN_TESTS` OR `UCIL_SKIP_TESTING_PLUGIN_E2E`.** Carries from WO-0076 scope_in #12 + WO-0079/0080 scope_in #25 + WO-0082 scope_in #25. Skip-path emits `[OK] P3-W11-F07` and exits 0 silently — does NOT exercise the load-bearing assertions.
- **Pre-flight `which npx node` BEFORE re-running the integration test from a clean session.** Missing `npx` produces a false-positive `PluginError::Spawn { kind: NotFound }` that masks real M1 detection. Per WO-0069 lessons §verifier #2 + WO-0075/0076/0077/0079/0080 carry. WO-0082 RFR §"Verifier notes" calls this out explicitly.
- **`scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug carries to WO-0082** (now 9 WOs deep). Workaround unchanged: M1/M2 in-place mutation contract from the RFR is the authoritative anti-laziness layer; reality-check.sh is informational only. Bucket B candidate for triage.

**Test-type effectiveness (which acceptance_tests caught bugs vs. were ceremonial)**:
- **Both mutation contracts (1× M1 + 1× M2) are non-ceremonial.** M1 catches manifest `transport.command` rot (e.g., upstream renames the npm package's binary entry-point, or sysadmin removes `npx` from PATH); M2 catches upstream tool-name renames (e.g., a hypothetical `@iflow-mcp/mcp-test-runner@0.3.0` renaming `run_tests` → `execute_framework_tests` would flip the M2 panic). Both flipped on first attempt with verbatim left/right values matching the RFR's expected panic shape.
- **Verify-script's INDEPENDENT JSON-RPC `tools/list` capture is non-ceremonial.** The independent capture (separate from the cargo test's `PluginManager::health_check_with_timeout` path) inspects `inputSchema.framework.enum` and asserts (a) tools[] len == 1, (b) tools[0].name == "run_tests", (c) framework enum len ≥ 6 from canonical set. The cargo test cannot make assertion (c) because `health.tools` exposes only the tool name list. **The independent capture catches a different layer of regression** — upstream could keep `run_tests` but reduce the framework enum to 3 values, breaking the F07 functional spec without breaking the cargo test. Verify script is the load-bearing layer for framework-enum coverage.
- **The `UCIL_SKIP_TESTING_PLUGIN_E2E` env-gated runtime skip path is potentially-ceremonial** (same shape as WO-0077). Default-to-RUN per scope_in #6 means the skip path never fires in the standard verifier flow. Surfaces a soft critic warning (silently exits OK) but not a regression detector — its purpose is to allow CI runners without npx/node to skip cleanly. Could be removed if all CI runners gain the two runtimes.

### Technical debt incurred

- **No new debt.** Three soft warnings from the critic are all carry-patterns from prior precedent (W1: WO-0080 grep/rustfmt; W2: scope_in internal contradiction = planner-ambiguity; W3: DEC-0005 module-coherence on three commits) — none represent net-new debt items.
- **Pre-existing follow-ups carry forward unchanged from WO-0080:**
  1. `scripts/verify/coverage-gate.sh` harness improvement to use `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER` (now 38 WOs deep; Bucket B / Bucket D triage candidate; intermittent).
  2. `scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug (carries from WO-0067/0068/0069/0070/0072/0073/0074/0075/0076/0077/0079/0080).
  3. Effectiveness-gate.sh claude-p sub-session timeout flake (3 open escalations) — pre-existing standing scope_out, awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO.
  4. AC #19 "no merge commits introduced on feat" wording — `git log feat ^main --merges = 0` form used successfully (carry from WO-0070..WO-0080).
  5. **Daemon-side `manifest.transport.env` table + spawn-time env propagation (carried from WO-0076 W1+W2).** NOT touched by WO-0082 (test-runner-mcp is self-resolving — no parent-process env-var mutation needed). Bucket D candidate or part of a future G7/G3 production-wiring WO.
  6. **G3/G4/G5/G6/G7/G8 production-wiring WOs** (`<Group>Source` traits + impls + `execute_g<N>` orchestrator + `merge_g<N>_<group>_context` aggregation, consuming all manifests over `tokio::process::Command` + MCP wire format). All 6 deferred per scope_out conventions.
- **Net-new follow-up work surfaced by WO-0082** (NOT debt; deferred-by-design):
  - **`TestRunnerG8Source` adapter** wiring the test-runner-mcp manifest against the F09 G8 test-discovery aggregator / F10 check_quality MCP tool. Deferred per scope_out #1, parallel to G1/G3/G4/G5/G6/G7/G8-mcp-pytest-runner production-wiring deferrals.
  - **DEC-0025 §Revisit-trigger re-check**: if `@iflow-mcp/mcp-test-runner` is unmaintained for 12 months OR removed from npm OR upstream `privsim/mcp-test-runner` is archived, supersede DEC-0025 with Option B (vendor in-house TS wrapper). If `privsim` publishes to npm under their own name, supersede with a fresh ADR pointing at that publication (more authoritative than the third-party mirror). Watch-list item for Phase 4/7 hardening.
- WO-0082 introduces ZERO new high-priority debt items and inherits all prior follow-ups without advancing them. **The Phase 3 deferral-revival sweep is now COMPLETE** — all three originally-deferred features (graphiti, ruff, test-runner-mcp) are landed via the DEC-0022/0023/0024+0025 supersedure chain. Phase 3 is at 21/45 = 46.7% post-F07.

These can ship as 1 batched WO (3 features) or 3 separate solo-feature WOs. F10's elevated attempts count (2) argues for solo-feature emission to reduce blast radius.

## Lessons Learned (WO-0083 — architecture-mcp-tools)

**Features**: P3-W10-F16 (`get_architecture`), P3-W10-F17 (`trace_dependencies`), P3-W10-F18 (`blast_radius`) — three coordinated G4-primary MCP tools wired through F09 `execute_g4` orchestrator (master-plan §3.2 rows 8/9/10 + §5.4)
**Rejections**: 0 (verifier-green on first attempt; verdict PASS at HEAD `26e1e15`; merged `354d96f`)
**Critic blockers**: none (CLEAN verdict). Two soft warnings: W1 — stale merge-base producing a phantom escalation-file deletion in `git diff main..feat/...` (NOT an executor mistake; the feat commits only touch `crates/ucil-daemon/src/server.rs` per `git show --numstat 63b9ebd`; verifier merge step carries main-side additions forward correctly under either fast-forward or 3-way semantics). W2 — `with_g4_sources` rustdoc has no `# Examples` section (matches local builder precedent — `with_g2_sources` / `with_find_similar_executor` also ship without; the three async handler methods carry the load-bearing `# Examples` ignore-doctests per scope_in #34).
**ADRs raised**: none (the WO cited DEC-0005 module-coherence + DEC-0007 frozen-test-at-module-root + DEC-0008 §4 dependency-inversion seam; no new ADRs authored)
**Coverage**: `ucil-daemon` ≥80% line via `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov` (the standing carve-out per AC19 + scope_in #31). New handlers + tests are purely additive on `crates/ucil-daemon/src/server.rs` — pre-WO line-coverage baseline is preserved by construction.

### What worked

- **Bundle-coordinated-features-around-shared-master-plan-§N.M-contract template now QUADRUPLE-validated** across G-family orchestration WOs: WO-0067 (classifier+reason parser around §6.2/§8.6), WO-0068 (executor+fusion around §6.1/§6.2), WO-0070 (G3 parallel merge around §6.1), WO-0083 (G4 architecture MCP tools around §3.2 rows 8/9/10 + §5.4). The recipe — single planner WO bundling 3 cohesive features whose tests + impls + dispatch wiring must coexist — is now load-bearing. Each iteration: ~700-900 LOC, ~3 commits (1 feat + 1 test + 1 chore), CLEAN critic verdict on first attempt, verifier-green on first attempt. **Zero per-feature execution risk at this maturity** for coordinated-features-around-shared-§N.M WOs.
- **DEC-0008 §4 dependency-inversion seam validates a 4th time.** The `G4Source` trait is UCIL-internal; `TestG4Source` impls inside `#[cfg(test)]` allow the MCP-tool surface to ship fully self-contained without production-wiring. Same shape as G1Source (WO-0047), G2 sources (WO-0044/WO-0050/WO-0051), G3Source (WO-0070), G4Source (WO-0083). The production-wiring deferral pattern (`CodeGraphContextG4Source` + `LSPCallHierarchyG4Source` impls deferred to a follow-up WO that bundles the daemon-startup-orchestration wiring) is now QUINTUPLE-validated. **For all future G-family MCP-tool surfaces, the trait-with-test-impl-now / production-impl-later split is canonical.**
- **Pre-baked M1/M2/M3 mutation contract with explicit md5 snapshot path lands cleanly on first verifier pass.** The RFR's `## Mutation contract` section carried six-column rows (file/lines, patch, targeted SAs, observed panic, restore command, pre-md5 path) per WO-0070 §planner #1 template. Verifier ran each mutation in sequence, observed the SA-tagged panic, restored via `git checkout --`, confirmed `md5sum -c /tmp/wo-0083-server-orig.md5` returned `OK`. Three substantively distinct failure modes (M1 = data-projection-zeroing, M2 = BFS-direction, M3 = sort-inversion). **The pre-md5 + in-place-Edit + git-checkout-restore pattern is now SEPTUPLE-validated** (WO-0067/0068/0069/0070/0072/0073/0083) and is the authoritative anti-laziness layer above `scripts/reality-check.sh`'s pre-existing-stash bug.
- **Spirit-over-literal SA targeting cleanly absorbs M3 deviation.** Scope_in #20 prescribed M3 should panic at SA5 (`impacted[0].path_weight >= impacted[1].path_weight`) — but the same sort-inversion mutation _also_ swaps `impacted[0].node` from `B` (correct) to `E` (lowest-weighted leaf), so SA4 (top-node-membership) fires _before_ SA5 in the test body's assertion order. Per scope_in #20's "or analogous descending-sort invariant violation" + scope_in #21's spirit-over-literal carve-out (citing WO-0070 §planner lessons), SA4 catching the mutation is acceptable — it is the same load-bearing semantic surface (descending-sort correctness over `path_weight`). Executor disclosed this in the RFR's `## Disclosed deviations` section. Verifier accepted. **The disclosed-deviation pattern (executor reinterprets a scope_in literal AND discloses with rationale citing established precedent) is now QUADRUPLE-validated** (WO-0070, WO-0072, WO-0077, WO-0083).
- **Manual `impl std::fmt::Debug for McpServer`** is the canonical absorption pattern for adding a non-`Debug` trait-object field to an existing `#[derive(Debug)]` struct. The new `g4_sources: Option<Arc<Vec<Arc<dyn G4Source>>>>` field would not auto-derive `Debug` because `G4Source` does not require `Debug` as a supertrait. Replacing `#[derive(Debug)]` with a manual `impl Debug` that surfaces only the source-list length is the cleaner alternative to bloating the trait surface with `Debug + ...` bounds. Same shape applies to any future trait-object-field addition where the trait omits `Debug`.
- **DEC-0005 module-coherence absorbs the 982-LOC feat commit cleanly.** The single feat commit (`63b9ebd`, +982 / -1) bundles three handler bodies + the field + the builder + the dispatch wiring as one cohesive unit. The sibling test commit (`a400673`, +574) lands the three frozen tests + the `TestG4Source` helper + the `make_g4_test_edge` builder + the `test_g4_source_list` factory. Splitting the feat commit per-handler would have produced stub-shaped intermediate states (a handler without a dispatch wire would not be reachable, and the M1/M2/M3 mutation-restoration contract requires all sites in one diff). Critic accepts as soft warning per DEC-0005 + WO-0067 (548 LOC) / WO-0068 (788 LOC) precedent. **At this maturity (DEC-0005 cited in 13+ WOs), the LOC-over-50 soft warning has effectively become a structural-coherence acknowledgment.**
- **Phase-1 invariant #9 (the 19 unwired tools fall through to `_meta.not_yet_implemented: true`) is preserved without test regression.** The dispatch wiring is gated by `g4_sources.is_some()` so when the daemon-startup-orchestration is run without G4 source registration, the three tools still fall through to the stub path. Catalog count stays at 22 (per `server::test_all_22_tools_registered`). The phase-1 invariant is the canonical guard against accidental regression-on-non-wired tools — same shape as G1 (WO-0047), G2 (WO-0050+0051), G3 (WO-0070).

### What to carry forward

**For planner**:
- **Production-wiring follow-up WO is now eligible** for `CodeGraphContextG4Source` + `LSPCallHierarchyG4Source` impls + daemon-startup-orchestration registration. Same shape as the deferred G3/G5/G6/G7/G8 production-wiring WOs (item 6 in WO-0082's debt list); the `<Group>Source` trait + impls + orchestrator + aggregation pattern is now standardized. Consider bundling G3+G4 production-wiring into a single WO since they share the codegraphcontext plugin runtime backbone (WO-0072 manifest + WO-0070 G3 orchestrator + WO-0073 G4 orchestrator + WO-0083 G4 MCP tool surface).
- **Bundle-coordinated-features template is QUADRUPLE-validated; treat as default for §3.2 row clusters.** Master-plan §3.2 rows that share an underlying orchestrator (G1-G8 family) SHOULD be bundled into a single WO whose tests + impls + dispatch wiring coexist in one diff per DEC-0005. Future planner passes traversing remaining §3.2 rows (e.g., G5 Context query rows, G7 quality-pipeline rows) SHOULD apply this template — NOT solo-feature emission unless the rows are operationally independent.
- **Pre-research the underlying orchestrator's BFS / projection invariants BEFORE writing M1/M2/M3 mutation prescriptions.** WO-0083 scope_in #20's "M3 = SA5 sort-invariant violation" was technically correct but did not anticipate that the same sort-inversion mutation flips `impacted[0].node` (a different SA) first. Future planner passes prescribing mutation contracts for sort-direction / BFS-direction failure modes SHOULD use "or analogous" or "spirit-over-literal" wording per WO-0070 §planner #5 + WO-0083 disclosed-deviation precedent — leaving room for the executor to tighten an SA bound that catches the mutation cleanly without over-prescribing the exact assertion-line that fires first. **The "or analogous" carve-out should be the default phrasing for all mutation prescriptions whose targeted invariant has multiple semantic projections.**
- **`# Examples` rustdoc on builder methods is OPTIONAL when the body is one-liner state-mutation.** WO-0083's W2 critic warning flagged `with_g4_sources` for missing `# Examples` — but the body is `self.g4_sources = Some(sources); self`, and existing peer builders (`with_g2_sources`, `with_find_similar_executor`) ship without `# Examples`. The `.claude/rules/rust-style.md` "non-trivial" qualifier covers this — trivial setters are exempt. Future scope_in items SHOULD explicitly cite "non-trivial" for rustdoc-Examples requirements OR list the public items where Examples are load-bearing (e.g., async handlers, public APIs that compose multiple types). **The rustdoc-Examples requirement is load-bearing for handler methods (where the example shows the param/response shape) but ceremonial for one-line setters.**
- **Phase 3 reaches 24/45 = 53.3% post-WO-0083** (up from 21/45 = 46.7% post-WO-0082 / WO-0079 / WO-0080). Subsequent planner passes (WO-0084+) target the remaining 21 unfinished features per scope_in #41 list: P3-W9-F11 (incremental test suite), P3-W10-F01 (Aider repo-map), P3-W10-F04/F09/F10/F11/F12/F13/F14/F15 (G5 Context query + conflict-resolution + bonus-context selector + multi-tier merging + warm processors + dependency-cruiser + Zoekt manifests), P3-W11-F01/F05/F06 (G7 quality pipeline entry + severity-merge + quality_issues table), P3-W11-F09/F10/F11/F12/F13/F14/F15/F16 (G8 test discovery + check_quality + review_changes + feedback loop + integration test suites + type_check + full-pipeline integration suite). Several of these admit the bundle-coordinated-features template — particularly P3-W10-F09/F10/F11/F12/F13 (response assembly + bonus context + multi-tier merging chain).

**For executor**:
- **Manual `impl Debug for X` when adding a non-`Debug` trait-object field is the canonical absorption pattern.** Replacing `#[derive(Debug)]` with a manual impl that surfaces only the operator-readable fields (e.g., source-list length, presence flags) is preferred over bloating the trait surface with `Debug + ...` bounds. WO-0083's `impl Debug for McpServer` (`server.rs:516-533`) is the reference shape: it preserves `#[derive(Clone)]` and surfaces the new field as `g4_sources: Some([N sources])` / `None`. **For any future PR adding a trait-object field whose trait does not require `Debug`, use this pattern verbatim.**
- **Disclosed-deviation pattern: when a mutation's targeted SA fires "earlier than prescribed" because the same code change has multiple semantic projections, the executor MAY tighten the targeted SA AND MUST disclose in the RFR's `## Disclosed deviations` section.** WO-0083's M3 prescription (SA5 sort-invariant) actually trips SA4 (top-node-membership) first — disclosed with rationale citing scope_in #20's "or analogous" + WO-0070 §planner spirit-over-literal carve-out. The verifier accepts the disclosure. **Do NOT silently tighten the SA assertion without disclosure** — that erodes the planner-executor contract.
- **Frozen-test selector substring-match REQUIRES module-root placement** (carries from WO-0068 §planner #1; reasserted by WO-0083). The three new frozen tests (`server::test_get_architecture_tool` / `..._trace_dependencies_tool` / `..._blast_radius_tool`) live at MODULE ROOT inside `crates/ucil-daemon/src/server.rs` (NOT inside an inner `mod tests { … }`); each `cargo test -p ucil-daemon server::test_<name>_tool` resolves uniquely under DEC-0007. **For any future bundle-coordinated-features WO, the frozen tests MUST sit at module root in the SAME source file as the production code** — splitting tests into a sibling `tests/` integration-test file breaks the substring-match selector convention.
- **The TestG4Source helper inside `#[cfg(test)] mod tests { ... }`** is the canonical pattern for in-process trait impls. Parameterised by `Vec<G4DependencyEdge>` + `String source_id` + default `G4SourceStatus::Available`; future test-impl helpers for G5/G6/G7/G8 sources SHOULD mirror this shape verbatim. **The pattern is now QUINTUPLE-validated** (TestG2Source via WO-0044, TestG3Source via WO-0070, TestG4Source via WO-0083 + via `executor.rs:3822` in WO-0073).

**For verifier**:
- **Stale merge-base producing phantom file-deletion in `git diff main..feat/...`: verify ALL deletions in the diff against `git show --numstat <each-feat-commit>`.** WO-0083's diff against main showed `ucil-build/escalations/20260508T1635Z-merge-wo-skip-verifier-on-main-branch.md` as `-235` lines — but the feat branch's commits (`63b9ebd`, `a400673`, `4c09079`) only edited `crates/ucil-daemon/src/server.rs` per per-commit numstat. The "deletion" is a stale merge-base artifact: `main` advanced to `a594e6f` after `feat` branched, adding the escalation file; `git diff main..feat` shows the absence-on-feat as a phantom deletion. Either fast-forward merge OR 3-way merge correctly carries the main-side addition forward. **For all future verifier passes, when the feat-branch diff shows file deletions, run `git show --numstat <each-feat-commit>` to confirm none are introduced by the feat commits themselves.** A phantom deletion is not a blocker for merge — it is a merge-base bookkeeping note.
- **M1+M2+M3 mutation contract sequential application, with md5 snapshot/verify between each, is canonical.** WO-0083's `/tmp/wo-0083-server-orig.md5` (`0b87e95ec7cd6d7b76f0e4c038a21104`) captures the pre-mutation state; `git checkout -- crates/ucil-daemon/src/server.rs` + `md5sum -c /tmp/wo-0083-server-orig.md5` confirms restoration after each. **Continue forward**: the canonical sequence is M1 → restore → confirm OK → M2 → restore → confirm OK → M3 → restore → confirm OK. Each mutation ≤ 3 lines of source change, ≤ 60 seconds wall-time.
- **The disclosed-deviation acceptance bar.** When the RFR's `## Disclosed deviations` section reinterprets a scope_in literal (e.g., "M3 trips SA4 before SA5"), verifier reads the disclosure, confirms the mutation is detected with substantively distinct failure mode, accepts. Do NOT reject for non-literal SA targeting when the disclosure cites established precedent (WO-0070 spirit-over-literal carve-out) AND the mutation is detected. **The acceptance bar: detection + substantive distinctness + disclosed precedent = accept.**
- **Standing carry-forwards** (now 39 WOs deep through WO-0083): coverage-gate.sh sccache RUSTC_WRAPPER workaround (`env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov`); effectiveness-gate.sh claude-p sub-session timeout flake (3 open escalations, awaiting harness-improvement WO); reality-check.sh pre-existing-stash bug; "no merge commits introduced on feat" via `git log feat ^main --merges = 0`. None are blockers for WO-0083 specifically.

**Test-type effectiveness (which acceptance_tests caught bugs vs. were ceremonial)**:
- **All three mutation contracts (M1+M2+M3) are non-ceremonial.** Each flipped its targeted test PASS → FAIL with a substantively distinct failure mode: M1 = SA3 module-list-emptiness (data-projection-zeroing); M2 = SA5 downstream-list-emptiness (BFS-direction failure); M3 = SA4 top-node-membership (analogous descending-sort invariant violation). Three different surfaces — verifier accepts.
- **SA4 (trace_dependencies upstream BFS) and SA7 (trace_dependencies direction-filter absent-`_meta.downstream`) are non-ceremonial guards** for direction-filtering correctness (load-bearing per scope_in #4). Neither was directly hit by M2 (which targets SA5 downstream-emptiness), but both guard against analogous regressions: an upstream-drop mutation would trip SA4; a direction-filter regression (showing downstream when direction=upstream) would trip SA7.
- **SA2 / SA6 / SA8 (response-shape canonicality + master-deadline canary + status-discriminant projection)** are ceremonial canaries — guard against future regressions (e.g., §15.2 trace-span misconfiguration tripping master_timed_out=true on the deterministic-positive-path; status-encoding regressions; tool-name field rename). NOT directly hit by M1/M2/M3, but each covers a real regression surface that the daemon-startup-orchestrator integration test will exercise once production-wiring lands.
- **SA6 (blast_radius array-shape preservation under array-input target)** is non-ceremonial — guards against an array-flattening regression (a regression that converts `[A, C]` → `"A,C"` or `"A"` would trip the assertion). Same applies to SA2 (single-string lifted to `["A"]` array) — both shape-canonicality assertions are load-bearing.
- **Zero ceremonial-only assertions overall.** Every SA either targets a mutation OR guards a load-bearing regression surface (BFS direction, sort invariant, response shape, deterministic-positive-path canary, array-shape preservation).

### Technical debt incurred

- **No new debt.** Two soft critic warnings are bookkeeping notes (W1 stale merge-base = verifier-step note, NOT executor mistake; W2 missing rustdoc Examples = matches local builder precedent, NOT a quality regression).
- **Pre-existing follow-ups carry forward unchanged from WO-0082:**
  1. `scripts/verify/coverage-gate.sh` harness improvement to use `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER` (now 39 WOs deep; Bucket B / Bucket D triage candidate; intermittent).
  2. `scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug (carries from WO-0067/0068/0069/0070/0072/0073/0074/0075/0076/0077/0079/0080/0082).
  3. Effectiveness-gate.sh claude-p sub-session timeout flake (3 open escalations) — pre-existing standing scope_out, awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO.

  6. **G3/G4/G5/G6/G7/G8 production-wiring WOs** (`<Group>Source` traits + impls + `execute_g<N>` orchestrator + `merge_g<N>_<group>_context` aggregation, consuming all manifests over `tokio::process::Command` + MCP wire format). **Six deferred per scope_out conventions; G4 is now ELIGIBLE for production-wiring follow-up** since the MCP-tool surface is landed.

  - **`CodeGraphContextG4Source` + `LSPCallHierarchyG4Source` adapters** wiring the F09 `execute_g4` orchestrator to the WO-0072 codegraphcontext plugin runtime AND to the P1-W5-F06 LSP call/type hierarchy bridge. Daemon-startup-orchestration registration: `McpServer::new().with_g4_sources(Arc::new(vec![codegraphcontext_g4, lsp_call_hierarchy_g4]))`. Deferred per scope_out #1 / #2 — same shape as G1 (WO-0047), G2 (WO-0044/0050/0051), G3 (WO-0070) production-wiring deferrals. **Consider bundling G3+G4 production-wiring into a single WO** since they share the codegraphcontext plugin runtime backbone.
- WO-0083 introduces ZERO new high-priority debt items and inherits all prior follow-ups without advancing them. **Phase 3 reaches 24/45 = 53.3% post-WO-0083** (up from 21/45 = 46.7% post-WO-0082). The bundle-coordinated-features template (QUADRUPLE-validated) is the recommended emission shape for the remaining 21 unfinished Phase 3 features wherever the rows share an underlying orchestrator.

## Lessons Learned (WO-0084 — tier-merger-and-conflict-resolution)

**Features**: P3-W10-F10 (`resolve_conflict` source-authority hierarchy `LSP/AST > SCIP > KG > text`, master-plan §18 line 1811), P3-W10-F12 (`merge_across_tiers` hot/warm/cold tier merging with `contributing_tiers` provenance + recency boost, master-plan §18 line 1813 + §12.3 + §11.3) — two coordinated pure-deterministic merge/provenance features in `crates/ucil-core/`.
**Rejections**: 0 (verifier-green on first attempt; verdict PASS at HEAD `9b2fdcb`; merged `fdab61f`).
**Critic blockers**: none (CLEAN verdict). Three soft warnings: W1 — `find_observed_at` private helper has subtle correctness fragility under duplicate-`(value, tier, confidence)`-triple inputs (frozen tests don't exercise; documented as future-correctness landmine for the consumer WO that wires real tier sources, NOT a blocker). W2 — M1/M2 panic-SA deviations (informational, accepted by precedent — spirit-over-literal). W3 — 995-LOC feat commit per DEC-0005 module-coherence (now cited in 14+ WOs).
**ADRs raised**: none (the WO cited DEC-0005 module-coherence + DEC-0007 frozen-test-at-module-root + DEC-0008 §4 dependency-inversion seam; no new ADRs authored).
**Coverage**: ucil-core **96.58%** line via `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov` (well above 85% AC floor); per-file fusion.rs **95.01%** + tier_merger.rs **87.30%** — both individually above the 85% floor.

### What worked

- **Bundle-coordinated-features template now QUINTUPLE-validated** across G-family / merge-family WOs: WO-0067 (classifier+reason parser around §6.2/§8.6), WO-0068 (executor+fusion around §6.1/§6.2), WO-0070 (G3 parallel merge around §6.1), WO-0083 (G4 architecture MCP tools around §3.2 rows 8/9/10 + §5.4), **WO-0084 (conflict-resolution + multi-tier merge around §18 lines 1811+1813 + §12.3 + §11.3)**. The recipe — single planner WO bundling 2-3 cohesive features whose tests + impls + (where applicable) dispatch wiring must coexist — is now load-bearing. Each iteration: ~700-1000 LOC, ~3 commits (1 feat + 1 test/verify + 1 chore), CLEAN critic verdict on first attempt, verifier-green on first attempt. **At this maturity, zero per-feature execution risk for coordinated-features-around-shared-§N.M WOs.**
- **DEC-0008 §4 dependency-inversion seam validates a 5th time.** `merge_across_tiers` takes pre-loaded `&[TieredResult<T>]` slices, NOT a `TierSource` trait. The dependency-inversion seam moves to the consumer WO that wires real tier readers (analogous to G1Source / G2 sources / G3Source / G4Source production-wiring deferrals). Same shape as WO-0047 (G1Source), WO-0044/0050/0051 (G2 sources), WO-0070 (G3Source), WO-0083 (G4Source). **The trait-with-test-impl-now / production-impl-later split is now QUINTUPLE-validated and canonical for all future merge/source surfaces.**
- **M1/M2 in-place mutation contract (Edit + `git checkout --` + md5 snapshot) now 14 WOs deep** and is the authoritative anti-laziness layer above `scripts/reality-check.sh`'s pre-existing-stash bug. WO-0084's `/tmp/wo-0084-fusion-orig.md5` (`c535481cfc0ce3b5b3389fe340a20d8e`) + `/tmp/wo-0084-tier-merger-orig.md5` (`2df2d48f6718403622b5b7d4690fde41`) snapshots both restored cleanly post-mutation. Two substantively distinct surfaces — M1 = boolean-precedence inversion (`<`→`>` on `SourceAuthority` discriminant comparison; `.min()`-equivalent → `.max()`-equivalent), M2 = data-projection erasure (`contributing_tiers` set to `vec![]` and tier-merge push-and-sort loop deleted). **Continue forward**: pre-md5 + in-place-Edit + git-checkout-restore is the canonical pattern for all future mutation contracts.
- **Spirit-over-literal SA targeting cleanly absorbs BOTH M1 and M2 deviations.** Scope_in #15 prescribed M1 panic at SA6 (`{value="a", LspAst, 0.5}` vs `{value="b", Text, 0.99}`); actually-observed M1 panic lands on SA3 first (per assertion order) with `{value="a", LspAst, 0.9}` vs `{value="b", Kg, 0.6}` — both are cross-tier authority precedence inversions, semantically equivalent. Scope_in #16 prescribed M2 panic at SA3 or SA5; M2 actually flips SA2 + SA3 + SA5 but Rust halts on first failure (SA2). Both deviations transparently disclosed in the RFR's `## Disclosed deviations` section. Verifier accepts. **The disclosed-deviation pattern is now QUINTUPLE-validated** (WO-0070, WO-0072, WO-0077, WO-0083, WO-0084) — executor reinterprets a scope_in literal AND discloses with rationale citing established precedent, verifier accepts when (a) the mutation IS detected, (b) the failure mode is substantively distinct, (c) the disclosure cites established precedent.
- **DEC-0005 module-coherence absorbs the 995-LOC feat commit cleanly.** The single feat commit `543e823` lands F10 fusion.rs delta (+429) + F12 tier_merger.rs (+565) + lib.rs `pub mod` declaration (+1) as ONE cohesive unit. Splitting per-feature would produce stub-shaped intermediate states (`pub mod tier_merger;` without the file would not compile; F10 fn without test would not exercise authority-precedence; M1/M2 mutation-restoration contract requires both surfaces to coexist in one diff). Cited precedent: WO-0067 ceqp.rs (548 LOC) + WO-0068 cross_group.rs (788 LOC) + WO-0083 server.rs (982 LOC). **At this maturity (DEC-0005 cited in 14+ WOs), the LOC-over-50 soft warning has effectively become a structural-coherence acknowledgment.**
- **Frozen tests at MODULE ROOT in the SAME source file as production code** continues to work cleanly under DEC-0007 substring-match. `test_conflict_resolution` lives in `fusion.rs:1278` (NOT inside `mod tests {}`); `test_multi_tier_query_merge` lives in `tier_merger.rs:356` (NOT inside `mod tests {}`). Each `cargo test -p ucil-core <module>::<test_name>` selector resolves uniquely from a `cargo clean` baseline. **Continue forward**: the bundle-coordinated-features template requires module-root frozen tests, NOT integration-test files in `tests/`.
- **Tracing carve-out for pure-deterministic CPU-bound merge functions** disclosed cleanly in the RFR. Both `resolve_conflict` and `merge_across_tiers` are pure-deterministic — no async, no IO, no `tokio::spawn`, no subprocess calls, no logging. The §15.2 carve-out applies (pure-deterministic-fallback module per WO-0067 §`lessons_applied` #5 + WO-0070 G3 parallel-merge precedent). Critic check 8 (Tracing) accepts the carve-out when explicitly disclosed.
- **Master-plan §-citations in module-level `//!` rustdoc** anchor the design contract to immutable spec text. `tier_merger.rs` cites §17 line 1636 (directory placement) + §12.3 lines 1348-1356 (HOT 0.2-0.4 / WARM 0.5-0.7 / COLD 0.8-1.0 confidence bands cited verbatim) + §11.3 (pull-based-relevance + recency boost driving merge-time recency bias) + §18 line 1813 (multi-tier query merging deliverable). `fusion.rs` cites §18 line 1811 (LSP/AST > SCIP > KG > text source authority hierarchy). **The §-citation density in module rustdoc is the canonical pattern for traceability** — every public type/fn carries WO ID + feature ID + master-plan §-numbers in its doc.

### What to carry forward

**For planner**:
- **Pre-loaded-slice merge functions are the dependency-inversion shape** (NOT trait-based readers). Future merge-family features (G5/G6/G7/G8 cross-tier merging or §12 hot/warm/cold pipeline) SHOULD take `&[TieredResult<T>]` (or analogous) slices and let the consumer WO wire the real tier readers. **Do NOT prescribe a `TierSource` / `<Group>Reader` trait for merge functions in the planner WO** — that bundles too much production-wiring into the merge-feature scope and would force stub-shaped intermediate states.
- **For mutation prescriptions targeting ordered-test-body assertion sequences, use "or analogous" or "spirit-over-literal" wording.** WO-0084's M1 prescription (SA6 panic) was technically correct but the same boolean-precedence inversion ALSO flips SA3 first. WO-0084's M2 prescription (SA3 or SA5) was technically correct but the same data-projection erasure ALSO flips SA2 first (and Rust halts on first failure). Scope_in #15-#16 already used the "or analogous" wording per WO-0070 §planner #5 + WO-0083 disclosed-deviation precedent — **continue this phrasing for ALL mutation prescriptions whose targeted invariant has multiple semantic projections OR whose targeted SA appears late in the test body.**
- **Bundle-coordinated-features template is QUINTUPLE-validated; treat as default for all §18-row clusters that share a thematic invariant.** Master-plan §18 rows that share an underlying contract (conflict-resolution + multi-tier-merge as §18 lines 1811+1813; sibling response-shape rows; G-family orchestrators) SHOULD be bundled into a single WO whose tests + impls + (where applicable) wiring coexist in one diff per DEC-0005. Future planner passes traversing remaining §18 rows SHOULD apply this template — NOT solo-feature emission unless the rows are operationally independent.
- **Phase 3 reaches 26/45 = 57.8% post-WO-0084** (up from 24/45 = 53.3% post-WO-0083). Subsequent planner passes (WO-0085+) target the remaining 19 unfinished features. Several of these admit the bundle-coordinated-features template — particularly P3-W10-F09/F11/F13/F14/F15 (response assembly + bonus context + warm processors + dependency-cruiser + Zoekt manifests) and the G7 quality-pipeline cluster (P3-W11-F01/F05/F06).
- **Recovery-via-rescan helpers (e.g., `find_observed_at`) carry a hidden uniqueness invariant.** When a private helper recovers metadata by linear-scanning input slices for a `(value, tier, confidence)` triple match (or similar key set), the correctness depends on that key being unique within the input. **For future merge/recovery-helper features, planner SHOULD prescribe**: (a) track the recovered field directly on the output struct OR a side-table keyed by index, NOT via re-scan; OR (b) explicitly document the uniqueness invariant the helper relies on AND add an SA assertion that exercises the invariant under near-duplicate inputs. Cite WO-0084 critic Warning #1 as precedent.

**For executor**:
- **Manual `Cmp`/`Ord`-via-discriminant comparison on enum** (e.g., `if c.source < top_source` over `SourceAuthority { LspAst, Scip, Kg, Text }`) is the canonical pattern for source-authority precedence — relies on the enum's variant-order in the `derive(PartialOrd, Ord)` impl. **The variant order in the enum declaration IS the authority hierarchy**; document this in the enum's rustdoc with the exact §-cite (e.g., `LSP/AST > SCIP > KG > text` per master-plan §18 line 1811). Future authority-precedence features should follow this shape.
- **`SystemTime` for recency boost is canonical** for hot/warm/cold tier merging — `entry.observed_at: SystemTime` is the comparison key (later wins). The default-branch fallback of `SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH` for the unreachable-in-practice case in `find_observed_at` is documented as such (NOT a stub-shaped placeholder per critic check). **Continue forward**: any merge function that needs a recency tiebreaker SHOULD use `SystemTime` (not `Instant`, not `chrono::DateTime<Utc>`) for std-only zero-dep simplicity; cite WO-0084 as the reference implementation.
- **Re-scan helpers MUST document their uniqueness invariant inline.** WO-0084's `find_observed_at` (in `tier_merger.rs:310-343`) has an inline comment asserting "the FIRST such observation in tier-order [...] is also the recency winner (the merge updates `source_tier` + `confidence` monotonically toward the recency winner)" — but this monotonicity claim only holds when input slices contain at most one observation per `(value, tier, confidence)` triple. **For any future re-scan helper, the inline doc-comment MUST**: (a) state the uniqueness invariant explicitly; (b) cite the consumer-WO contract that guarantees the invariant; (c) describe the failure mode if the invariant is violated. The critic Warning #1 lays this out — treat as a hard rule going forward.
- **Disclosed-deviation pattern: when a mutation's targeted SA fires "earlier than prescribed" because the ordered test body trips an earlier assertion first (Rust halts on first failure), the executor MAY tighten the targeted SA AND MUST disclose in the RFR's `## Disclosed deviations` section.** WO-0084's M1 (SA3 vs prescribed SA6) AND M2 (SA2 vs prescribed SA3/SA5) both fall into this category — disclosed with rationale citing scope_in #15-#16's "or analogous" + WO-0070/0083 spirit-over-literal carve-out. The verifier accepts the disclosure. **Do NOT silently tighten the SA assertion without disclosure** — that erodes the planner-executor contract.

**For verifier**:
- **M1/M2 mutation contract sequential application, with md5 snapshot/verify between each, is canonical.** WO-0084's `/tmp/wo-0084-fusion-orig.md5` + `/tmp/wo-0084-tier-merger-orig.md5` capture the pre-mutation state; `git checkout -- <file>` + `md5sum -c <md5-file>` confirms restoration after each. **Continue forward**: the canonical sequence is M1 → restore → confirm OK → M2 → restore → confirm OK (extending to M3 etc. when bundles add more mutations). Each mutation ≤ 3 lines of source change, ≤ 60 seconds wall-time.
- **`merge_across_tiers` has one non-obvious branch (`find_observed_at` re-scan helper) that is NOT exercised by `test_multi_tier_query_merge`.** Critic Warning #1 documents the duplicate-`(value, tier, confidence)`-triple edge case. For the consumer WO that wires real tier sources (when it lands), verifier SHOULD add an acceptance test that exercises near-duplicate inputs and verifies the recency winner is correctly identified. Until then, the WO-0084 acceptance is the correct bar (frozen tests use unique triples per value).
- **The disclosed-deviation acceptance bar (now 5 WOs deep)**: detection + substantive distinctness + disclosed precedent = accept. WO-0084 has TWO disclosed deviations (M1 SA3 vs SA6, M2 SA2 vs SA3/SA5); both detected with substantive distinctness; both cite established precedent (WO-0070 spirit-over-literal). Accept.
- **Standing carry-forwards (now 40 WOs deep through WO-0084)**: coverage-gate.sh sccache RUSTC_WRAPPER workaround (`env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov`); effectiveness-gate.sh claude-p sub-session timeout flake (3 open escalations, awaiting harness-improvement WO); reality-check.sh pre-existing-stash bug; "no merge commits introduced on feat" via `git log feat ^main --merges = 0`. None are blockers for WO-0084 specifically.

**Test-type effectiveness (which acceptance_tests caught bugs vs. were ceremonial)**:
- **M1 (P3-W10-F10) is non-ceremonial.** Boolean-precedence inversion on `SourceAuthority` discriminant comparison flips the test PASS → FAIL with `(SA3) cross-tier authority precedence` panic. Authority-hierarchy regression detected.
- **M2 (P3-W10-F12) is non-ceremonial.** Data-projection erasure of `contributing_tiers` flips the test PASS → FAIL with `(SA2) single-tier source_tier + contributing_tiers` panic. Tier-provenance metadata loss detected (also catches SA3 + SA5).
- **fusion.rs SA1 (empty input) + SA2 (single-candidate) are boundary checks**, not directly hit by M1/M2 but guard real regression surfaces (early-return correctness; happy-path projection).
- **fusion.rs SA4 (tied top tier disagreeing values → `Unresolvable` retains BOTH) + SA5 (tied top tier same value → highest confidence wins) are semantic invariants** for the slate-retention + within-tier confidence tie-break invariants. Neither directly hit by M1, but each guards a load-bearing regression surface (a tie-break-direction inversion would trip SA5; a slate-emptying mutation would trip SA4).
- **tier_merger.rs SA1 (empty inputs) is a boundary check.** SA4 (cross-tier different-values both surface, ordered Hot < Cold) is a sort-order invariant — guards against an ordering regression.
- **Zero ceremonial-only assertions overall.** Every SA either targets a mutation OR guards a load-bearing regression surface (boundary, slate-retention, tie-break, sort-order, tier-provenance, authority-precedence).

### Technical debt incurred

- **No new debt.** Three soft critic warnings are acknowledgments / disclosures, not regressions: W1 (`find_observed_at` re-scan helper subtle correctness fragility under duplicate-`(value, tier, confidence)`-triple inputs) is a documented future-correctness landmine for the consumer WO; W2 (M1/M2 panic-SA deviations) is a transparently disclosed spirit-over-literal absorption; W3 (995-LOC feat commit) is the DEC-0005 module-coherence carve-out.
- **Pre-existing follow-ups carry forward unchanged from WO-0083:**
  1. `scripts/verify/coverage-gate.sh` harness improvement to use `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER` (now 40 WOs deep; Bucket B / Bucket D triage candidate; intermittent).
  2. `scripts/reality-check.sh` pre-existing-stash bug (carries from WO-0067/0068/0069/0070/0072/0073/0074/0075/0076/0077/0079/0080/0082/0083).
  3. Effectiveness-gate.sh claude-p sub-session timeout flake (3 open escalations) — pre-existing standing scope_out, awaiting dedicated harness-improvement WO.
  4. AC #19 "no merge commits introduced on feat" wording — `git log feat ^main --merges = 0` form used successfully (carry from WO-0070..WO-0083).
  5. **Daemon-side `manifest.transport.env` table + spawn-time env propagation (carried from WO-0076 W1+W2).** NOT touched by WO-0084 (pure-deterministic merge module — no plugin-manifest changes). Bucket D candidate or part of a future G7/G3 production-wiring WO.
  6. **G3/G4/G5/G6/G7/G8 production-wiring WOs** (`<Group>Source` traits + impls + `execute_g<N>` orchestrator + `merge_g<N>_<group>_context` aggregation, consuming all manifests over `tokio::process::Command` + MCP wire format). Six deferred per scope_out conventions; G4 remains ELIGIBLE for production-wiring follow-up since the WO-0083 MCP-tool surface is landed.
- **Net-new follow-up work surfaced by WO-0084** (NOT debt; deferred-by-design):
  - **Consumer WO that wires real tier sources to `merge_across_tiers`.** Will need to (a) load `TieredResult<T>` slices from hot/warm/cold-tier readers (LMDB tag cache, SQLite/LanceDB warm tier, cold-tier persistence layer per master-plan §12.3), (b) ensure each tier emits at most one observation per `(value, tier, confidence)` triple OR refactor `find_observed_at` to track `observed_at` directly on the output struct (per critic Warning #1), (c) wire the merged output to the daemon-side query response assembly (P3-W10-F09 + F11). Deferred per scope_out conventions; eligible for bundling with G5 cross-tier merge or §12 hot/warm/cold pipeline production-wiring.
  - **Consumer WO that wires `resolve_conflict` to the daemon-side fusion pipeline.** Will need to (a) construct `ConflictCandidate<T>` slates from G1/G2/G3/G4 source results, (b) wire `resolve_conflict` into the response-assembly path so disagreement-detection and cross-tier authority precedence are applied before the response is shipped to MCP clients, (c) thread the `ConflictResolution<T>::Unresolvable { candidates, reason }` variant through the response shape so MCP clients see disagreement metadata. Deferred per scope_out conventions; eligible for bundling with response-assembly + bonus-context-selector (P3-W10-F09 + F11).
- WO-0084 introduces ZERO new high-priority debt items and inherits all prior follow-ups without advancing them. **Phase 3 reaches 26/45 = 57.8% post-WO-0084** (up from 24/45 = 53.3% post-WO-0083). The bundle-coordinated-features template (QUINTUPLE-validated) is the recommended emission shape for the remaining 19 unfinished Phase 3 features wherever the rows share an underlying orchestrator OR a thematic invariant.

## Lessons Learned (WO-0085 — g7-quality-pipeline-foundation)

**Features**: P3-W11-F01 (`G7Source` trait + `execute_g7` parallel orchestrator, master-plan §3.2 row 14 + §5.7 + §6.1 + §15.2 line 1519 `ucil.group.quality` span), P3-W11-F05 (`merge_g7_by_severity` severity-weighted merge fusion, master-plan §5.7 lines 539-559), P3-W11-F06 (`quality_issues` table tracking via SELECT-then-UPSERT in `persist_diagnostics` + `soft_delete_resolved_quality_issues` retention helper, master-plan §12.1 + §18 Phase 3 Week 11) — three coordinated G7-quality-pipeline-foundation features spanning `crates/ucil-daemon/` (new `g7.rs`) + `crates/ucil-lsp-diagnostics/` (existing `quality_pipeline.rs` deltas).
**Rejections**: 0 (verifier-green on first attempt; verdict PASS at HEAD `80cbed3`; merged `62796d9`).
**Critic blockers**: none (CLEAN verdict). Five soft warnings: W1 — commit subject 73 chars (3 over 70-char soft target on `feat(lsp-diagnostics): persist quality_issues with upsert and soft-delete`); W2 — `unwrap()` in production code at `g7.rs:650` (the M2-targeted `.iter().map(|i| i.severity).min().unwrap()` line) — author addressed via `# Panics` rustdoc proving unreachability (`BTreeMap::entry().or_default().push(issue)` ensures every group is non-empty) AND ties the literal `.unwrap()` shape to the M2 mutation contract, but did NOT cite explicitly in the RFR's `## Disclosed deviations` section; W3 — `expect()` in production code at `g7.rs:422` mirrors `g3.rs:376` precedent verbatim (`join_all_g7: every slot must be filled before returning` paralleling `join_all_g3: every slot must be filled`), informational; W4 — doc rot in pre-existing carried-forward comment at `quality_pipeline.rs:107` (`"future Phase-1 work-orders will extend this enum"` carried verbatim from WO-0016 but this is Phase 3 work), informational; W5 — test-side `ScriptedFakeSerenaClient` reuse from WO-0048 covered under WO-0048 line 363's `#[cfg(test)]` carve-out + WO-0069 §executor lessons (informational, not blocking — `SerenaClient` is the UCIL-owned dependency-inversion seam per DEC-0008 §4, NOT a mock of Serena's MCP wire format).
**ADRs raised**: none (the WO cited DEC-0005 module-coherence + DEC-0007 frozen-test-at-module-root + DEC-0008 §4 dependency-inversion seam; no new ADRs authored).
**Coverage**: ucil-daemon **89.63%** line via `env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov` (above the 80% AC floor; ~9.6% headroom over 80% AC23 standing protocol floor); ucil-lsp-diagnostics **94.72%** line (well above the 75% existing-crate floor).

### What worked

- **Bundle-coordinated-features template now SEXTUPLE-validated** across G-family / merge-family / persistence-extension WOs: WO-0067 (classifier+reason parser, §6.2/§8.6), WO-0068 (executor+fusion, §6.1/§6.2), WO-0070 (G3 parallel merge, §6.1), WO-0083 (G4 architecture MCP tools, §3.2 rows 8/9/10 + §5.4), WO-0084 (conflict-resolution + multi-tier merge, §18 lines 1811+1813 + §12.3 + §11.3), **WO-0085 (G7 quality pipeline foundation, §3.2 row 14 + §5.7 + §12.1 + §15.2)**. The recipe — single planner WO bundling 2-3 cohesive features whose tests + impls + (where applicable) trait-seam wiring must coexist — is now load-bearing across SIX consecutive iterations. Each iteration: ~700-1300 LOC, 3-4 commits, CLEAN critic verdict on first attempt, verifier-green on first attempt. **At this maturity, zero per-feature execution risk for coordinated-features-around-shared-§N.M WOs; treat as default for all remaining Phase 3 §18-row clusters.**
- **DEC-0008 §4 dependency-inversion seam validates a 6th time.** `G7Source` is a UCIL-owned trait — NOT a re-export of any external wire format. Production `LspDiagnosticsG7Source` / `EslintG7Source` / `RuffG7Source` / `SemgrepG7Source` impls deferred to follow-up production-wiring WOs that bundle daemon-startup orchestration. Same shape as G1Source (WO-0047), G2 sources (WO-0044/0050/0051), G3Source (WO-0070), G4Source (WO-0083), tier-merger pre-loaded slices (WO-0084). **The trait-with-test-impl-now / production-impl-later split is now SEXTUPLE-validated and canonical for ALL future merge/source surfaces.**
- **Three-mutation contract (M1+M2+M3) for 3-feature bundles is the new default.** WO-0085 ships M1 (per-source-timeout bypass in `run_g7_source` for F01) + M2 (severity-precedence inversion `.min()`→`.max()` in `merge_g7_by_severity` for F05) + M3 (`first_seen` overwrite in `persist_diagnostics` UPDATE branch for F06) — one mutation per feature, each targeting the load-bearing SA for that feature. Compare WO-0083 (3 features, M1+M2+M3) vs WO-0084 (2 features, M1+M2). **Continue forward**: for N-feature bundles where N=3, plan M1+M2+M3; for N=2, plan M1+M2. Each mutation ≤ 3 lines of source change, ≤ 60 seconds wall-time, in-place Edit + `git checkout --` + md5sum verify — the canonical anti-laziness layer above `scripts/reality-check.sh`'s pre-existing-stash bug (now 15 WOs deep).
- **`Severity` enum discriminant ordering with `Critical = 0`** is the canonical pattern for severity-weighted merge fusion. `#[derive(PartialOrd, Ord)]` gives `Critical < High < Medium < Low < Info`, so `.iter().map(|i| i.severity).min()` selects the MOST severe (smallest discriminant). Doc the rationale verbatim cite-§5.7-line-555-556 in the enum's rustdoc. The pattern paired with the SA6 sentinel-row vocabulary canary (`vec![Critical, Critical, High, Medium, Low, Info]` → output sorted severity-ascending with lowercase `severity.as_str()` projection) gives a planner-anticipated double-coverage: M2 (`.min()`→`.max()` inversion) trips SA3 (Medium+Critical → keeps Critical), AND SA6 (sentinel ordering) would also trip on any sort-direction inversion. **Continue forward**: for any future `Severity`-like enum where `Ord` is load-bearing, follow this `MOST-severe = SMALLEST discriminant` convention + add a sentinel-row vocabulary SA.
- **F06 SELECT-then-UPSERT trend-tracking pattern** is the canonical shape for `quality_issues`-style tables that need to preserve `first_seen` across re-observations while updating `last_seen`. The dedup key `(file_path, COALESCE(line_start, -1), category, severity, message)` per master-plan §12.1 row uniqueness — `rule_id` and `source_tool` are NOT in the dedup key (different rule_ids on the same line+severity+message would be a contradiction; pinning them in the dedup key would split otherwise-identical issues). The resolve-transition step (`UPDATE ... SET resolved = 1 WHERE file_path = ?1 AND resolved = 0 AND id NOT IN (...)`) handles the empty-diagnostics / partial-recovery case. **Continue forward**: any future `*_issues` / `*_observations` / `*_findings` table with `first_seen` + `last_seen` + `resolved` columns SHOULD follow this exact pattern.
- **`unwrap()` in production code can be load-bearing for mutation contracts** when a `# Panics` rustdoc proves unreachability AND the literal `.unwrap()` shape is itself the M-targeted line. WO-0085's `g7.rs:650` `.iter().map(|i| i.severity).min().unwrap()` is the M2 target; replacing it with a `.unwrap_or(Severity::Info)` fallback would silently swallow the M2 mutation. Critic W2 noted the deviation but the author's `# Panics` rustdoc + M2-anchoring justified it. **Lesson for future executors**: when shipping unavoidable `.unwrap()` patterns to enable mutation-contract testing, proactively cite in the RFR's `## Disclosed deviations` section. Document the unreachability proof in `# Panics` rustdoc AND tie the line shape to the targeted mutation contract — this is the canonical pattern.
- **Frozen tests at MODULE ROOT** continue to work cleanly under DEC-0007 substring-match. `g7::test_g7_parallel_pipeline` lives at `g7.rs:737`, `g7::test_g7_severity_merge` at `g7.rs:941`, `quality_pipeline::test_quality_issues_tracking` at `quality_pipeline.rs:1090` (all NOT inside `mod tests {}`). Each `cargo test -p <crate> <module>::<test_name>` selector resolves uniquely from a `cargo clean` baseline. **Continue forward**: the bundle-coordinated-features template requires module-root frozen tests, NOT integration-test files in `tests/` (now 6 WOs deep: WO-0067/0068/0070/0083/0084/0085).
- **Tracing carve-out for pure-deterministic CPU-bound merge functions** disclosed cleanly in the RFR. `merge_g7_by_severity` is pure-deterministic — no async, no IO, no `tokio::spawn`, no subprocess calls, no logging — and is exempt from §15.2 per WO-0067 §`lessons_applied` #5 + WO-0070 G3 merger precedent. `execute_g7` (which IS async/IO/orchestration) DOES carry `#[tracing::instrument(name = "ucil.group.quality")]` per §15.2 line 1519. `soft_delete_resolved_quality_issues` (which IS async/IO with rusqlite) carries `#[tracing::instrument(name = "ucil.lsp.soft_delete_resolved_quality_issues")]`.

### What to carry forward

**For planner**:
- **For mutation prescriptions involving proc-macro-literal contexts (e.g., `#[tracing::instrument(fields(... = expr as u64))]`), the `as u64` cast trips `clippy::cast_possible_truncation` under `#![deny(warnings)]` and there is no clean `u64::try_from` form inside the proc-macro literal.** WO-0085 scope_in #9 prescribed `fields(source_count = sources.len(), master_deadline_ms = master_deadline.as_millis() as u64)` but executor dropped to `fields(source_count = sources.len())` matching G3 (`g3.rs:445`) and G4 (`g4.rs:536`) precedent. **Future planner passes prescribing tracing fields with numeric casts SHOULD either** (a) match the existing G3/G4 precedent (single `source_count` field, master_deadline auto-captured by tracing through fn arg), OR (b) explicitly carve out the `clippy::cast_possible_truncation` allow. **Default to (a) until a feature actually requires the cast.**
- **3-mutation contract (M1+M2+M3) for 3-feature bundles is now load-bearing.** Future planner passes emitting 3-feature bundles SHOULD prescribe one mutation per feature targeting the feature's load-bearing SA. Each mutation: in-place Edit + targeted-SA + `git checkout --` + md5sum verify. WO-0085 reaches 27/45 = 60.0% post-WO-0085 (up from 26/45 = 57.8% post-WO-0084). Subsequent planner passes traversing remaining §18 rows SHOULD continue this pattern.
- **Phase 3 reaches 27/45 = 60.0% post-WO-0085** (up from 26/45 = 57.8% post-WO-0084). 18 unfinished Phase 3 features remain. Eligible bundle-coordinated emissions: **G7 production-wiring** (LspDiagnosticsG7Source + EslintG7Source + RuffG7Source + SemgrepG7Source impls + daemon-startup orchestration registration, bundling P3-W11-F02/F03/F04 plugin-runtime-wiring); **response-assembly bundle** (P3-W10-F09 + F11 + F13 — response shape + bonus-context-selector + warm processors); **dependency-cruiser + Zoekt manifests** (P3-W10-F14 + F15); **incremental computation integration test suite** (P3-W9-F11). Apply the bundle-coordinated-features template wherever rows share an underlying orchestrator OR a thematic invariant.
- **Doc rot in carried-forward comments should be scrubbed when extending modules across phase boundaries.** WO-0085 W4 (`quality_pipeline.rs:107` says `"future Phase-1 work-orders"` but this is Phase 3) is informational, but the planner SHOULD instruct the executor to amend such carried-forward comments when an extension WO touches the same module across a phase boundary. Consider adding to scope_in: "If pre-existing carried-forward comments reference earlier phase numbers, amend to current phase + cite the WO that does so."

**For executor**:
- **`#[tracing::instrument]` `fields(...)` numeric casts trip `clippy::cast_possible_truncation`** under `#![deny(warnings)]`. Drop to the auto-captured-via-fn-arg form (matching G3/G4 precedent) OR add a pinpoint `#[allow(clippy::cast_possible_truncation)]` with rationale. Default: drop the field, let tracing auto-capture the fn arg.
- **`SystemTime` for retention-cutoff arithmetic** is canonical. `now - retention_days * 24 * 3600` rendered as SQLite-comparable `TEXT` via a hand-rolled UTC formatter (or single-line `chrono` shim if `chrono` is already a transitive dep — check via `cargo metadata --format-version 1 -p <crate> | jq '.packages[0].dependencies[] | select(.name=="chrono")'` BEFORE deciding). WO-0085 used `std::time::SystemTime` only; no new workspace dep introduced.
- **Test-side `Test*` prefix is canonical** for in-process trait impls under DEC-0008 §4 (e.g., `TestG7Source` mirroring `TestG3Source` (WO-0070) and `TestG4Source` (WO-0083)). The pre-flight word-ban scrub `grep -niE 'mock|fake|stub' <production-side-of-file>` returns empty. **The `Test` prefix differentiates UCIL-internal trait impls from external-wire-format mocks** — the latter are categorically forbidden per CLAUDE.md, the former are the dependency-inversion seam per DEC-0008 §4.
- **`#[allow(dead_code)]` on helpers like `join_all_g7` mirroring WO-0070 §executor lesson** is required so M1 mutation (replacing the parallel join with sequential `.await`) does NOT trigger `#![deny(warnings)]`. The helper IS referenced by `execute_g7` so M1's specific patch (replacing `tokio::time::timeout` with bare `source.execute().await`) does NOT orphan it; the `#[allow]` is future-proofing for any M1-style mutation that swaps the join call site for a sequential `for ... .await` loop. Inline rustdoc MUST cite the M1 contract.
- **When shipping unavoidable `.unwrap()` patterns** to enable mutation-contract testing, proactively cite in the RFR's `## Disclosed deviations` section. Document the unreachability proof in `# Panics` rustdoc AND tie the line shape to the targeted mutation contract. WO-0085 had this disclosure in the rustdoc (`g7.rs:618-625`) but NOT in the RFR — critic W2 surfaced the gap. **Always RFR-disclose `.unwrap()` / `.expect()` shipped in production code, even when the rustdoc justifies it.**

**For verifier**:
- **3-mutation sequential application (M1 → restore → confirm OK → M2 → restore → confirm OK → M3 → restore → confirm OK), with md5 snapshot/verify between each, is canonical for 3-feature bundles.** WO-0085 used two pre-md5 paths (`/tmp/wo-0085-g7-orig.md5` for M1+M2, `/tmp/wo-0085-quality-pipeline-orig.md5` for M3) since M1+M2 target `g7.rs` and M3 targets `quality_pipeline.rs`. Each mutation ≤ 3 lines of source change, ≤ 60 seconds wall-time. The disclosed-deviation acceptance bar (now 6 WOs deep through WO-0085): detection + substantive distinctness + disclosed precedent = accept.
- **F06 trend-tracking acceptance test** has 6 SA-numbered scenarios covering first-INSERT / re-observation-UPDATE / last_seen-advance / resolve-transition / soft-delete-past-retention / soft-delete-within-retention. SA2 (re-observation preserves `first_seen`) is the M3-targeted load-bearing assertion. SA5 (soft-delete past retention deletes resolved row) is the soft-delete-cutoff regression guard. SA6 (soft-delete within retention preserves the row) is the OFF-by-N retention-cutoff regression guard. **For future trend-tracking features with `first_seen`/`last_seen`/`resolved` columns, verifier SHOULD expect this 6-scenario shape.**
- **Standing carry-forwards (now 41+ WOs deep through WO-0085)**: coverage-gate.sh sccache `RUSTC_WRAPPER` workaround (`env -u RUSTC_WRAPPER cargo llvm-cov`); effectiveness-gate.sh claude-p sub-session timeout flake (3 open escalations); reality-check.sh pre-existing-stash bug (now 15 WOs deep); "no merge commits introduced on feat" via `git log feat ^main --merges = 0`. None are blockers for WO-0085 specifically.

### Test-type effectiveness (which acceptance_tests caught bugs vs. were ceremonial)

- **M1 (P3-W11-F01 per-source-timeout bypass) is non-ceremonial.** Replacing `tokio::time::timeout(per_source_deadline, source.execute(query))` with bare `source.execute(query).await` flips `g7::test_g7_parallel_pipeline` PASS → FAIL with `(SA4a) outcome.results[1].status; left: Available, right: TimedOut` panic. Per-source deadline regression detected.
- **M2 (P3-W11-F05 severity-precedence inversion) is non-ceremonial.** Changing `.iter().map(|i| i.severity).min().unwrap()` to `.iter().map(|i| i.severity).max().unwrap()` flips `g7::test_g7_severity_merge` PASS → FAIL with `(SA3b) highest severity wins; left: Medium, right: Critical` panic. Severity-precedence regression detected.
- **M3 (P3-W11-F06 `first_seen` overwrite on UPSERT update) is non-ceremonial.** Changing the UPDATE statement from `SET last_seen = datetime('now'), resolved = 0` to `SET first_seen = datetime('now'), last_seen = datetime('now'), resolved = 0` flips `quality_pipeline::test_quality_issues_tracking` PASS → FAIL with `(SA2c) first_seen UNCHANGED across re-observation` panic. Trend-tracking invariant regression detected.
- **F01 SA1/SA2/SA3/SA5 are ceremonial sanity checks** (3 results returned, master-deadline does NOT trip, Available source preserves issues, Errored source preserves error). SA6 (parallelism wall-clock < 5000 ms) is a backstop that would catch sequentialised execution if M1 + sequentialisation regressed together.
- **F05 SA1/SA2/SA4/SA5 are ceremonial sanity checks** (empty input → `vec![]`; single-issue input preserves all fields; cross-group highest-wins; tied-severity merge picks alphabetical-first source_tool). SA6 (sentinel-row vocabulary canary) is the lowercase-vocabulary regression guard — would also catch M2 (severity sort order).
- **F06 SA1/SA3/SA4/SA5/SA6 are ceremonial sanity checks** (first observation INSERTs row with non-null `first_seen`/`last_seen`/`resolved == 0`; re-observation `last_seen >= first_seen`; empty-diagnostics resolve outstanding rows; soft-delete past retention / preserves within retention). All would catch their named regression surfaces.
- **Zero ceremonial-only assertions overall.** Every SA either targets a mutation OR guards a load-bearing regression surface (deadline-trip, severity-precedence, trend-tracking, resolve-transition, retention-cutoff, parallelism-wall-clock, vocabulary-canary).

Same shape as G3 (WO-0070) and G4 (WO-0083) production-wiring deferrals; eligible for bundling with G3/G4 production-wiring follow-ups.
